To find connected components: compute MaxR = Rows - 1 and MaxC = Cols - 1 before the findall; use findall with between/3 over [0, MaxR] and [0, MaxC] to collect all cells of the target color into AllCells; pass AllCells to extract_components.

To extract components iteratively: if the remaining list is empty, return the empty component list; if the head cell is already in Done, skip it and recurse; otherwise run BFS from the head cell over the remaining cells to find the component; record the component; mark its cells as done; remove its cells from the remaining list; recurse on the pruned remaining list.

To run BFS for one component: maintain a queue and a visited set; if the queue is empty, return the visited set as the component; if the front cell is already visited, dequeue and recurse; otherwise find all 4-connected neighbors of the front cell that are in Available and not yet visited; append those neighbors to the queue; add the front cell to visited; recurse.

To compute a bounding box: use findall to collect all R values from r(R,_) cells; use findall to collect all C values from r(_,C) cells; compute min_list and max_list over each.

To rotate 90 degrees clockwise: new grid has Cols rows and Rows columns; for new row NR and new column NC, the source row is NewCols - 1 - NC and the source column is NR; use maplist with YALL lambdas to build each new row.

To rotate 180 degrees: compose two 90-degree clockwise rotations.

To rotate 270 degrees clockwise: compose three 90-degree clockwise rotations.

To reflect across the horizontal axis: reverse the list of rows.

To reflect across the vertical axis: reverse each row independently.

To reflect across the main diagonal (transpose): use numlist to generate column indices 0 through Cols-1; for each column index C, extract that column from the original grid using gd_col; the resulting list of columns is the transposed grid.

To reflect across the anti-diagonal: rotate 90 degrees clockwise, then reflect across the vertical axis.

To translate: for each cell (R, C) in the output grid, the source position is (R - DR, C - DC); if that source position is within the grid bounds, read its color; otherwise use the background color.

To crop: use numlist to build row and column index lists for the inclusive rectangle; for each (R, C) pair in those lists, read the color from the source grid.

To overlay: for each cell (R, C) of the base grid, compute the patch position (R - DR, C - DC); if that position is within the patch bounds and the patch color is non-zero, use the patch color; otherwise use the base color.

To diff two grids: verify that both grids have the same Rows and Cols; compute MaxR and MaxC before findall; iterate over all (R, C) pairs using between/3; for each pair where the two colors differ, record r(R, C, Old, New).

To test equality: use structural unification; two grids are equal if and only if they are the same Prolog term.

To detect symmetry axes: for each axis in [h, v, d1, d2], apply the corresponding reflection; test equality with the original; collect the axes that pass.

To flood fill: read the color at the seed cell; find all connected components of that color; select the component containing the seed cell; use foldl over the component cells to set each cell to the new color, threading the grid state through the fold.

To make a uniform grid: build one row of Cols copies of Color using length and maplist with =(Color); build Rows copies of that row using length and maplist with =(Row).

To set one cell: use nth0/4 in select mode to decompose the grid at row R, getting OldRow and RestRows; decompose OldRow at column C to get the remaining cells; reconstruct NewRow by inserting Color at position C; reconstruct Grid2 by inserting NewRow at position R.

END OF DOCUMENT - PROLOGAI PSEUDOCODE


THE LOGIC OF THE ARC-AGI STRUCTURAL ANALOGY AND TRANSFORMATION INFERENCE PACK (PR 57)

To normalize a shape: collect all row indices via findall; collect all column indices via findall; compute min_list for rows and for columns; subtract MinR from every row index and MinC from every column index in the cell list; sort the shifted list.

To test shape equality: normalize both cell sets; test structural equality of the two normalized lists.

To compute a bounding box: collect row indices and column indices via findall; compute min_list and max_list for each.

To apply a D4 isometry to a shape: for identity, normalize and return; for rot90, compute the bounding box max row, then map (R,C) to (C, MaxR-R), then normalize; for rot180 and rot270, compose the rot90 step two or three times; for ref_h, map (R,C) to (MaxR-R, C) using the bounding box max row, then normalize; for ref_v, map (R,C) to (R, MaxC-C) using the bounding box max column, then normalize; for ref_d1 (transpose), map (R,C) to (C,R), then normalize; for ref_d2, apply rot90 then ref_d1.

To find isometry candidates between two shapes: normalize Shape2 once; for each of the 8 D4 isometries, apply the isometry to Shape1 and compare the result to the normalized Shape2; collect those that match.

To infer a color map from two parallel color lists: pair each input color with the corresponding output color using maplist; retain only non-identity pairs (where input color does not equal output color) using findall with the condition F \= T; remove duplicates with list_to_set.

To infer a grid color map: flatten both grids to lists; infer the color map from the parallel flat lists.

To match objects by shape: for each input object and each output object, test shape equality; collect all matching in_obj-out_obj pairs.

To compute an object offset: find the bounding box top-left of each cell set; subtract the first top-left from the second to get the row delta and column delta.

To find grid isometries: for each of the 8 D4 isometries, apply the isometry to Grid1; test structural equality with Grid2; collect matching isometry names.

To find examples-consistent isometry and color map: split the pairs into two lists (inputs and outputs); try each D4 isometry in order; apply it to the first input grid; infer the color map from the transformed first input to the first expected output; verify every training pair with ay_verify_pair: apply the isometry, apply the color map, test equality with the expected output.

To verify one training pair (named predicate ay_verify_pair): apply the isometry to the input grid to get a fresh TGrid; apply the color map to TGrid to get Predicted; test equality of Predicted with the expected output. Using a named predicate ensures TGrid and Predicted are fresh local variables on every call.

To apply a named D4 isometry to a grid: dispatch to the corresponding gd_rotate* or gd_reflect* predicate from pack grid; for identity, return the grid unchanged.

To apply a color map to a grid: delegate to gd_color_map from pack grid.

To solve from examples: call ay_examples_isometry to find Iso and ColorMap; apply the isometry to the test grid; apply the color map to the result; the final grid is the predicted output.

END OF DOCUMENT - PROLOGAI PSEUDOCODE


PART 48 - SCENE PACK ALGORITHMS

Section 48.1 - Background Color Identification

The background color is defined as the most frequently occurring color in the grid. The algorithm:

  sc_bg_color(Grid, BgColor):
    Colors = gd_colors(Grid)                 % sorted unique color set
    Pairs = [(count(Grid, C), C) : C in Colors]
    BgColor = color of pair with maximum count

The implementation uses findall to collect Count-Color pairs and max_member/2 to select the maximum. SWI-Prolog's standard order on numbers means max_member correctly selects the pair with the greatest numeric count.

Edge case: if two colors appear equally often, max_member returns the one that compares greater in standard order. For ARC-AGI grids, the background is nearly always the most common color by a significant margin, so this edge case rarely affects correctness.

Section 48.2 - Object Extraction

sc_objects/2 builds the complete object inventory:

  sc_objects(Grid, Objects):
    BgColor = sc_bg_color(Grid)
    FgColors = gd_colors(Grid) minus BgColor
    Objects = foldl(collect_color_objects(Grid), FgColors, [])

  collect_color_objects(Grid, Color, Acc, NewAcc):
    CellSets = gd_objects(Grid, Color)       % list of 4-connected components
    ColorObjs = [obj(Color, Cells) : Cells in CellSets]
    NewAcc = Acc ++ ColorObjs

The named predicate make_obj/3 is used with maplist to wrap each CellSet as obj(Color, CellSet). Using a named predicate rather than a YALL lambda is critical here. In the foldl call, collect_color_objects/4 is called once per foreground color. Inside collect_color_objects, maplist(make_obj(Color), CellSets, ColorObjs) is called. If make_obj were a YALL lambda, the Color variable in the lambda body would be unified with the actual color on the first call (say, color 1) and would remain bound to 1 for all subsequent calls, causing the maplist to fail or produce wrong results for other colors (say, color 2). The named predicate make_obj/3 receives Color as a fresh argument on each call, correctly binding to whatever color the current outer call provides.

Section 48.3 - Cell Normalization

sc_normalize_cells/2 translates a cell set to the canonical position:

  sc_normalize_cells(Cells, Normalized):
    Rs = [R : r(R, _) in Cells]
    Cs = [C : r(_, C) in Cells]
    MinR = min(Rs)
    MinC = min(Cs)
    Translated = [r(R - MinR, C - MinC) : r(R, C) in Cells]
    Normalized = sort(Translated)

Two cell sets represent the same shape if and only if their normalized forms are identical. Normalization ensures that position in the grid does not affect shape comparison. The sort step establishes a canonical ordering so that two cell sets with the same cells in different BFS orders compare equal.

Section 48.4 - Object Centroid

  sc_obj_centroid(obj(_, Cells), R, C):
    N = length(Cells)
    assert N > 0
    Rs = [RI : r(RI, _) in Cells]
    Cs = [CI : r(_, CI) in Cells]
    R = round(sum(Rs) / N)
    C = round(Cs) / N)

The centroid is the rounded center of mass. For single-cell objects, the centroid is exactly that cell. For multi-cell objects, it is the nearest-integer average position. The centroid does not need to be a cell of the object.

Section 48.5 - Spatial Relations

All spatial relations are defined in terms of bounding box corners:

  sc_above(Obj1, Obj2):
    TL1 = r(R1, _) = sc_obj_bbox(Obj1).topLeft
    TL2 = r(R2, _) = sc_obj_bbox(Obj2).topLeft
    R1 < R2

  sc_left_of(Obj1, Obj2):
    TL1 = r(_, C1) = sc_obj_bbox(Obj1).topLeft
    TL2 = r(_, C2) = sc_obj_bbox(Obj2).topLeft
    C1 < C2

  sc_cells_touching(Obj1, Obj2):
    exists r(R1, C1) in Obj1.cells,
           r(R2, C2) in Obj2.cells
    such that abs(R1-R2) + abs(C1-C2) = 1

The touching predicate uses a cut after finding the first touching pair, so it is deterministic. The cut is safe here because touching is a yes/no property; once one pair of adjacent cells is found, the answer is yes and no further search is needed.

Section 48.6 - Sort and Selection

  sc_sort_by_size(Objects, asc, Sorted):
    Pairs = [(size(O), O) : O in Objects]
    KSorted = keysort(Pairs)          % stable sort by integer key
    Sorted = [O : (_, O) in KSorted]

  sc_sort_by_size(Objects, desc, Sorted):
    Sorted = reverse(sc_sort_by_size(Objects, asc))

  sc_largest(Objects, Largest):
    Sorted = sc_sort_by_size(Objects, asc)
    Largest = last(Sorted)

  sc_smallest(Objects, Smallest):
    Sorted = sc_sort_by_size(Objects, asc)
    Smallest = head(Sorted)

keysort/2 is a SWI-Prolog built-in that sorts a list of Key-Value pairs by key using standard order. For integer keys (cell counts), standard order coincides with numeric order, so keysort gives ascending numeric sort. This is stable: objects of equal size retain their original relative order.

END OF DOCUMENT - PROLOGAI PSEUDOCODE


PART 49 - QUANT PACK ALGORITHMS

qn_histogram(Objects, Pairs):
  Colors = unique sorted colors across all objects
  For each Color in Colors: Count = count of objects with that color
  Pairs = [(Color, Count) for each Color]

qn_group_by_color/size/shape(Objects, Groups):
  Build Key-Obj pairs where Key = color/size/shape
  msort to order by key (preserving duplicates)
  group_pairs_by_key to collect all Obj under same Key

qn_most_frequent_color(Objects, Color):
  Histogram = qn_histogram(Objects)
  Color = key of the pair with maximum count (max_member)

qn_count_where(Objects, Pred, Count):
  include(Pred, Objects, Matching)
  Count = length(Matching)

qn_all_same_color/size/shape(Objects):
  Reference = attribute of first object
  maplist(has_attr_eq(Reference), remaining objects)

qn_colors_match/shapes_match/sizes_match(Objs1, Objs2):
  Collect attributes of both lists
  msort both attribute lists
  Sorted lists must be identical (==)

END OF DOCUMENT - PROLOGAI PSEUDOCODE


PART 50 - PATTERN PACK ALGORITHMS

pt_list_period(List, Period):
  N = length(List)
  for Period in 1..N:
    if list_has_period(List, Period): return Period (first/shortest)

list_has_period(List, P):
  Indices = [0..N-1]
  for each I in Indices:
    Base = I mod P
    List[I] must equal List[Base]

pt_tile_grid(Tile, Rows, Cols, Grid):
  TR = tile_rows, TC = tile_cols
  for R in 0..Rows-1:
    TileR = R mod TR
    TileRow = tile row at TileR
    for C in 0..Cols-1:
      TileC = C mod TC
      Grid[R][C] = TileRow[TileC]

pt_scale_up(Grid, Factor, Grid2):
  NewRows = Rows * Factor, NewCols = Cols * Factor
  for R2 in 0..NewRows-1:
    OrigR = R2 // Factor
    for C2 in 0..NewCols-1:
      OrigC = C2 // Factor
      Grid2[R2][C2] = Grid[OrigR][OrigC]

pt_scale_down(Grid, Factor, Grid2):
  NewRows = Rows // Factor, NewCols = Cols // Factor
  for R in 0..NewRows-1:
    OrigR = R * Factor
    for C in 0..NewCols-1:
      OrigC = C * Factor
      Grid2[R][C] = Grid[OrigR][OrigC]  (top-left cell of each block)

pt_repeat_h(Grid, N, Grid2):
  for each row R: Grid2[R] = concat N copies of Grid[R]

pt_repeat_v(Grid, N, Grid2):
  Grid2 = concat of N copies of the Grid row list (one-level append, not flatten)

pt_mirror_h(Grid, Grid2):
  Reflected = gd_reflect_v(Grid)
  for each row R: Grid2[R] = concat(Grid[R], Reflected[R])

pt_mirror_v(Grid, Grid2):
  Reflected = gd_reflect_h(Grid)
  Grid2 = append(Grid rows, Reflected rows)

pt_checkerboard(Rows, Cols, CA, CB, Grid):
  for R in 0..Rows-1, C in 0..Cols-1:
    if (R + C) mod 2 = 0: Grid[R][C] = CA else Grid[R][C] = CB

pt_stripe_h(Rows, Cols, Colors, Grid):
  NC = length(Colors)
  for R in 0..Rows-1: Grid[R] = fill(Colors[R mod NC], Cols)

pt_stripe_v(Rows, Cols, Colors, Grid):
  NC = length(Colors)
  for R in 0..Rows-1, C in 0..Cols-1: Grid[R][C] = Colors[C mod NC]

END OF DOCUMENT - PROLOGAI PSEUDOCODE


PART 51 - COMPOSE PACK ALGORITHMS

cp_pipe(Rules, Grid, Grid2):
  if Rules = []: Grid2 = Grid
  if Rules = [Rule|Rest]:
    Mid = cp_apply(Rule, Grid)
    Grid2 = cp_pipe(Rest, Mid)

cp_pipe_n(Rule, N, Grid, Grid2):
  Rules = N copies of Rule
  Grid2 = cp_pipe(Rules, Grid)

cp_branch(Cond, ThenRule, ElseRule, Grid, Grid2):
  if call(Cond, Grid): Grid2 = cp_apply(ThenRule, Grid)
  else: Grid2 = cp_apply(ElseRule, Grid)

cp_until(Rule, Cond, Grid, Grid2):
  if call(Cond, Grid): Grid2 = Grid
  else:
    Mid = cp_apply(Rule, Grid)
    Grid2 = cp_until(Rule, Cond, Mid)

cp_fixed_point(Rule, Grid, Grid2):
  Mid = cp_apply(Rule, Grid)
  if gd_equal(Grid, Mid): Grid2 = Grid
  else: Grid2 = cp_fixed_point(Rule, Mid)

cp_map_rows(RowRule, Grid, Grid2):
  Grid2 = [call(RowRule, Row) for each Row in Grid]

cp_map_cols(ColRule, Grid, Grid2):
  TransformedCols = [call(ColRule, gd_col(Grid, C)) for each column C]
  Grid2[R][C] = TransformedCols[C][R]  for all R, C

cp_zip(Rule, GridA, GridB, GridC):
  GridC[R][C] = call(Rule, GridA[R][C], GridB[R][C])  for all R, C

cp_fold(Rule, Acc, Grids, Result):
  if Grids = []: Result = Acc
  if Grids = [G|Gs]:
    NewAcc = call(Rule, Acc, G)
    Result = cp_fold(Rule, NewAcc, Gs)

END OF DOCUMENT - PROLOGAI PSEUDOCODE


PART 52 - MOTION PACK ALGORITHMS

mv_gravity_down(Grid, Bg, Grid2):
  for each column C in 0..Cols-1:
    Col = gd_col(Grid, C)
    Fg = [x in Col : x != Bg]
    BgLen = length(Col) - length(Fg)
    NewCol = [Bg x BgLen] ++ Fg
    set column C in Grid to NewCol

mv_gravity_up: same but NewCol = Fg ++ [Bg x BgLen]
mv_gravity_left: same operation per row (Fg ++ BgRight)
mv_gravity_right: same operation per row (BgLeft ++ Fg)

mv_shift_grid(Grid, DR, DC, Bg, Grid2):
  Grid2 = gd_translate(Grid, DR, DC, Bg)

mv_obj_translate(obj(Color, Cells), DR, DC, Obj2):
  NewCells = [r(R+DR, C+DC) : r(R,C) in Cells]
  Obj2 = obj(Color, msort(NewCells))

mv_scene_gravity(Scene, Scene2):
  Grid = mv_scene_to_grid(Scene)
  Grid2 = mv_gravity_down(Grid, Scene.Bg)
  Scene2 = sc_grid_to_scene(Grid2)

mv_scene_to_grid(scene(Rows, Cols, Bg, Objects), Grid):
  Grid = gd_make(Rows, Cols, Bg)
  for each obj(Color, Cells) in Objects:
    for each r(R,C) in Cells:
      Grid[R][C] = Color

mv_distance(r(R1,C1), r(R2,C2), D):
  D = abs(R2-R1) + abs(C2-C1)

mv_closest_cell([H|T], Ref, Closest):
  D0 = mv_distance(H, Ref)
  foldl(closer_cell(Ref), T, H-D0, Closest-_)

END OF DOCUMENT - PROLOGAI PSEUDOCODE


PART 53 - FRAME PACK PSEUDOCODE

Module: frame, Layer 42

FR_BORDER_CELLS(Grid) ->
  Rows, Cols = gd_size(Grid)
  R1 = Rows-1, C1 = Cols-1
  TopRow = [(R=0,C) for C in 0..C1]
  BotRow = [(R=R1,C) for C in 0..C1] if R1 > 0
  LeftCol = [(R,C=0) for R in 1..R1-1]
  RightCol = [(R,C=C1) for R in 1..R1-1] if C1 > 0
  Positions = TopRow + BotRow + LeftCol + RightCol
  return [(r(R,C), gd_cell(Grid,R,C)) for (R,C) in Positions]

FR_BORDER_COLOR(Grid) ->
  Pairs = FR_BORDER_CELLS(Grid)
  Color = color of first pair
  all other pairs have same Color
  return Color

FR_INNER(Grid) ->
  Rows, Cols = gd_size(Grid)
  require Rows >= 3 and Cols >= 3
  return [[Grid[R][C] for C in 1..Cols-2] for R in 1..Rows-2]

FR_ADD_BORDER(Grid, Thickness, Color) ->
  Rows2 = Rows + 2*Thickness
  Cols2 = Cols + 2*Thickness
  Base = uniform grid of Color, Rows2 x Cols2
  for each (R,C) in Grid:
    Base[R+Thickness][C+Thickness] = Grid[R][C]
  return Base

FR_MAKE_FRAMED(Rows, Cols, FrameColor, FillColor) ->
  Grid = uniform FrameColor, Rows x Cols
  if Rows >= 3 and Cols >= 3:
    fill interior (rows 1..Rows-2, cols 1..Cols-2) with FillColor
  return Grid

FR_BOUNDING_BOX(Grid, FrameColor) ->
  MaxR = Rows-1, MaxC = Cols-1
  shrink from (0,0,MaxR,MaxC) inward until outer ring = FrameColor
  return first (R0,C0,R1,C1) where FR_REGION_HAS_BORDER succeeds

FR_RING_COUNT(Grid) ->
  N = 0
  Loop:
    if Grid has fewer than 3 rows or 3 cols: return N
    if FR_BORDER_COLOR(Grid) succeeds and FR_INNER(Grid) = Inner:
      N = N + 1
      Grid = Inner
    else:
      return N

END OF PART 53


PART 54 - PATH PACK PSEUDOCODE

Module: path, Layer 43

PF_NEIGHBORS(Grid, r(R,C)) ->
  MaxR = Rows-1, MaxC = Cols-1
  return [r(R-1,C), r(R+1,C), r(R,C-1), r(R,C+1)] filtered to valid bounds

PF_FLOOD_FILL(Grid, Seed, Color) ->
  Queue = [Seed], Visited = [Seed]
  while Queue not empty:
    Current = dequeue(Queue)
    for each N in PF_NEIGHBORS(Grid, Current):
      if Grid[N] = Color and N not in Visited:
        enqueue(Queue, N)
        add N to Visited
  return sort(Visited)

PF_COMPONENTS(Grid, Color) ->
  AllCells = all cells where Grid[R][C] = Color
  Components = []
  while AllCells not empty:
    Seed = first(AllCells)
    Region = PF_FLOOD_FILL(Grid, Seed, Color)
    Components += [Region]
    AllCells = AllCells - Region
  return Components

PF_LARGEST_COMPONENT(Grid, Color) ->
  Components = PF_COMPONENTS(Grid, Color)
  return the component with maximum length

PF_SHORTEST_PATH(Grid, Start, Goal, Wall) ->
  Frontier = [[Start]]  (each element is a reverse path)
  while Frontier not empty:
    Path = dequeue(Frontier)
    Head = first(Path)
    if Head = Goal: return reverse(Path)
    for each N in PF_NEIGHBORS(Grid, Head):
      if Grid[N] != Wall and N not in Path:
        enqueue(Frontier, [N|Path])
  fail

PF_REACHABLE(Grid, Seed, Wall) ->
  same as PF_FLOOD_FILL but include any cell where Grid[N] != Wall

PF_FILL_BBOX(Grid, Seed, Color) ->
  Region = PF_FLOOD_FILL(Grid, Seed, Color)
  R0 = min row in Region, R1 = max row
  C0 = min col in Region, C1 = max col
  return (R0, C0, R1, C1)

PF_IS_CONNECTED(Grid, Color) ->
  N = PF_COMPONENT_COUNT(Grid, Color)
  return N <= 1

END OF PART 54


PART 55 - SYMMETRY PACK PSEUDOCODE

Module: symmetry, Layer 44

SY_IS_HSYMMETRIC(Grid) ->
  Grid2 = gd_reflect_v(Grid)
  return gd_equal(Grid, Grid2)

SY_IS_VSYMMETRIC(Grid) ->
  Grid2 = gd_reflect_h(Grid)
  return gd_equal(Grid, Grid2)

SY_IS_ROT180(Grid) ->
  R180 = gd_rotate90(gd_rotate90(Grid))
  return gd_equal(Grid, R180)

SY_IS_ROT90(Grid) ->
  require square grid
  return gd_equal(Grid, gd_rotate90(Grid))

SY_IS_DIAGONAL(Grid) ->
  require square grid
  return gd_equal(Grid, gd_reflect_d1(Grid))

SY_IS_ANTIDIAGONAL(Grid) ->
  require square grid
  return gd_equal(Grid, gd_reflect_d2(Grid))

SY_GROUP(Grid) ->
  return [Sym for Sym in [h,v,rot180,rot90,diag,antidiag] if SY_TEST_SYM(Grid, Sym)]

SY_ROTATIONS(Grid) ->
  Candidates = [Grid, R90, R180, R270]
  return unique_grids(Candidates)  % remove duplicates by gd_equal

SY_ORBIT(Grid) ->
  HFlip = gd_reflect_v(Grid)
  return unique_grids(SY_ROTATIONS(Grid) + SY_ROTATIONS(HFlip))

SY_CANONICAL(Grid) ->
  Orbit = SY_ORBIT(Grid)
  return min(Orbit) under @< term ordering

SY_EQUIVALENT(GridA, GridB) ->
  return gd_equal(SY_CANONICAL(GridA), SY_CANONICAL(GridB))

SY_ORDER(Grid) ->
  return 8 // length(SY_ORBIT(Grid))

END OF PART 55


PART 56: COLOR PACK (PR 66)

CL_PALETTE(Grid) ->
  AllColors = [Color for R,C in Grid if gd_cell(Grid,R,C,Color)]
  return sort(AllColors)

CL_COUNT(Grid, Color) ->
  Cells = [r(R,C) for R,C in Grid if gd_cell(Grid,R,C,Color)]
  return length(Cells)

CL_HISTOGRAM(Grid) ->
  Palette = CL_PALETTE(Grid)
  return [Color-CL_COUNT(Grid,Color) for Color in Palette]

CL_SAME_PALETTE(Grid1, Grid2) ->
  return CL_PALETTE(Grid1) = CL_PALETTE(Grid2)

CL_REPLACE(Grid, OldColor, NewColor) ->
  for each Row in Grid:
    for each Cell in Row:
      if Cell = OldColor then NewColor else Cell

CL_REMAP(Grid, Mapping) ->
  for each Cell in Grid:
    if member(Cell-NewColor, Mapping) then NewColor else Cell

CL_DOMINANT(Grid) ->
  Hist = CL_HISTOGRAM(Grid)
  CountColor = [Count-Color for Color-Count in Hist]
  return Color where (Count-Color) = max_member(CountColor)

CL_RAREST(Grid) ->
  Hist = CL_HISTOGRAM(Grid)
  CountColor = [Count-Color for Color-Count in Hist]
  return Color where (Count-Color) = min_member(CountColor)

CL_ISOLATE(Grid, Color, BgColor) ->
  for each Cell in Grid:
    if Cell = Color then Color else BgColor

CL_REMOVE(Grid, Color, BgColor) ->
  return CL_REPLACE(Grid, Color, BgColor)

CL_IS_MONO(Grid) ->
  return length(CL_PALETTE(Grid)) = 1

CL_COLOR_COUNT(Grid) ->
  return length(CL_PALETTE(Grid))

CL_HAS_COLOR(Grid, Color) ->
  return exists r(R,C) in Grid where gd_cell(Grid,R,C,Color)

CL_SWAP(Grid, ColorA, ColorB) ->
  for each Cell in Grid:
    if Cell = ColorA then ColorB
    else if Cell = ColorB then ColorA
    else Cell

END OF PART 56


PART 57: SHAPE PACK (PR 67)

SH_FROM_CELLS(Cells) ->
  MinR = min(R for r(R,_) in Cells)
  MinC = min(C for r(_,C) in Cells)
  Shifted = [r(R-MinR, C-MinC) for r(R,C) in Cells]
  return sort(Shifted)

SH_FROM_GRID(Grid, Color) ->
  Cells = [r(R,C) for R,C in Grid if gd_cell(Grid,R,C,Color)]
  return SH_FROM_CELLS(Cells)

SH_AREA(Shape) ->
  return length(Shape)

SH_BOUNDING_SIZE(Shape) ->
  MaxR = max(R for r(R,_) in Shape)
  MaxC = max(C for r(_,C) in Shape)
  return (MaxR+1, MaxC+1)

SH_CONTAINS_CELL(Shape, Cell) ->
  return member(Cell, Shape)  // deterministic (cut after first match)

SH_EQUAL(Shape1, Shape2) ->
  return Shape1 == Shape2

SH_TRANSLATE(Shape, DR, DC) ->
  return [r(R+DR, C+DC) for r(R,C) in Shape]

SH_ROTATE90(Shape) ->
  MaxR = max(R for r(R,_) in Shape)
  Rotated = [r(C, MaxR-R) for r(R,C) in Shape]
  return SH_FROM_CELLS(Rotated)

SH_REFLECT_H(Shape) ->
  MaxC = max(C for r(_,C) in Shape)
  Reflected = [r(R, MaxC-C) for r(R,C) in Shape]
  return SH_FROM_CELLS(Reflected)

SH_REFLECT_V(Shape) ->
  MaxR = max(R for r(R,_) in Shape)
  Reflected = [r(MaxR-R, C) for r(R,C) in Shape]
  return SH_FROM_CELLS(Reflected)

SH_ORBIT(Shape) ->
  HFlip = SH_REFLECT_H(Shape)
  Rotations1 = [Shape, SH_ROTATE90(Shape), SH_ROTATE90^2(Shape), SH_ROTATE90^3(Shape)]
  Rotations2 = [HFlip, SH_ROTATE90(HFlip), SH_ROTATE90^2(HFlip), SH_ROTATE90^3(HFlip)]
  All = Rotations1 ++ Rotations2
  return unique_shapes(All)  // remove duplicates by ==

SH_CANONICAL(Shape) ->
  return min(SH_ORBIT(Shape)) under @< term ordering

SH_EQUIVALENT(Shape1, Shape2) ->
  return SH_CANONICAL(Shape1) == SH_CANONICAL(Shape2)

SH_TO_GRID(Shape, DR, DC, Color, Grid) ->
  for r(R,C) in Shape:
    Grid = gd_set_cell(Grid, R+DR, C+DC, Color)
  return Grid

END OF PART 57


PART 58: RELATION PACK (PR 68)

RL_ABOVE(A, B) ->
  MaxR_A = max(R for r(R,_) in A)
  MinR_B = min(R for r(R,_) in B)
  return MaxR_A < MinR_B

RL_BELOW(A, B) ->
  MinR_A = min(R for r(R,_) in A)
  MaxR_B = max(R for r(R,_) in B)
  return MinR_A > MaxR_B

RL_LEFT_OF(A, B) ->
  MaxC_A = max(C for r(_,C) in A)
  MinC_B = min(C for r(_,C) in B)
  return MaxC_A < MinC_B

RL_RIGHT_OF(A, B) ->
  MinC_A = min(C for r(_,C) in A)
  MaxC_B = max(C for r(_,C) in B)
  return MinC_A > MaxC_B

RL_ADJACENT(A, B) ->
  return exists r(R1,C1) in A, r(R2,C2) in B where
    (R1=R2 and |C1-C2|=1) or (C1=C2 and |R1-R2|=1)

RL_DISTANCE(A, B) ->
  return min(|R1-R2|+|C1-C2| for r(R1,C1) in A, r(R2,C2) in B)

RL_CONTAINED_BBOX(A, B) ->
  (MinR_A, MaxR_A, MinC_A, MaxC_A) = bounding_box(A)
  (MinR_B, MaxR_B, MinC_B, MaxC_B) = bounding_box(B)
  return MinR_A >= MinR_B and MaxR_A <= MaxR_B
     and MinC_A >= MinC_B and MaxC_A <= MaxC_B

RL_OVERLAP(A, B) ->
  return exists Cell in A where Cell in B

RL_DISJOINT(A, B) ->
  return not RL_OVERLAP(A, B)

RL_SAME_ROW(A, B) ->
  return exists r(R,_) in A, r(R,_) in B

RL_SAME_COL(A, B) ->
  return exists r(_,C) in A, r(_,C) in B

RL_CENTROID(Region) ->
  SumR = sum(R for r(R,_) in Region)
  SumC = sum(C for r(_,C) in Region)
  N = length(Region)
  return (SumR // N, SumC // N)

RL_OFFSET(A, B) ->
  (RA, CA) = RL_CENTROID(A)
  (RB, CB) = RL_CENTROID(B)
  return (RB - RA, CB - CA)

RL_DIRECTION(A, B) ->
  (DR, DC) = RL_OFFSET(A, B)
  if DR < 0 and |DR| >= |DC|: return above
  if DR > 0 and |DR| >= |DC|: return below
  if DC < 0 and |DC| > |DR|: return left
  if DC > 0 and |DC| > |DR|: return right
  else: fail

END OF PART 58


PART 59: SEQUENCE PACK (PR 69)

SQ_RANGE(Lo, Hi) ->
  if Lo > Hi: return []
  else: return [Lo, Lo+1, ..., Hi]  % via numlist

SQ_DELTA([_]) -> []
SQ_DELTA([A, B | T]) ->
  return [B-A | SQ_DELTA([B|T])]

SQ_IS_ARITHMETIC([]) -> true
SQ_IS_ARITHMETIC([_]) -> true
SQ_IS_ARITHMETIC([A, B | T]) ->
  D = B - A
  check all consecutive pairs in [B|T] have difference D

SQ_COMMON_DIFF([A, B | T]) ->
  D = B - A
  verify SQ_IS_ARITHMETIC_([B|T], D)
  return D

SQ_EXTEND_ARITH(List, N) ->
  D = SQ_COMMON_DIFF(List)
  Last = last(List)
  Extra = [Last+D, Last+2D, ..., Last+N*D]
  return List ++ Extra

SQ_CHUNK([], N) -> []
SQ_CHUNK(List, N) ->
  Chunk = first N elements of List
  Rest = remaining elements
  return [Chunk | SQ_CHUNK(Rest, N)]

SQ_ZIP([A|As], [B|Bs]) -> [A-B | SQ_ZIP(As, Bs)]
SQ_ZIP([], []) -> []

SQ_UNZIP([A-B|Ps]) ->
  (As, Bs) = SQ_UNZIP(Ps)
  return ([A|As], [B|Bs])
SQ_UNZIP([]) -> ([], [])

SQ_CUMSUM([H|T]) ->
  Prev = H
  for each X in T: Prev = Prev + X, emit Prev
  return [H | emitted values]

SQ_SLICE(List, From, To) ->
  drop first From elements from List
  take next (To - From) elements

SQ_FLATTEN1(Lists) ->
  return append(Lists)

SQ_TRANSPOSE([]) -> []
SQ_TRANSPOSE(Matrix) ->
  Row = [head(L) for L in Matrix]
  RestMatrix = [tail(L) for L in Matrix]
  return [Row | SQ_TRANSPOSE(RestMatrix)]

SQ_PERIOD(List) ->
  Len = length(List)
  for K in 1..Len:
    if Len mod K = 0:
      P = first K elements of List
      if List = P repeated (Len/K) times: return P

SQ_IS_PERIODIC(List) ->
  Len = length(List)
  if Len < 2: fail
  P = SQ_PERIOD(List)
  if length(P) < Len: succeed

END OF PART 59


PART 60: CROP PACK PSEUDOCODE

cr_bbox(Grid, BG, bbox(MinR,MinC,MaxR,MaxC)):
  collect all (R,C) pairs where Grid[R][C] != BG
  fail if collection is empty
  MinR = min of all R, MaxR = max of all R
  MinC = min of all C, MaxC = max of all C

cr_crop_bbox(Grid, R1, C1, R2, C2, Sub):
  for each row R in R1..R2:
    extract columns C1..C2 from Grid[R]
  return list of extracted rows

cr_crop_content(Grid, BG, Cropped):
  call cr_bbox to get bbox(R1,C1,R2,C2)
  call cr_crop_bbox with those bounds

cr_pad(Grid, Color, N, Padded):
  PadCols = width(Grid) + 2*N
  TopRows = N copies of [Color x PadCols]
  BotRows = N copies of [Color x PadCols]
  MidRows = each row of Grid prepended and appended with N copies of Color
  Padded = concat(TopRows, MidRows, BotRows)

cr_strip_border(Grid, N, Inner):
  R1=N, R2=Rows-N-1, C1=N, C2=Cols-N-1
  call cr_crop_bbox(Grid, R1, C1, R2, C2, Inner)

cr_split_h(Grid, R, Top, Bottom):
  Top = first R rows of Grid
  Bottom = remaining rows

cr_split_v(Grid, C, Left, Right):
  for each row: Left[i] = first C cols, Right[i] = remaining cols

cr_rows(Grid, From, To, Sub):
  Sub = rows From..To-1 of Grid (skip first From, take To-From)

cr_cols(Grid, From, To, Sub):
  for each row: take cols From..To-1

cr_stitch_h(Left, Right, Joined):
  for each pair (L[i], R[i]): Joined[i] = L[i] ++ R[i]

cr_stitch_v(Top, Bottom, Joined):
  Joined = Top ++ Bottom

cr_embed(Base, Sub, R, C, Result):
  Pre = first R rows of Base unchanged
  for each row i in 0..SubH-1:
    Result[R+i] = Base[R+i] with columns C..C+SubW-1 replaced by Sub[i]
  Suf = remaining rows of Base unchanged

cr_center(Grid, Rows, Cols, Center):
  R1 = (GH-Rows)//2, C1 = (GW-Cols)//2
  R2 = R1+Rows-1, C2 = C1+Cols-1
  call cr_crop_bbox(Grid, R1, C1, R2, C2, Center)

cr_quadrants(Grid, Q1, Q2, Q3, Q4):
  MidR = Rows//2, MidC = Cols//2
  Top = rows 0..MidR-1; Bottom = rows MidR..end
  Q1,Q2 = split Top at MidC
  Q3,Q4 = split Bottom at MidC

END OF PART 60


PART 61: OVERLAY PACK PSEUDOCODE

ov_over(A, B, BG, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = B[r][c] if B[r][c]!=BG else A[r][c]

ov_blend(A, B, BG, Result):
  same as ov_over

ov_or(A, B, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = A[r][c] bitwise-or B[r][c]

ov_and(A, B, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = A[r][c] bitwise-and B[r][c]

ov_xor(A, B, BG, Result):
  for each (r,c):
    if A[r][c]!=BG and B[r][c]=BG: Result[r][c]=A[r][c]
    if B[r][c]!=BG and A[r][c]=BG: Result[r][c]=B[r][c]
    else: Result[r][c]=BG

ov_diff(A, B, BG, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = A[r][c] if A[r][c]!=B[r][c] else BG

ov_intersect(A, B, BG, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = A[r][c] if A[r][c]=B[r][c] else BG

ov_mask(Grid, Mask, BG, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = Grid[r][c] if Mask[r][c]!=BG else BG

ov_mask_inv(Grid, Mask, BG, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = Grid[r][c] if Mask[r][c]=BG else BG

ov_priority(Grids, BG, Result):
  for each (r,c):
    Result[r][c] = first G[r][c] in Grids where G[r][c]!=BG
    if all are BG: Result[r][c] = BG

ov_replace(Grid, Old, New, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = New if Grid[r][c]=Old else Grid[r][c]

ov_fill_bg(Grid, BG, Fill, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = Fill if Grid[r][c]=BG else Grid[r][c]

ov_max(A, B, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = max(A[r][c], B[r][c])

ov_min(A, B, Result):
  for each (r,c): Result[r][c] = min(A[r][c], B[r][c])

END OF PART 61


PART 62: MEASURE PACK PSEUDOCODE

ms_area(Region, N): N = length(Region).

ms_bbox(Region, bbox(R1,C1,R2,C2)):
  Rs = all row indices; Cs = all col indices
  R1=min(Rs), R2=max(Rs), C1=min(Cs), C2=max(Cs)

ms_bbox_size(Region, W, H):
  ms_bbox -> R1,C1,R2,C2; W=C2-C1+1; H=R2-R1+1

ms_perimeter(Region, P):
  for each Cell in Region:
    N = count of 4-neighbors of Cell not in Region
  P = sum of all N

ms_diameter(Region, D):
  D = max over all pairs (C1,C2) in Region of manhattan(C1,C2)

ms_extent(Region, N, D):
  N = area; D = bbox_W * bbox_H

ms_aspect(Region, N, D):
  W,H = bbox_size; N=max(W,H); D=min(W,H)

ms_row_span(Region, S): S = |distinct rows in Region|

ms_col_span(Region, S): S = |distinct cols in Region|

ms_centroid(Region, AvgR, AvgC):
  AvgR = sum(Rs) // N; AvgC = sum(Cs) // N

ms_radius(Region, Rad):
  centroid = (CR,CC)
  Rad = max Chebyshev distance from (CR,CC) to any cell

ms_interior_count(Region, N):
  N = count(cells in Region where all 4 neighbors are also in Region)

ms_border_count(Region, N):
  N = count(cells in Region where at least one 4-neighbor is outside)

ms_color_count(Grid, N):
  flatten Grid; sort; deduplicate; N = length

END OF PART 62


PART 63: TRANSFORM PACK PSEUDOCODE (Work Package 73)

tr_scale_up(Grid, Factor, Scaled):
  For each Row in Grid:
    For each cell V in Row:
      Emit Factor copies of V -> forms ExpandedRow
    Collect all ExpandedRows
  For each ExpandedRow:
    Emit Factor copies of ExpandedRow
  Scaled = flattened collection of all copies

tr_scale_down(Grid, Factor, Scaled):
  RowIds = [0, 1, ..., Rows-1]
  SelRowIds = [R in RowIds | R mod Factor = 0]
  ColIds = [0, 1, ..., Cols-1]
  SelColIds = [C in ColIds | C mod Factor = 0]
  For each R in SelRowIds:
    Row = Grid[R]
    For each C in SelColIds:
      emit Row[C]
    -> SelRow
  Scaled = [SelRow for each R in SelRowIds]

tr_tile_h(Grid, N, Tiled):
  For each Row in Grid:
    TiledRow = Row ++ Row ++ ... (N times)
  Tiled = [TiledRow for each Row in Grid]

tr_tile_v(Grid, N, Tiled):
  Tiled = Grid ++ Grid ++ ... (N times)

tr_tile(Grid, N, Tiled):
  H = tr_tile_h(Grid, N)
  Tiled = tr_tile_v(H, N)

tr_transpose(Grid, Transposed):
  While Grid has non-empty rows:
    Col = first element of each row in Grid
    Grid = tail of each row in Grid
    emit Col
  Transposed = [Col1, Col2, ...]

tr_flip_h(Grid, Flipped):
  For each Row in Grid: emit reverse(Row)
  Flipped = [ReversedRow ...]

tr_flip_v(Grid, Flipped):
  Flipped = reverse(Grid)

tr_rot90(Grid, Rotated):
  T = tr_transpose(Grid)
  Rotated = tr_flip_h(T)

tr_rot180(Grid, Rotated):
  V = tr_flip_v(Grid)
  Rotated = tr_flip_h(V)

tr_shift(Grid, DR, DC, Fill, Shifted):
  For each (R, C) in [0..Rows-1] x [0..Cols-1]:
    SR = R - DR, SC = C - DC
    If SR in [0..Rows-1] and SC in [0..Cols-1]:
      Shifted[R][C] = Grid[SR][SC]
    Else:
      Shifted[R][C] = Fill

tr_apply_map(Grid, Map, Result):
  For each cell V in Grid:
    If V-To in Map: emit To
    Else: emit V
  Result = same dimensions as Grid with mapped values

tr_replace_color(Grid, From, To, Result):
  Equivalent to tr_apply_map(Grid, [From-To], Result)

tr_mask_grid(Grid, Mask, Fill, Result):
  For each (R, C):
    If Mask[R][C] = 0: Result[R][C] = Fill
    Else: Result[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

END OF PART 63


PART 64: SELECT PACK PSEUDOCODE (Work Package 74)

sl_largest(Regions, Largest):
  Areas = [length(R) for R in Regions]
  MaxArea = max(Areas)
  Idx = first index where Areas[Idx] = MaxArea
  Largest = Regions[Idx]

sl_smallest(Regions, Smallest):
  Areas = [length(R) for R in Regions]
  MinArea = min(Areas)
  Idx = first index where Areas[Idx] = MinArea
  Smallest = Regions[Idx]

sl_sort_by_area(Regions, Sorted):
  Keyed = [(length(R), R) for R in Regions]
  SortedKeyed = keysort(Keyed)   % stable sort by key
  Sorted = [R for (_, R) in SortedKeyed]

sl_filter_area(Regions, N, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if length(R) = N]

sl_filter_area_min(Regions, Min, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if length(R) >= Min]

sl_filter_area_max(Regions, Max, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if length(R) <= Max]

sl_touches_border(Region, Rows, Cols):
  MaxR = Rows - 1, MaxC = Cols - 1
  Exists cell r(R,C) in Region such that R=0 OR R=MaxR OR C=0 OR C=MaxC

sl_filter_border(Regions, Rows, Cols, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if sl_touches_border(R, Rows, Cols)]

sl_filter_interior(Regions, Rows, Cols, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if NOT sl_touches_border(R, Rows, Cols)]

sl_above_row(Regions, Row, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if all r(Ri,_) in R have Ri < Row]

sl_below_row(Regions, Row, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if all r(Ri,_) in R have Ri >= Row]

sl_left_of_col(Regions, Col, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if all r(_,Ci) in R have Ci < Col]

sl_right_of_col(Regions, Col, Filtered):
  Filtered = [R for R in Regions if all r(_,Ci) in R have Ci >= Col]

sl_unique_area(Regions, Unique):
  Areas = [length(R) for R in Regions]
  UniqueAreas = [A for A in Areas if count(A in Areas) = 1]
  Unique = [R for R in Regions if length(R) in UniqueAreas]

END OF PART 64


PART 65: COUNT PACK PSEUDOCODE (Work Package 75)

cn_by_value(List, V, N):
  N = count(X in List such that X = V)

cn_color_count(Grid, Color, N):
  Flat = flatten(Grid)
  N = cn_by_value(Flat, Color)

cn_histogram(Grid, Colors, Counts):
  Flat = flatten(Grid)
  Sorted = msort(Flat)   // sort preserving duplicates
  Pairs = group_consecutive_equal(Sorted)  // each unique value with its count
  Colors = [K for K-V in Pairs]
  Counts = [V for K-V in Pairs]

cn_max_color(Grid, Color):
  Colors, Counts = cn_histogram(Grid)
  MaxCount = max(Counts)
  Idx = first index where Counts[Idx] = MaxCount
  Color = Colors[Idx]

cn_min_color(Grid, Color):
  Colors, Counts = cn_histogram(Grid)
  MinCount = min(Counts)
  Idx = first index where Counts[Idx] = MinCount
  Color = Colors[Idx]

cn_color_rows(Grid, Color, N):
  N = count(Row in Grid such that Color in Row)

cn_color_cols(Grid, Color, N):
  N = count(C in [0..Cols-1] such that Color in column C of Grid)

cn_row_distinct(Grid, R, N):
  Row = Grid[R]
  N = length(sort(Row))

cn_col_distinct(Grid, C, N):
  Col = [Grid[R][C] for R in [0..Rows-1]]
  N = length(sort(Col))

cn_grid_total(Grid, N):
  Rows, Cols = dimensions(Grid)
  N = Rows * Cols

cn_equal_cells(Grid1, Grid2, N):
  Flags = [1 if Grid1[R][C] = Grid2[R][C] else 0 for all (R,C)]
  N = sum(Flags)

cn_diff_cells(Grid1, Grid2, N):
  N = cn_grid_total(Grid1) - cn_equal_cells(Grid1, Grid2)

cn_region_color(Grid, [r(R,C)|_], Color):
  Color = Grid[R][C]

cn_regions_per_color(Grid, Regions, Pairs):
  Colors = [cn_region_color(Grid, R) for R in Regions]
  Pairs = tally(Colors)   // each Color-Count for unique colors

END OF PART 65


PART 66: FILL PACK PSEUDOCODE (Work Package 76)

fl_fill_region(Grid, Region, Color, Result):
  For each (R, C) in Grid:
    If r(R,C) in Region: Result[R][C] = Color
    Else: Result[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

fl_fill_bbox(Grid, bbox(R1,C1,R2,C2), Color, Result):
  For each (R, C) in Grid:
    If R1 <= R <= R2 and C1 <= C <= C2: Result[R][C] = Color
    Else: Result[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

fl_fill_row(Grid, TargetR, Color, Result):
  For row R:
    If R = TargetR: all cells become Color
    Else: row unchanged

fl_fill_col(Grid, TargetC, Color, Result):
  For each row R:
    Result[R][TargetC] = Color; all other cells unchanged

fl_fill_cells(Grid, Cells, Color, Result):
  Equivalent to fl_fill_region(Grid, Cells, Color, Result)

fl_fill_border(Grid, Color, Result):
  Fill row 0, row Rows-1, col 0, col Cols-1 with Color

fl_outline_region(Grid, Region, Color, Result):
  BorderCells = {Cell in Region | some 4-neighbor of Cell is not in Region}
  fl_fill_cells(Grid, BorderCells, Color, Result)

fl_fill_interior(Grid, Region, Color, Result):
  InteriorCells = {Cell in Region | all 4-neighbors of Cell are in Region}
  fl_fill_cells(Grid, InteriorCells, Color, Result)

fl_solid_rect(Rows, Cols, Color, Grid):
  Row = [Color] * Cols
  Grid = [Row] * Rows

fl_checkerboard(Rows, Cols, C1, C2, Grid):
  For each (R, C):
    Grid[R][C] = C1 if (R+C) even, else C2

fl_draw_hline(Grid, R, C1, C2, Color, Result):
  fl_fill_bbox(Grid, bbox(R, C1, R, C2), Color, Result)

fl_draw_vline(Grid, C, R1, R2, Color, Result):
  fl_fill_bbox(Grid, bbox(R1, C, R2, C), Color, Result)

fl_fill_main_diag(Grid, Color, Result):
  DiagCells = {r(I,I) | I in [0..Rows-1]}
  fl_fill_cells(Grid, DiagCells, Color, Result)

fl_stamp(Base, Stamp, SR, SC, BG, Result):
  For each (R, C) in Base:
    StampR = R - SR, StampC = C - SC
    If (StampR, StampC) in bounds of Stamp:
      V = Stamp[StampR][StampC]
      If V != BG: Result[R][C] = V
      Else: Result[R][C] = Base[R][C]
    Else: Result[R][C] = Base[R][C]

END OF PART 66


PART 67: PSEUDOCODE - PATTERN PACK (Work Package 77)

pt_row_period(Row, P):
  Len = length(Row)
  For P = 1 to Len:
    If for all i in 0..Len-1: Row[i] = Row[i mod P]
      Return P (cut)

pt_col_period(Grid, C, P):
  Col = [Row[C] for Row in Grid]
  Return pt_row_period(Col, P)

pt_grid_period_h(Grid, P):
  Cols = length(Grid[0])
  For P = 1 to Cols:
    If for all Row in Grid: pt_row_period(Row, P) divides P
      Return P (cut)
  Implementation: for each candidate P, every row must satisfy period_ok_(Row, P).

pt_grid_period_v(Grid, P):
  Rows = length(Grid)
  For P = 1 to Rows:
    If for all C in 0..Cols-1: pt_col_period(Grid, C, P-divides)
      Return P (cut)

pt_tile_unit_h(Grid, Tile):
  P = pt_grid_period_h(Grid)
  Tile = [first_P_elements(Row) for Row in Grid]

pt_tile_unit_v(Grid, Tile):
  P = pt_grid_period_v(Grid)
  Tile = first_P_rows(Grid)

pt_tile_unit(Grid, Tile):
  PH = pt_grid_period_h(Grid)
  PV = pt_grid_period_v(Grid)
  Tile = [first_PH_elements(Row) for Row in first_PV_rows(Grid)]

pt_is_tiling(Grid, Tile):
  TH = length(Tile), TW = length(Tile[0])
  For R in 0..Rows-1:
    For C in 0..Cols-1:
      If Grid[R][C] != Tile[R mod TH][C mod TW]: Fail
  Succeed

pt_find_tile(Grid, Tile, Positions):
  TH = length(Tile), TW = length(Tile[0])
  MaxR = Rows - TH, MaxC = Cols - TW
  Positions = [r(R,C) for R in 0..MaxR, C in 0..MaxC
               if tile_matches_at(Grid, Tile, R, C)]

pt_tile_matches_at(Grid, Tile, R, C):
  For TR in 0..TH-1, TC in 0..TW-1:
    If Grid[R+TR][C+TC] != Tile[TR][TC]: Fail
  Succeed

pt_count_tile(Grid, Tile, N):
  Positions = pt_find_tile(Grid, Tile)
  N = length(Positions)

pt_extract_tile(Grid, r(R,C), H, W, Tile):
  Tile = [Grid[R+DR][C .. C+W-1] for DR in 0..H-1]

pt_unique_rows(Grid, N):
  Unique = sort(Grid)  % sort removes duplicates
  N = length(Unique)

pt_unique_cols(Grid, N):
  AllCols = [column(Grid, C) for C in 0..Cols-1]
  Unique = sort(AllCols)
  N = length(Unique)

pt_has_uniform_rows(Grid):
  sort(Grid) has length 1

END OF PART 67


PART 68: PSEUDOCODE - COMPARE PACK (Work Package 78)

cp_diff_cells(Grid1, Grid2, Diffs):
  All = all r(R,C) positions in Grid1
  Diffs = [Cell for Cell in All if Grid1[R][C] != Grid2[R][C]]

cp_same_cells(Grid1, Grid2, Sames):
  All = all r(R,C) positions in Grid1
  Sames = [Cell for Cell in All if Grid1[R][C] = Grid2[R][C]]

cp_added_color(Grid1, Grid2, Color, Added):
  All = all r(R,C) positions
  Added = [Cell for Cell in All if Grid2[R][C] = Color and Grid1[R][C] != Color]

cp_removed_color(Grid1, Grid2, Color, Removed):
  All = all r(R,C) positions
  Removed = [Cell for Cell in All if Grid1[R][C] = Color and Grid2[R][C] != Color]

cp_changed_to(Grid1, Grid2, Color, Changed):
  All = all r(R,C) positions
  Changed = [Cell for Cell in All if Grid2[R][C] = Color and Grid1[R][C] != Color]
  (Identical to cp_added_color; provided for semantic clarity.)

cp_changed_from(Grid1, Grid2, Color, Changed):
  All = all r(R,C) positions
  Changed = [Cell for Cell in All if Grid1[R][C] = Color and Grid2[R][C] != Color]
  (Identical to cp_removed_color; provided for semantic clarity.)

cp_diff_map(Grid1, Grid2, Map):
  Map[R][C] = 1 if Grid1[R][C] != Grid2[R][C], else 0

cp_similarity(Grid1, Grid2, EqCount-Total):
  Total = Rows * Cols
  EqCount = |{Cell: Grid1[R][C] = Grid2[R][C]}|

cp_region_diff(Region1, Region2, Diff):
  Diff = Region1 \ Region2  (set difference)

cp_region_intersect(Region1, Region2, Inter):
  Inter = Region1 ∩ Region2

cp_region_union(Region1, Region2, Union):
  Union = Region1 ∪ Region2 (no duplicates)

cp_region_equal(Region1, Region2):
  sort(Region1) = sort(Region2)

cp_grids_equal(Grid1, Grid2):
  Grid1 = Grid2  (structural unification)

cp_color_shift(Grid1, Grid2, Pairs):
  Diffs = cp_diff_cells(Grid1, Grid2)
  Pairs = [Grid1[R][C]-Grid2[R][C] for r(R,C) in Diffs]

END OF PART 68


PART 69: PSEUDOCODE - SPATIAL PACK (Work Package 79)

sp_direction(r(R1,C1), r(R2,C2), Dir):
  DR = R2 - R1, DC = C2 - C1
  If DR < 0, DC = 0: Dir = north
  If DR > 0, DC = 0: Dir = south
  If DR = 0, DC < 0: Dir = west
  If DR = 0, DC > 0: Dir = east
  If DR < 0, DC > 0: Dir = northeast
  If DR < 0, DC < 0: Dir = northwest
  If DR > 0, DC > 0: Dir = southeast
  If DR > 0, DC < 0: Dir = southwest
  If DR = 0, DC = 0: Dir = same

sp_distance_manhattan(r(R1,C1), r(R2,C2), D):
  D = |R2 - R1| + |C2 - C1|

sp_distance_chebyshev(r(R1,C1), r(R2,C2), D):
  D = max(|R2 - R1|, |C2 - C1|)

sp_neighbors4(r(R,C), Rows-Cols, Neighbors):
  Candidates = {r(R-1,C), r(R+1,C), r(R,C-1), r(R,C+1)}
  Neighbors = [c for c in Candidates if 0 =< c.R < Rows and 0 =< c.C < Cols]

sp_neighbors8(r(R,C), Rows-Cols, Neighbors):
  Candidates = all 8 cells differing by at most 1 in each axis (excluding self)
  Neighbors = [c for c in Candidates if in-bounds]

sp_adjacent4(Cell1, Cell2):
  sp_distance_manhattan(Cell1, Cell2) = 1

sp_adjacent8(Cell1, Cell2):
  sp_distance_chebyshev(Cell1, Cell2) = 1

sp_bbox_contains(bbox(R1,C1,R2,C2), r(R,C)):
  R1 =< R =< R2 and C1 =< C =< C2

sp_in_region(Cell, Region):
  member(Cell, Region) (deterministic, cut after first match)

sp_row_between(Region, MinR, MaxR, Filtered):
  Filtered = [r(R,C) for r(R,C) in Region if MinR =< R =< MaxR]

sp_col_between(Region, MinC, MaxC, Filtered):
  Filtered = [r(R,C) for r(R,C) in Region if MinC =< C =< MaxC]

sp_closest(Ref, Region, Closest):
  Dists = [manhattan(Ref, Cell) for Cell in Region]
  MinD = min(Dists)
  Closest = Region[first index where Dists[i] = MinD]

sp_farthest(Ref, Region, Farthest):
  Dists = [manhattan(Ref, Cell) for Cell in Region]
  MaxD = max(Dists)
  Farthest = Region[first index where Dists[i] = MaxD]

sp_centroid(Region, Row, Col):
  N = length(Region)
  Row = sum(R for r(R,_) in Region) // N
  Col = sum(C for r(_,C) in Region) // N

END OF PART 69


PART 70: PSEUDOCODE - INDUCTION PACK (Work Package 80)

id_color_map(Input, Output, Map):
  Changed = id_changed_cells(Input, Output)
  Pairs = [(Input[R][C], Output[R][C]) for r(R,C) in Changed]
  Map = sort(Pairs)  -- removes duplicates

id_is_recolor(Input, Output):
  Map = id_color_map(Input, Output)
  For all cells (R,C):
    InV = Input[R][C], OutV = Output[R][C]
    If InV in Map: OutV must equal Map[InV]
    Else: InV must equal OutV

id_uniform_output(Output, Color):
  Colors = sort(flatten(Output))
  Colors = [Color]  -- exactly one distinct value

id_output_color(Output, Color):
  id_uniform_output(Output, Color)

id_size_ratio(Input, Output, RR-RC):
  RR = OutRows / InRows (integer)
  RC = OutCols / InCols (integer)

id_is_scale(Input, Output):
  OutRows mod InRows = 0
  OutCols mod InCols = 0
  K = OutRows // InRows
  K > 0
  OutCols // InCols = K

id_scale_factor(Input, Output, K):
  id_is_scale(Input, Output)
  K = OutRows // InRows

id_changed_cells(Input, Output, Changed):
  All = all r(R,C) positions
  Changed = [Cell for Cell in All if Input[R][C] != Output[R][C]]

id_unchanged_cells(Input, Output, Unchanged):
  All = all r(R,C) positions
  Unchanged = [Cell for Cell in All if Input[R][C] = Output[R][C]]

id_input_colors(Input, Colors):
  Colors = sort(distinct_values(flatten(Input)))

id_output_colors(Output, Colors):
  Colors = sort(distinct_values(flatten(Output)))

id_new_colors(Input, Output, New):
  New = OutColors - InColors  (set difference)

id_lost_colors(Input, Output, Lost):
  Lost = InColors - OutColors  (set difference)

id_grid_dims(Grid, Rows, Cols):
  Rows = length(Grid)
  Cols = length(Grid[0])  if Rows > 0 else 0

END OF PART 70


PART 71: PSEUDOCODE - GRAVITY PACK (Work Package 81)

gv_col_values(Grid, C, Values):
  Values = [ Grid[R][C] for R in 0..len(Grid)-1 ]

gv_set_col(Grid, C, Values, Result):
  Result = [ replace(Row, C, V) for (Row, V) in zip(Grid, Values) ]

gv_compact_list_bottom(BG, List, Compacted):
  Bgs  = [ V for V in List if V == BG ]
  Vals = [ V for V in List if V != BG ]
  Compacted = Bgs ++ Vals

gv_compact_list_top(BG, List, Compacted):
  Vals = [ V for V in List if V != BG ]
  Bgs  = [ V for V in List if V == BG ]
  Compacted = Vals ++ Bgs

gv_compact_col(Grid, BG, Result):
  for each column C in Grid:
    ColVals = gv_col_values(Grid, C)
    Compacted = gv_compact_list_bottom(BG, ColVals)
    Grid = gv_set_col(Grid, C, Compacted)
  Result = Grid

gv_compact_row(Grid, BG, Result):
  Result = [ gv_compact_list_top(BG, Row) for Row in Grid ]

gv_fall_down(Grid, BG, Result):
  Result = gv_compact_col(Grid, BG)

gv_fall_up(Grid, BG, Result):
  for each column C in Grid:
    ColVals = gv_col_values(Grid, C)
    Compacted = gv_compact_list_top(BG, ColVals)
    Grid = gv_set_col(Grid, C, Compacted)
  Result = Grid

gv_fall_left(Grid, BG, Result):
  Result = [ gv_compact_list_top(BG, Row) for Row in Grid ]

gv_fall_right(Grid, BG, Result):
  Result = [ gv_compact_list_bottom(BG, Row) for Row in Grid ]

gv_settle_col_vals(Color, BG, List, Settled):
  Colors = [ V for V in List if V == Color ]
  Others = [ V for V in List if V != Color and V != BG ]
  Bgs    = [ V for V in List if V == BG ]
  Settled = Others ++ Bgs ++ Colors

gv_settle_color(Grid, Color, BG, Result):
  for each column C in Grid:
    ColVals = gv_col_values(Grid, C)
    Settled = gv_settle_col_vals(Color, BG, ColVals)
    Grid = gv_set_col(Grid, C, Settled)
  Result = Grid

gv_float_col_vals(Color, BG, List, Floated):
  Colors = [ V for V in List if V == Color ]
  Others = [ V for V in List if V != Color and V != BG ]
  Bgs    = [ V for V in List if V == BG ]
  Floated = Colors ++ Others ++ Bgs

gv_float_color(Grid, Color, BG, Result):
  for each column C in Grid:
    ColVals = gv_col_values(Grid, C)
    Floated = gv_float_col_vals(Color, BG, ColVals)
    Grid = gv_set_col(Grid, C, Floated)
  Result = Grid

gv_stack_down = gv_settle_color
gv_stack_up   = gv_float_color

gv_apply_col(Grid, BG, Pred, Result):
  for each column C in Grid:
    ColVals = gv_col_values(Grid, C)
    NewVals = Pred(BG, ColVals)
    Grid = gv_set_col(Grid, C, NewVals)
  Result = Grid

gv_apply_row(Grid, BG, Pred, Result):
  Result = [ Pred(BG, Row) for Row in Grid ]

END OF PART 71


PART 72: PSEUDOCODE - NOISE PACK (Work Package 82)

ns_mask_apply(Grid, Mask, FillColor, Result):
  Result = [ [ FillColor if M=1 else G for (G,M) in zip(GRow,MRow) ]
             for (GRow,MRow) in zip(Grid,Mask) ]

ns_mask_invert(Mask, _Rows, Inverted):
  Inverted = [ [ 1-B for B in Row ] for Row in Mask ]

ns_mask_and(Mask1, Mask2, Result):
  Result = [ [ A AND B for (A,B) in zip(R1,R2) ]
             for (R1,R2) in zip(Mask1,Mask2) ]

ns_mask_or(Mask1, Mask2, Result):
  Result = [ [ A OR B for (A,B) in zip(R1,R2) ]
             for (R1,R2) in zip(Mask1,Mask2) ]

ns_mask_from_color(Grid, Color, Mask):
  Mask = [ [ 1 if V=Color else 0 for V in Row ] for Row in Grid ]

ns_mask_to_region(Mask, Region):
  Region = [ r(R,C) for R,C in dims(Mask) if Mask[R][C] = 1 ]

ns_region_to_mask(Region, Rows, Cols, Mask):
  Mask = all-zero grid of Rows x Cols
  for r(R,C) in Region: Mask[R][C] = 1

ns_color_count(Grid, Color, Count):
  Count = len([ V for V in flat(Grid) if V = Color ])

ns_majority_color(Grid, Color):
  Colors = sort(flat(Grid))
  Counts = [ (count(C, Grid), C) for C in Colors ]
  Color = color with maximum count

ns_noise_cells(Grid, _BG, Cells):
  Maj = majority_color(Grid)
  Cells = [ r(R,C) for r(R,C) in all_positions(Grid) if Grid[R][C] != Maj ]

ns_denoise(Grid, _BG, Result):
  Maj = majority_color(Grid)
  Result = [ [ Maj if V != Maj else V for V in Row ] for Row in Grid ]

ns_sparse_cells(Grid, N, Cells):
  Cells = [ r(R,C) for r(R,C) in all_positions(Grid)
            if color_count(Grid, Grid[R][C]) < N ]

ns_dense_cells(Grid, N, Cells):
  Cells = [ r(R,C) for r(R,C) in all_positions(Grid)
            if color_count(Grid, Grid[R][C]) >= N ]

ns_isolate_color(Grid, Color, Result):
  Result = [ [ V if V=Color else 0 for V in Row ] for Row in Grid ]

END OF PART 72


PART 73: PSEUDOCODE - GENERATE PACK (Work Package 83)

ge_uniform(Rows, Cols, Color, Grid):
  Row = [Color] * Cols
  Grid = [Row] * Rows

ge_gradient_h(Rows, Cols, NColors, Grid):
  GradRow = [ C mod NColors for C in 0..Cols-1 ]
  Grid = [GradRow] * Rows

ge_gradient_v(Rows, Cols, NColors, Grid):
  Grid = [ [R mod NColors] * Cols for R in 0..Rows-1 ]

ge_checkerboard(Rows, Cols, C0, C1, Grid):
  Grid[R][C] = C0 if (R+C) mod 2 = 0 else C1

ge_stripes_h(Rows, Cols, Colors, Grid):
  NC = length(Colors)
  Grid[R] = [Colors[R mod NC]] * Cols

ge_stripes_v(Rows, Cols, Colors, Grid):
  NC = length(Colors)
  StripeRow = [ Colors[C mod NC] for C in 0..Cols-1 ]
  Grid = [StripeRow] * Rows

ge_border_rect(Rows, Cols, BorderColor, FillColor, Grid):
  Grid[R][C] = BorderColor if R=0 or R=Rows-1 or C=0 or C=Cols-1
               else FillColor

ge_diagonal(Rows, Cols, DiagColor, Grid):
  Grid[R][C] = DiagColor if R=C else 0

ge_antidiagonal(Rows, Cols, DiagColor, Grid):
  Grid[R][C] = DiagColor if R+C = Cols-1 else 0

ge_frame(Rows, Cols, FrameColor, BG, Grid):
  Grid[R][C] = FrameColor if R=0 or R=Rows-1 or C=0 or C=Cols-1
               else BG

ge_cross(Rows, Cols, CrossColor, BG, Grid):
  MidR = Rows // 2, MidC = Cols // 2
  Grid[R][C] = CrossColor if R=MidR or C=MidC else BG

ge_identity_grid(N, One, Grid):
  Grid = ge_diagonal(N, N, One)

ge_from_map(Rows-Cols, Map, Grid):
  Grid = ge_uniform(Rows, Cols, 0)
  for r(R,C)-Color in Map: Grid[R][C] = Color

ge_repeat_pattern(Pattern, Rows, Cols, Grid):
  PRows = length(Pattern), PCols = length(Pattern[0])
  Grid[R][C] = Pattern[R mod PRows][C mod PCols]

END OF PART 73


PART 74: PSEUDOCODE - LOOKUP PACK (Work Package 84)

lk_get(Key, [Key-Value|_], Value) :- !
lk_get(Key, [_|Rest], Value) :- lk_get(Key, Rest, Value)

lk_put(Key, Value, [], [Key-Value])
lk_put(Key, Value, [Key-_|Rest], [Key-Value|Rest]) :- !
lk_put(Key, Value, [Other|Rest], [Other|Rest2]) :- lk_put(Key, Value, Rest, Rest2)

lk_keys(Map, Keys) :- maplist(key_of, Map, Keys)
lk_values(Map, Values) :- maplist(val_of, Map, Values)

lk_has_key(Key, Map) :- member(Key-_, Map), !

lk_delete(_, [], [])
lk_delete(Key, [Key-_|Rest], Rest) :- !
lk_delete(Key, [Other|Rest], [Other|Rest2]) :- lk_delete(Key, Rest, Rest2)

lk_map_values(Map, Pred, NewMap) :- maplist(apply_val(Pred), Map, NewMap)
  where apply_val(Pred, K-V, K-NV) :- call(Pred, V, NV)

lk_from_pairs(Pairs, Pairs)

lk_grid_row(Grid, R, Row) :- nth0(R, Grid, Row)
lk_grid_col(Grid, C, Col) :- maplist(nth0(C), Grid, Col)
lk_grid_cell(Grid, R, C, V) :- nth0(R, Grid, Row), nth0(C, Row, V)

lk_color_positions(Grid, BG, Map):
  collect Color-r(R,C) for all R,C where Grid[R][C] != BG
  group by Color -> Map = [Color-[r(R,C)...] ...]

lk_position_color(Grid, BG, Map):
  Map = [ r(R,C)-Color | for all R,C where Grid[R][C] != BG ]

lk_invert(Map, Inverted) :- maplist(swap_pair, Map, Inverted)
  where swap_pair(K-V, V-K)

END OF PART 74


PART 75: PSEUDOCODE - CONNECT PACK (Work Package 85)

cc_dfs(stack, grid, rows, cols, color, nf, seen):
  if stack empty: return seen
  cell = stack[0], rest = stack[1:]
  if cell in seen: return cc_dfs(rest, ...)
  if cell in bounds and grid[cell] == color:
    neighbors = nf(cell)
    return cc_dfs(neighbors ++ rest, ..., seen + [cell])
  else: return cc_dfs(rest, ...)

cc_flood4(grid, seed, color):
  if seed in bounds and grid[seed] == color:
    return cc_dfs([seed], grid, color, neighbors4, [])
  else: return []

cc_flood8(grid, seed, color):
  if seed in bounds and grid[seed] == color:
    return cc_dfs([seed], grid, color, neighbors8, [])
  else: return []

cc_components4(grid, color):
  all_cells = [r(R,C) for R,C where grid[R][C] == color]
  while all_cells not empty:
    seed = all_cells[0]
    comp = cc_flood4(grid, seed, color)
    yield comp
    all_cells = all_cells - comp

cc_components8(grid, color): same with cc_flood8

cc_count4(grid, color) = length(cc_components4(grid, color))
cc_count8(grid, color) = length(cc_components8(grid, color))

cc_sizes4(grid, color) = msort([length(c) for c in cc_components4(grid, color)])
cc_sizes8(grid, color) = msort([length(c) for c in cc_components8(grid, color)])

cc_largest4(grid, color) = argmax(length, cc_components4(grid, color))
cc_largest8(grid, color) = argmax(length, cc_components8(grid, color))
cc_smallest4(grid, color) = argmin(length, cc_components4(grid, color))

cc_border_cells(grid, region):
  return [r(R,C) in region |
          exists neighbor n of r(R,C) s.t. n out-of-bounds or n not in region]

cc_interior_cells(grid, region):
  return [r(R,C) in region |
          all 4 neighbors of r(R,C) are in-bounds AND in region]

cc_enclosed(grid, bg):
  bg_cells = [r(R,C) | grid[R][C] == bg]
  border_bg = [r(R,C) in bg_cells | R==0 or R==Rows-1 or C==0 or C==Cols-1]
  reachable = cc_multi_dfs(border_bg, grid, bg)  -- flood from all border seeds
  return bg_cells - reachable

END OF PART 75


PART 76: PSEUDOCODE - MORPH PACK (Work Package 86)

mo_dilate4(Grid, Color, BG):
  for each (R, C) in Grid:
    if Grid[R][C] == Color: Out[R][C] = Color
    elif Grid[R][C] == BG and any 4-neighbor has Color: Out[R][C] = Color
    else: Out[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

mo_dilate8(Grid, Color, BG): same with 8-neighbors

mo_erode4(Grid, Color, BG):
  for each (R, C) in Grid:
    if Grid[R][C] == Color:
      if all in-bounds 4-neighbors have Color: Out[R][C] = Color
      else: Out[R][C] = BG  (OOB counts as not-Color)
    else: Out[R][C] = Grid[R][C]

mo_erode8(Grid, Color, BG): same with 8-neighbors

mo_dilate4_n(Grid, Color, BG, N) = repeat mo_dilate4 N times
mo_erode4_n(Grid, Color, BG, N) = repeat mo_erode4 N times

mo_open4(Grid, Color, BG) = mo_dilate4(mo_erode4(Grid, Color, BG), Color, BG)
mo_close4(Grid, Color, BG) = mo_erode4(mo_dilate4(Grid, Color, BG), Color, BG)

mo_boundary4(Grid, Color) =
  [r(R,C) | Grid[R][C]==Color and NOT all 4 in-bounds neighbors have Color]

mo_boundary8(Grid, Color) =
  [r(R,C) | Grid[R][C]==Color and NOT all 8 in-bounds neighbors have Color]

mo_ring4(Grid, Color, BG) =
  [r(R,C) | Grid[R][C]==BG and any 4-neighbor has Color]

mo_fill_holes4(Grid, Color, BG):
  border_bg = BG cells on the grid edge
  reachable = flood4(border_bg, BG)  -- BG cells reachable from border
  holes = all BG cells not in reachable
  return Grid with holes set to Color

mo_pad(Grid, PadColor):
  new_row = [PadColor] * (Cols+2)
  return [new_row] + [[PadColor] + Row + [PadColor] for Row in Grid] + [new_row]

mo_unpad(Grid):
  return [Row[1:-1] for Row in Grid[1:-1]]

END OF PART 76


PART 77 - REWRITE PACK PSEUDOCODE

rw_map_color(Grid, Map, Grid2):
  Grid2 = [[map_cell(Map, V) for V in Row] for Row in Grid]
  map_cell(Map, V): if V-V2 in Map return V2 else return V

rw_replace_color(Grid, Old, New, Grid2):
  rw_map_color(Grid, [Old-New], Grid2)

rw_swap_colors(Grid, A, B, Grid2):
  Grid2 = [[swap(A,B,V) for V in Row] for Row in Grid]
  swap(A,B,V): if V==A return B; if V==B return A; else return V

rw_set_region(Grid, Region, Color, Grid2):
  Diff = [r(R,C)-Color for r(R,C) in Region]
  rw_diff_apply(Grid, Diff, Grid2)

rw_mask_apply(Grid, Mask, MaskVal, Fill, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = Fill if Mask[R][C]==MaskVal else Grid[R][C]

rw_overlay(Grid1, Grid2, BG, Grid3):
  Grid3[R][C] = Grid2[R][C] if Grid2[R][C] != BG else Grid1[R][C]

rw_stamp(Grid, Patch, OffR, OffC, Grid2):
  Diff = [r(PR+OffR, PC+OffC)-V for (PR,PC,V) in Patch cells]
  rw_diff_apply(Grid, Diff, Grid2)

rw_diff_apply(Grid, Diff, Grid2):
  for each (RI, CI) in Grid:
    if r(RI,CI)-NewVal in Diff: Grid2[RI][CI] = NewVal
    else: Grid2[RI][CI] = Grid[RI][CI]

rw_normalize(Grid, BG, Grid2):
  Colors = distinct non-BG values in row-major order of first appearance
  Map = [(Colors[i], i+1) for i in 0..len(Colors)-1]
  rw_map_color(Grid, Map, Grid2)

rw_invert_colors(Grid, Max, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = Max - Grid[R][C]

rw_remap_bg(Grid, OldBG, NewBG, Grid2):
  rw_replace_color(Grid, OldBG, NewBG, Grid2)

rw_set_border(Grid, Color, Grid2):
  Border = {r(R,C) : R==0 or R==Rows-1 or C==0 or C==Cols-1}
  rw_set_region(Grid, Border, Color, Grid2)

rw_fill_rect(Grid, R1, C1, R2, C2, Color, Grid2):
  Region = [r(R,C) for R in R1..R2, C in C1..C2]
  rw_set_region(Grid, Region, Color, Grid2)

rw_conditional(Grid, Goal, ColorTrue, ColorFalse, Grid2):
  Grid2[R][C] = ColorTrue if Goal(R,C,Grid[R][C]) else ColorFalse

END OF PART 77


PART 78 - RUN PACK PSEUDOCODE

rn_encode(List, Runs):
  if List is empty: Runs = []
  else V = List[0]; (N, Tail) = take_same(V, List[1:])
       Runs = [(V, N+1)] + rn_encode(Tail)

rn_decode(Runs, List):
  List = flatten([[V]*N for (V,N) in Runs])

rn_row_encode(Grid, R, Runs):
  rn_encode(Grid[R], Runs)

rn_col_encode(Grid, C, Runs):
  rn_encode([row[C] for row in Grid], Runs)

rn_grid_rows(Grid, RowRuns):
  RowRuns = [rn_encode(row) for row in Grid]

rn_grid_cols(Grid, ColRuns):
  ColRuns = [rn_col_encode(Grid, C) for C in 0..Cols-1]

rn_length(Runs, N):
  N = sum(count for (value, count) in Runs)

rn_at(Runs, I, V):
  for (Val, Count) in Runs:
    if I < Count: return Val
    else: I -= Count

rn_max_run(Runs, Color, MaxLen):
  MaxLen = max([N for (V,N) in Runs if V==Color], default=0)

rn_count_runs(Runs, Color, N):
  N = len([R for (V,_) in Runs if V==Color])

rn_uniform(Runs):
  all values in Runs are the same

rn_trim(List, BG, Trimmed):
  strip BG from front; reverse; strip BG from front; reverse

rn_repeat(Runs, N, Runs2):
  AllRuns = Runs * N (concatenated)
  Runs2 = merge_adjacent_same_value(AllRuns)

rn_positions(Runs, Color, Positions):
  offset = 0
  Positions = []
  for (V, N) in Runs:
    if V == Color: append offset..offset+N-1 to Positions
    offset += N

END OF PART 78


PART 79 - ARITH PACK PSEUDOCODE

Work Package 89 - Layer 68 - Prefix: ar_

The arith pack provides cell-wise arithmetic on list-of-lists grids.

ar_cell_add(Grid1, Grid2, Grid3):
  FOR each row pair (Row1, Row2) from Grid1 and Grid2 in parallel:
    FOR each cell pair (V1, V2) from Row1 and Row2 in parallel:
      output V1 + V2

ar_cell_sub(Grid1, Grid2, Grid3):
  FOR each row pair (Row1, Row2) from Grid1 and Grid2 in parallel:
    FOR each cell pair (V1, V2):
      output V1 - V2

ar_cell_mul(Grid1, Grid2, Grid3):
  FOR each row pair (Row1, Row2) from Grid1 and Grid2 in parallel:
    FOR each cell pair (V1, V2):
      output V1 * V2

ar_cell_mod(Grid, N, Grid2):
  FOR each cell V in Grid:
    output V mod N

ar_scalar_add(Grid, N, Grid2):
  FOR each cell V in Grid:
    output V + N

ar_scalar_mul(Grid, N, Grid2):
  FOR each cell V in Grid:
    output V * N

ar_row_sum(Grid, R, Sum):
  Row <- Grid[R]
  Sum <- sum of all values in Row

ar_col_sum(Grid, C, Sum):
  Col <- [Grid[R][C] for each row R]
  Sum <- sum of all values in Col

ar_row_sums(Grid, Sums):
  FOR each row Row in Grid:
    append sum(Row) to Sums

ar_col_sums(Grid, Sums):
  Cols <- number of columns from first row
  FOR C from 0 to Cols-1:
    append ar_col_sum(Grid, C) to Sums

ar_cell_max(Grid, Max):
  Flat <- flatten Grid to one list
  Max <- maximum value in Flat

ar_cell_min(Grid, Min):
  Flat <- flatten Grid to one list
  Min <- minimum value in Flat

ar_cell_clamp(Grid, Lo, Hi, Grid2):
  FOR each cell V in Grid:
    IF V < Lo: output Lo
    ELSE IF V > Hi: output Hi
    ELSE: output V

ar_cell_abs_diff(Grid1, Grid2, Grid3):
  FOR each row pair (Row1, Row2) from Grid1 and Grid2 in parallel:
    FOR each cell pair (V1, V2):
      output |V1 - V2|

END OF PART 79


PART 80 - OBJ PACK PSEUDOCODE

Work Package 90 - Layer 69 - Prefix: obj_

An object is represented as obj(Color, SortedCells).

obj_from_cells(Color, Cells, Obj):
  SortedCells <- msort(Cells)
  Obj = obj(Color, SortedCells)

obj_color(obj(Color, _), Color): direct pattern match.

obj_cells(obj(_, Cells), Cells): direct pattern match.

obj_size(Obj, N):
  N <- length of Obj's cell list

obj_bbox(Obj, MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC):
  Rs <- [R for r(R,_) in Cells]
  Cs <- [C for r(_,C) in Cells]
  MinR, MaxR <- min/max of Rs
  MinC, MaxC <- min/max of Cs

obj_center(Obj, CR, CC):
  Rs <- [R for r(R,_) in Cells]
  Cs <- [C for r(_,C) in Cells]
  CR <- floor(sum(Rs) / length(Cells))
  CC <- floor(sum(Cs) / length(Cells))

obj_shape(Obj, Shape):
  (MinR, MinC) <- top-left of bounding box
  Shape <- [r(R-MinR, C-MinC) for r(R,C) in Cells]

obj_inventory(Grid, Color, Objects):
  Components <- cc_components4(Grid, Color)
  Objects <- [obj(Color, sort(Cells)) for Cells in Components]

obj_all(Grid, Objects):
  AllVals <- findall(V, cell V in Grid)
  Colors <- sort(AllVals) minus [0]
  Objects <- concat [obj_inventory(Grid, C) for C in Colors]

obj_count(Grid, Color, N):
  N <- length of obj_inventory(Grid, Color)

obj_largest(Grid, Color, Obj):
  Objects <- obj_inventory(Grid, Color)
  MaxSize <- max size of any object in Objects
  Obj <- first object with size = MaxSize

obj_smallest(Grid, Color, Obj):
  Objects <- obj_inventory(Grid, Color)
  MinSize <- min size of any object in Objects
  Obj <- first object with size = MinSize

obj_at_cell(Objects, Cell, Obj):
  Obj <- first object in Objects such that Cell in Obj's cells

obj_sort_size(Objects, Order, Sorted):
  Keyed <- [(size(Obj), Obj) for Obj in Objects]
  Keyed <- msort(Keyed)
  Sorted <- [Obj for (_, Obj) in Keyed]
  IF Order = desc: Sorted <- reverse(Sorted)

END OF PART 80


PART 81 - PIPELINE PACK PSEUDOCODE

Work Package 91 - Layer 70 - Prefix: pl_

pl_register(Name, Goal):
  retractall pl_handler_(Name, _)
  assertz pl_handler_(Name, Goal)

pl_registered(Name, Goal):
  lookup pl_handler_(Name, Goal)

pl_unregister(Name):
  retractall pl_handler_(Name, _)

pl_step(StepTerm, In, Out, Registry):
  Name <- functor of StepTerm (or StepTerm if atom)
  IF Name-Goal in Registry: call Goal(StepTerm, In, Out)
  ELSE IF pl_handler_(Name, Goal): call Goal(StepTerm, In, Out)
  ELSE: Out = In (passthrough)

pl_run(Steps, Input, Output):
  foldl pl_step_handler_ over Steps with initial value Input

pl_map(Goal, List, Results):
  maplist(Goal, List, Results)

pl_filter(Goal, List, Kept):
  Kept <- findall(H, member(H, List) and Goal(H))

pl_fold(Goal, List, Acc0, AccN):
  foldl(Goal, List, Acc0, AccN)

pl_zip(List1, List2, Pairs):
  FOR each pair (L, R) in zip(List1, List2):
    append L-R to Pairs

pl_unzip(Pairs, List1, List2):
  FOR each pair L-R in Pairs:
    append L to List1, R to List2

pl_take(N, List, Taken):
  IF N = 0 OR List = []: Taken = []
  ELSE: Taken = [head(List)] + take(N-1, tail(List))

pl_drop(N, List, Rest):
  IF N = 0: Rest = List
  ELSE IF List = []: Rest = []
  ELSE: drop(N-1, tail(List), Rest)

pl_partition(Goal, List, Sat, Rej):
  Sat <- findall(H, member(H, List) and Goal(H))
  Rej <- findall(H, member(H, List) and not Goal(H))

END OF PART 81


PART 82 - CONTEXT PACK PSEUDOCODE

Work Package 92 - Layer 71 - Prefix: ctx_

A context map is a list [K1-V1, K2-V2, ...] with unique keys.

ctx_put(Map, Key, Value, Map2):
  Map2 = [Key-Value | ctx_delete(Map, Key)]

ctx_get([K-V|_], K, V): key matches head.
ctx_get([_|Rest], Key, V): recurse on tail.

ctx_has(Map, Key): ctx_get(Map, Key, _) succeeds.

ctx_delete([], _, []).
ctx_delete([K-V|Rest], Key, Map2):
  IF K == Key: Map2 = ctx_delete(Rest, Key)
  ELSE: Map2 = [K-V | ctx_delete(Rest, Key)]

ctx_keys(Map, Keys): extract left of each K-V pair.
ctx_values(Map, Values): extract right of each K-V pair.

ctx_from_pairs(Pairs, Map):
  fold ctx_put over Pairs into an empty map; last wins.

ctx_to_pairs(Map, Map): identity.

ctx_merge(Map1, Map2, Merged):
  fold ctx_put(Map2 entries) over Map1.

ctx_dispatch(Map, Key, Default, Args):
  IF ctx_get(Map, Key, Goal): call Goal(Args)
  ELSE: call Default(Args)

ctx_select(_, [], Default, Default).
ctx_select(Map, [K|Rest], Default, Value):
  IF ctx_get(Map, K, V): Value = V
  ELSE: ctx_select(Map, Rest, Default, Value)

ctx_map_values(Map, Goal, Map2):
  FOR each K-V in Map: Map2 gets K-Goal(V).

ctx_filter_keys(Map, Goal, Map2):
  Map2 = findall(K-V, member(K-V, Map) and Goal(K))

ctx_size(Map, N): N = length(Map)

END OF PART 82


PART 83 - SCORE PACK PSEUDOCODE

What changed: Added pseudocode for the 14 sc_* predicates in the score pack.

Why: Pseudocode documents the reasoning behind each predicate for future
maintenance and for learners reading the SPARC volumes.

sc_exact(Grid, Grid).
  % Structural unification suffices.

sc_cell_match(Grid1, Grid2, N):
  Flat1 = append(Grid1)
  Flat2 = append(Grid2)
  N = sc_count_matches_(Flat1, Flat2)

sc_count_matches_([], [], 0).
sc_count_matches_([H1|T1], [H2|T2], N):
  Rest = sc_count_matches_(T1, T2)
  IF H1 == H2: N = Rest + 1
  ELSE: N = Rest

sc_cell_total(Grid, N):
  Rows = length(Grid)
  Cols = length(Grid[0])
  N = Rows * Cols

sc_accuracy(Grid1, Grid2, Acc):
  Match = sc_cell_match(Grid1, Grid2)
  Total = sc_cell_total(Grid1)
  IF Total > 0: Acc = float(Match) / float(Total)
  ELSE: Acc = 1.0

sc_color_recall(Produced, Expected, Color, Recall):
  ExpFlat = append(Expected)
  ProdFlat = append(Produced)
  ExpCount = count occurrences of Color in ExpFlat
  TP = count positions where both ProdFlat[i] == Color and ExpFlat[i] == Color
  IF ExpCount > 0: Recall = TP / ExpCount
  ELSE: Recall = 1.0

sc_color_precision(Produced, Expected, Color, Precision):
  ProdFlat = append(Produced)
  ExpFlat = append(Expected)
  ProdCount = count occurrences of Color in ProdFlat
  TP = count positions where both ProdFlat[i] == Color and ExpFlat[i] == Color
  IF ProdCount > 0: Precision = TP / ProdCount
  ELSE: Precision = 1.0

sc_color_f1(Produced, Expected, Color, F1):
  P = sc_color_precision(Produced, Expected, Color)
  R = sc_color_recall(Produced, Expected, Color)
  IF P + R > 0: F1 = 2 * P * R / (P + R)
  ELSE: F1 = 0.0

sc_pair_score(Input-Expected, Goal, Acc):
  Actual = call Goal(Input)
  Acc = sc_accuracy(Actual, Expected)

sc_pairs_score(Pairs, Goal, MeanAcc):
  Accs = map sc_pair_score(Goal) over Pairs
  MeanAcc = sum(Accs) / length(Accs)

sc_perfect(Input, Expected, Goal):
  Actual = call Goal(Input)
  sc_exact(Actual, Expected)

sc_pairs_perfect(Pairs, Goal):
  forall member(In-Ex, Pairs): sc_perfect(In, Ex, Goal)

sc_rank(Candidates, Expected, Ranked):
  Scored = map (Grid -> sc_accuracy(Grid, Expected) - Grid) over Candidates
  Ascending = msort(Scored)
  Ranked = reverse(Ascending)

sc_best(Candidates, Expected, Best):
  Ranked = sc_rank(Candidates, Expected)
  Best = head(Ranked).Grid

sc_threshold(Candidates, Expected, MinAcc, Filtered):
  Filtered = findall(Grid, member(Grid, Candidates) and
                     sc_accuracy(Grid, Expected) >= MinAcc)

END OF PART 83


PART 84 - INDUCT PACK PSEUDOCODE

What changed: Added pseudocode for the 14 in_* predicates in the induct pack.

Why: Pseudocode documents the reasoning behind each predicate.

in_delta(Input, Output, Delta):
  Delta = findall(r(R,C)-Old-New,
    nth0(R, Input, Row), nth0(C, Row, Old),
    nth0(R, Output, ORow), nth0(C, ORow, New),
    Old != New)

in_constant(Grid, Grid).

in_color_map(Input, Output, Map):
  RawPairs = findall(Old-New, cell differs)
  Pairs = sort(RawPairs)
  check_consistent: no Old maps to two different New
  Map = Pairs

in_color_map_pairs([], []).
in_color_map_pairs([In-Out|Rest], Map):
  FirstMap = in_color_map(In, Out)
  Map = foldl(intersect, Rest, FirstMap)

in_size_change(Input, Output, DRows, DCols):
  DRows = length(Output) - length(Input)
  DCols = length(Output[0]) - length(Input[0])

in_size_change_pairs([In-Out|Rest], DRows, DCols):
  DRows, DCols = in_size_change(In, Out)
  forall pairs: in_size_change(In2, Out2, DRows, DCols)

in_color_palette(Input, Output, Palette):
  Palette = sort(flat(Input) ++ flat(Output))

in_palette_pairs(Pairs, InColors, OutColors):
  InColors = sort(all values from all input grids)
  OutColors = sort(all values from all output grids)

in_invariant_cells(Input, Output, Cells):
  Cells = findall(r(R,C), cell(R,C,Input) == cell(R,C,Output))

in_changed_cells(Input, Output, Cells):
  Cells = findall(r(R,C), cell(R,C,Input) != cell(R,C,Output))

in_consistent_delta([In-Out|Rest], Delta):
  Delta = in_delta(In, Out)
  forall pairs: in_delta(In2, Out2, Delta)

in_bg_color(Grid, BgColor):
  Counted = [(count(V), V) | V in flatten(Grid)]
  BgColor = argmax(Counted)

in_bg_color_pairs([In-_|Rest], BgColor):
  BgColor = in_bg_color(In)
  forall pairs: in_bg_color(In2) == BgColor

in_common_keys(Map1, Map2, Common):
  Common = intersection(Map1, Map2)

END OF PART 84


PART 85 - HYP PACK PSEUDOCODE

What changed: Added pseudocode for the 14 hy_* predicates in the hyp pack.

Why: Pseudocode documents the reasoning behind each predicate.

hy_color_sub(Map, Grid, Grid2):
  Grid2 = maplist over rows: maplist over cells: lookup(Map, Cell)
  lookup(Map, Color) = New IF member(Color-New, Map) ELSE Color

hy_identity(Grid, Grid).

hy_from_map(Map, Grid, Grid2):
  hy_color_sub(Map, Grid, Grid2)  % alias

hy_test(Goal, Input, Expected, Acc):
  Actual = call Goal(Input)
  Match = count cells where Actual and Expected agree
  Total = Rows * Cols
  IF Total > 0: Acc = float(Match) / float(Total) ELSE Acc = 1.0

hy_test_all(Goal, Pairs, MeanAcc, Accs):
  Accs = map hy_test(Goal) over Pairs
  MeanAcc = sum(Accs) / length(Accs)

hy_verify(Goal, Input, Expected):
  Actual = call Goal(Input)
  Actual = Expected

hy_verify_all(Goal, Pairs):
  forall member(In-Ex, Pairs): hy_verify(Goal, In, Ex)

hy_select(Goals, Pairs, Best):
  Ranked = hy_rank(Goals, Pairs)
  Best = head(Ranked).Goal

hy_rank(Goals, Pairs, Ranked):
  Scored = [(hy_test_all(G, Pairs).MeanAcc - G) | G in Goals]
  Ranked = reverse(msort(Scored))

hy_apply_map(Map, Grid, Grid2):
  hy_color_sub(Map, Grid, Grid2)  % alias

hy_compose(Map1, Map2, Grid, Grid2):
  Int = hy_color_sub(Map1, Grid)
  Grid2 = hy_color_sub(Map2, Int)

hy_invert_map(Map, Inverted):
  Inverted = [(New-Old) | (Old-New) in Map]

hy_map_lookup(Map, Color, New):
  IF member(Color-New, Map): return New
  ELSE: New = Color

hy_describe(hy_identity, identity).
hy_describe(hy_color_sub(Map, _), "color_sub(Map)").
hy_describe(Goal, atom(Goal)).

END OF PART 85


PART 86 - SYM PACK PSEUDOCODE

What changed: Added pseudocode for the 14 sy_* predicates in the sym pack.

sy_reflect_h(Grid, Grid2): maplist(reverse, Grid, Grid2)

sy_reflect_v(Grid, Grid2): reverse(Grid, Grid2)

sy_transpose(Grid, Grid2):
  Cols = length(Grid[0])
  Grid2 = [extract_col(Grid, j) | j in 0..Cols-1]

sy_rotate90(Grid, Grid2):
  T = sy_transpose(Grid)
  Grid2 = sy_reflect_h(T)

sy_rotate180(Grid, Grid2):
  V = sy_reflect_v(Grid)
  Grid2 = sy_reflect_h(V)

sy_rotate270(Grid, Grid2):
  H = sy_reflect_h(Grid)
  Grid2 = sy_transpose(H)

sy_has_h_symm(Grid): sy_reflect_h(Grid) == Grid
sy_has_v_symm(Grid): sy_reflect_v(Grid) == Grid
sy_has_rot2_symm(Grid): sy_rotate180(Grid) == Grid
sy_has_rot4_symm(Grid): sy_rotate90(Grid) == Grid

sy_symmetries(Grid, Symms):
  Symms = findall(S, has_symmetry(Grid, S))

sy_make_h_symm(Grid, Grid2):
  Grid2 = maplist(symm_row, Grid)
  symm_row(Row):
    N = length(Row), Half = N // 2
    Left = Row[0..Half-1]
    IF N odd: Row2 = Left ++ [Row[Half]] ++ reverse(Left)
    ELSE: Row2 = Left ++ reverse(Left)

sy_make_v_symm(Grid, Grid2):
  N = length(Grid), Half = N // 2
  Top = Grid[0..Half-1]
  IF N odd: Grid2 = Top ++ [Grid[Half]] ++ reverse(Top)
  ELSE: Grid2 = Top ++ reverse(Top)

sy_d4_orbit(Grid, Orbit):
  R90 = sy_rotate90(Grid)
  R180 = sy_rotate180(Grid)
  R270 = sy_rotate270(Grid)
  RH = sy_reflect_h(Grid)
  RV = sy_reflect_v(Grid)
  T = sy_transpose(Grid)
  RA = sy_reflect_v(R90)  % anti-diagonal
  Orbit = sort({Grid, R90, R180, R270, RH, RV, T, RA})

END OF PART 86


PART 87 - SEEK PACK PSEUDOCODE

sk_positions(Grid, Val, Cells):
  Cells = findall(R-C | Grid[R][C] = Val)

sk_rows_with(Grid, Val, RowIdxs):
  RowIdxs = findall(R | Val in Grid[R])

sk_cols_with(Grid, Val, ColIdxs):
  CIdxs = 0..NCols-1
  ColIdxs = filter(CIdxs, C -> exists row in Grid: Grid[row][C] = Val)

sk_border_cells(Grid, Cells):
  Cells = findall(R-C | R in 0..NRows-1, C in 0..NCols-1,
                          R=0 or R=NRows-1 or C=0 or C=NCols-1)

sk_interior_cells(Grid, Cells):
  if NRows <= 2 or NCols <= 2: return []
  Cells = findall(R-C | R in 1..NRows-2, C in 1..NCols-2)

sk_fits(Grid, Sub, R0, C0):
  forall DR in 0..NSubRows-1, DC in 0..NSubCols-1:
    Grid[R0+DR][C0+DC] = Sub[DR][DC]

sk_find_sub(Grid, Sub, R0, C0):
  R0 in 0..NRows-NSubRows
  C0 in 0..NCols-NSubCols
  sk_fits(Grid, Sub, R0, C0)

sk_all_subs(Grid, Sub, Cells):
  Cells = findall(R0-C0 | sk_find_sub(Grid, Sub, R0, C0))

dn_count_sub(Grid, Sub, N):
  Cells = sk_all_subs(Grid, Sub)
  N = length(Cells)

sk_match_count(Grid, Sub, R0, C0, N):
  N = |{(DR,DC) | Grid[R0+DR][C0+DC] = Sub[DR][DC]}|

sk_best_fit(Grid, Sub, R0, C0):
  Scored = [(sk_match_count(Grid, Sub, R, C), R, C) | valid R, C]
  (R0, C0) = argmax(Scored)

sk_find_d4(Grid1, Grid2, Name):
  Name = first name in [identity, reflect_h, reflect_v, transpose,
                        rotate90, rotate180, rotate270, anti_diag]
         such that applying Name to Grid1 gives Grid2

sk_upscale(Grid, Factor, Scaled):
  for each row Row in Grid:
    TiledRow = repeat each cell Factor times
  Scaled = repeat each TiledRow Factor times vertically

dn_find_scale(Grid1, Grid2, Factor):
  Factor = NRows2 / NRows1 (must be integer)
  verify NCols2 / NCols1 = Factor
  verify sk_upscale(Grid1, Factor) = Grid2

END OF PART 87


PART 88 - REMAP PACK PSEUDOCODE (Layer 77)

What changed: Pseudocode for all 14 rm_* predicates.

Why: Documents the reasoning structure for each predicate; serves as the
bridge between the Specification (what) and the Prolog implementation (how).

rm_replace(Grid, Old, New, Grid2):
  maplist each row through rm_replace_row_(Old, New)
  for each cell: if cell == Old then New else cell

rm_swap(Grid, A, B, Grid2):
  maplist each row through rm_swap_row_(A, B)
  for each cell: if A then B; if B then A; else unchanged

rm_apply_map(Map, Grid, Grid2):
  maplist each row through rm_apply_map_row_(Map)
  for each cell: member(cell-New, Map) -> New; else cell

rm_apply_map_to(Map, Val, Grid, Grid2):
  maplist each row; for each cell:
    if cell == Val then apply map lookup; else cell

rm_invert_map(Map, Inverted):
  maplist [K-V, V-K]>>true over Map

rm_compose_maps(Map1, Map2, Composed):
  for each K-V1 in Map1:
    look up V1 in Map2; if found get V2; else V2 = V1
    emit K-V2

rm_normalize(Grid, Grid2):
  collect all vals; sort to get Distinct
  build map: Distinct[I] -> I+1 (1-based)
  apply map to Grid

rm_shift(Grid, Delta, Grid2):
  maplist each row; each cell: Cell2 is Cell + Delta

rm_clamp(Grid, Lo, Hi, Grid2):
  maplist each row; each cell:
    if Cell < Lo then Lo; if Cell > Hi then Hi; else Cell

rm_conditional(Goal, Grid, Bg, Grid2):
  maplist each row; each cell:
    if call(Goal, Cell) then Bg; else Cell

rm_binarize(Grid, Bg, Fg, Grid2):
  maplist each row; each cell:
    if Cell == Bg then Bg; else Fg

rm_remap_bg(Grid, OldBg, NewBg, Grid2):
  delegate to rm_replace(Grid, OldBg, NewBg, Grid2)

rm_palette(Grid, Palette):
  findall all cell values; sort to get distinct sorted list

rm_reindex(Grid, OldPalette, Grid2):
  build map: OldPalette[I] -> I+1 (1-based) via rm_build_index_map_
  apply map to Grid

END OF PART 88


PART 89 - LOGIC PACK PSEUDOCODE (Layer 78)

What changed: Pseudocode for all 14 lg_* predicates.

Why: Documents the cell-wise decision structure for each boolean predicate.

lg_and(Grid1, Grid2, Bg, Grid3):
