oo_mirror_v_cells_(Cells, R0, _C0, H1, NewCells) [private]:
  For each R-C in Cells: Nr = R-R0.
  NewR = R0+H1-Nr, NewC = C (unchanged).

oo_mirror_v(Grid, V, Bg, Out):
  Cells = oo_cells_of(Grid, V).
  oo_bbox(Cells, R0, C0, R1, _C1).
  H1 = R1-R0.
  NewCells = oo_mirror_v_cells_(Cells, R0, C0, H1).
  Grid1 = oo_set_cells_(Grid, Cells, Bg).
  Out = oo_set_cells_(Grid1, NewCells, V).

END OF PART 159


PART 160 — PAIR PACK PSEUDOCODE (pr_* prefix, Layer 149)

pr_normalize_(Cells, Norm) [private]:
  Rs = findall(R, member(r(R,_), Cells)).
  Cs = findall(C, member(r(_,C), Cells)).
  MinR = min_list(Rs).
  MinC = min_list(Cs).
  Shifted = findall(r(R-MinR, C-MinC), member(r(R,C), Cells)).
  Norm = sort(Shifted).

pr_cell_d4_(id,  _H1, _W1, r(R,C), r(R,  C   )) [private].
pr_cell_d4_(r90,  H1, _W1, r(R,C), r(C,  H1-R)) [private].
pr_cell_d4_(r180, H1,  W1, r(R,C), r(H1-R, W1-C)) [private].
pr_cell_d4_(r270,_H1,  W1, r(R,C), r(W1-C, R  )) [private].
pr_cell_d4_(fh,  _H1,  W1, r(R,C), r(R,  W1-C)) [private].
pr_cell_d4_(fv,   H1, _W1, r(R,C), r(H1-R, C  )) [private].
pr_cell_d4_(fd1, _H1, _W1, r(R,C), r(C,  R   )) [private].
pr_cell_d4_(fd2,  H1,  W1, r(R,C), r(W1-C, H1-R)) [private].

pr_min_term_(A, B, A) [private]:
  A @< B.
pr_min_term_(A, B, B) [private]:
  otherwise.

pr_obj_shape(Obj, Shape):
  Obj = obj(_, Cells).
  Norm = pr_normalize_(Cells).
  Rs = findall(R, member(r(R,_), Norm)).
  Cs = findall(C, member(r(_,C), Norm)).
  H1 = max_list(Rs).   % max row in normalized cells (min is 0)
  W1 = max_list(Cs).   % max col in normalized cells (min is 0)
  Ops = [id, r90, r180, r270, fh, fv, fd1, fd2].
  Transforms = findall(S,
    (member(Op, Ops),
     Mapped = findall(r(NR,NC),
                (member(r(R,C), Norm),
                 pr_cell_d4_(Op, H1, W1, r(R,C), r(NR,NC)))),
     S = pr_normalize_(sort(Mapped)))).
  Shape = foldl(pr_min_term_, Transforms).

pr_obj_color(obj(Color, _), Color).

pr_obj_size(obj(_, Cells), N):
  N = length(Cells).

pr_shape_eq(Obj1, Obj2):
  S = pr_obj_shape(Obj1).
  S = pr_obj_shape(Obj2).

pr_color_eq(Obj1, Obj2):
  C = pr_obj_color(Obj1).
  C = pr_obj_color(Obj2).

pr_size_eq(Obj1, Obj2):
  N = pr_obj_size(Obj1).
  N = pr_obj_size(Obj2).

pr_group_by_(Objs, KeyGoal, Groups) [private]:
  Keys = sort(findall(K, (member(O, Objs), K = call(KeyGoal, O)))).
  Groups = findall(K-Grp,
    (member(K, Keys),
     Grp = findall(O, (member(O, Objs), call(KeyGoal, O) = K)))).

pr_group_color(Objs, Groups):
  Colors = sort(findall(C, (member(O, Objs), pr_obj_color(O, C)))).
  Groups = findall(C-Grp,
    (member(C, Colors),
     Grp = findall(O, (member(O, Objs), pr_obj_color(O, C))))).

pr_group_size(Objs, Groups):
  Sizes = sort(findall(N, (member(O, Objs), pr_obj_size(O, N)))).
  Groups = findall(N-Grp,
    (member(N, Sizes),
     Grp = findall(O, (member(O, Objs), pr_obj_size(O, N))))).

pr_group_shape(Objs, Groups):
  Shapes = sort(findall(S, (member(O, Objs), pr_obj_shape(O, S)))).
  Groups = findall(S-Grp,
    (member(S, Shapes),
     Grp = findall(O, (member(O, Objs), pr_obj_shape(O, S))))).

pr_unique_color(Objs, Obj):
  pr_group_color(Objs, Groups).
  member(_-[Obj], Groups).   % exactly one object in the group

pr_unique_size(Objs, Obj):
  pr_group_size(Objs, Groups).
  member(_-[Obj], Groups).   % exactly one object in the group

pr_match_color(Objs1, Objs2, Pairs):
  Pairs = findall(C-O1-O2,
    (member(O1, Objs1), member(O2, Objs2),
     pr_obj_color(O1, C), pr_obj_color(O2, C))).

pr_match_size(Objs1, Objs2, Pairs):
  Pairs = findall(N-O1-O2,
    (member(O1, Objs1), member(O2, Objs2),
     pr_obj_size(O1, N), pr_obj_size(O2, N))).

pr_match_shape(Objs1, Objs2, Pairs):
  Pairs = findall(S-O1-O2,
    (member(O1, Objs1), member(O2, Objs2),
     pr_obj_shape(O1, S), pr_obj_shape(O2, S))).

END OF PART 160


PART 161 - PSEUDOCODE: ARRANGE PACK (ag_* PREFIX, LAYER 150)

ag_centroid(obj(_, Cells), r(CR, CC)):
  Rs = findall(R: r(R,_) in Cells)
  Cs = findall(C: r(_,C) in Cells)
  N = length(Rs)
  SR = sum_list(Rs), SC = sum_list(Cs)
  CR = SR // N, CC = SC // N

ag_offset(Obj1, Obj2, r(DR, DC)):
  ag_centroid(Obj1, r(R1, C1))
  ag_centroid(Obj2, r(R2, C2))
  DR = R2 - R1, DC = C2 - C1

ag_row_order(Obj1, Obj2):
  ag_centroid(Obj1, r(R1, _))
  ag_centroid(Obj2, r(R2, _))
  R1 =< R2

ag_col_order(Obj1, Obj2):
  ag_centroid(Obj1, r(_, C1))
  ag_centroid(Obj2, r(_, C2))
  C1 =< C2

ag_row_aligned(Obj1, Obj2):
  ag_centroid(Obj1, r(R, _))
  ag_centroid(Obj2, r(R, _))   % same R by unification

ag_col_aligned(Obj1, Obj2):
  ag_centroid(Obj1, r(_, C))
  ag_centroid(Obj2, r(_, C))   % same C by unification

ag_sort_by_row(Objs, Sorted):
  Pairs = findall(R-O: O in Objs, ag_centroid(O, r(R,_)))
  SortedPairs = keysort(Pairs)
  Sorted = findall(O: _-O in SortedPairs)

ag_sort_by_col(Objs, Sorted):
  Pairs = findall(C-O: O in Objs, ag_centroid(O, r(_,C)))
  SortedPairs = keysort(Pairs)
  Sorted = findall(O: _-O in SortedPairs)

ag_consec_gaps_([], []).
ag_consec_gaps_([_], []) :- cut.
ag_consec_gaps_([A,B|T], [B-A | ag_consec_gaps_([B|T])]).

ag_row_gaps(Objs, Gaps):
  Rs0 = findall(R: O in Objs, ag_centroid(O, r(R,_)))
  Rs = sort(Rs0)
  Gaps = ag_consec_gaps_(Rs)

ag_col_gaps(Objs, Gaps):
  Cs0 = findall(C: O in Objs, ag_centroid(O, r(_,C)))
  Cs = sort(Cs0)
  Gaps = ag_consec_gaps_(Cs)

ag_all_equal_([_]) :- cut.
ag_all_equal_([X,X|T]) :- ag_all_equal_([X|T]).

ag_equal_row_gaps(Objs):
  Gaps = ag_row_gaps(Objs)
  Gaps = [_|_]
  ag_all_equal_(Gaps)

ag_equal_col_gaps(Objs):
  Gaps = ag_col_gaps(Objs)
  Gaps = [_|_]
  ag_all_equal_(Gaps)

ag_group_bbox(Objs, R0, C0, R1, C1):
  Rs = findall(R: obj(_,Cells) in Objs, r(R,_) in Cells)
  Cs = findall(C: obj(_,Cells) in Objs, r(_,C) in Cells)
  R0 = min_list(Rs), C0 = min_list(Cs)
  R1 = max_list(Rs), C1 = max_list(Cs)

ag_nearest(RefObj, Objs, Nearest):
  ag_centroid(RefObj, r(RR, RC))
  Pairs = findall(D-O:
    O in Objs,
    ag_centroid(O, r(OR, OC)),
    D = abs(OR-RR) + abs(OC-RC))
  [_-Nearest | _] = keysort(Pairs)

END OF PART 161


PART 162 - PSEUDOCODE: XFORM PACK (xf_* PREFIX, LAYER 151)

xf_recolor(obj(_, Cells), Color, obj(Color, Cells)).

xf_translate(obj(Color, Cells), r(DR, DC), obj(Color, Out)):
  Out = sort(findall(r(R+DR, C+DC): r(R,C) in Cells))

xf_normalize(obj(Color, Cells), obj(Color, Norm)):
  MinR = min_list(findall(R: r(R,_) in Cells))
  MinC = min_list(findall(C: r(_,C) in Cells))
  Norm = sort(findall(r(R-MinR, C-MinC): r(R,C) in Cells))

xf_d4(obj(Color, Cells), Op, obj(Color, Out)):
  MinR, MinC = min row/col of Cells
  NormCells = cells translated to origin
  H1, W1 = max row/col of NormCells
  Trans = sort(findall(r(NR,NC): r(R,C) in NormCells, xf_cell_d4_(Op,R,C,H1,W1,NR,NC)))
  Out = sort(findall(r(R+MinR,C+MinC): r(R,C) in Trans))

xf_same_cells(obj(_, Cells), obj(_, Cells)).

xf_cell_offset(Obj1, Obj2, r(DR, DC)):
  normalize both to Norm1, Norm2
  Norm1.cells = Norm2.cells   % unification
  DR = min_row(Obj2) - min_row(Obj1)
  DC = min_col(Obj2) - min_col(Obj1)

xf_is_recolor(obj(C1, Cells), obj(C2, Cells)) :- C1 \= C2.

xf_cells_added(obj(_,C1), obj(_,C2), subtract(C2, C1)).
xf_cells_removed(obj(_,C1), obj(_,C2), subtract(C1, C2)).

xf_cells_kept(obj(_,C1), obj(_,C2), Kept):
  Kept = sort(findall(Cell: Cell in C1, memberchk(Cell, C2)))

xf_overlap_count(Obj1, Obj2, N):
  xf_cells_kept(Obj1, Obj2, Kept), N = length(Kept)

xf_any_d4(Obj1, Obj2, Op):
  normalize Obj1 -> N1, Obj2 -> N2
  H1, W1 = max row/col of N1.cells
  for Op in [id, r90, r180, r270, fh, fv, fd1, fd2]:
    Raw = findall(r(NR,NC): r(R,C) in N1.cells, xf_cell_d4_(Op,R,C,H1,W1,NR,NC))
    if sort(Raw) = N2.cells: return Op (cut)

xf_scale_factor(obj(_,C1), obj(_,C2), N):
  Len1 = length(C1), Len2 = length(C2)
  Len1 > 0, 0 =:= Len2 mod Len1
  N = Len2 // Len1, N >= 1

xf_merge(obj(Color, C1), obj(Color, C2), obj(Color, sort(C1 ++ C2))).

END OF PART 162


PART 163: QUERY PACK PSEUDOCODE (qu_* prefix, Layer 152)

Private helper:

qu_norm_(Cells, Norm):
  Rs = findall(R: r(R,_) in Cells)
  Cs = findall(C: r(_,C) in Cells)
  MinR = min_list(Rs), MinC = min_list(Cs)
  Norm = sort(findall(r(R-MinR, C-MinC): r(R,C) in Cells))

qu_form_(obj(_, Cells), Form):
  qu_norm_(Cells, Form)

Aggregate counts:

qu_count_by_color(Objs, Counts):
  Cs0 = findall(C: obj(C,_) in Objs)
  Colors = sort(Cs0)
  Counts = findall(C-N: C in Colors,
                   Grp = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(C,_)),
                   N = length(Grp))

qu_count_by_size(Objs, Counts):
  Ss0 = findall(S: obj(_,Cells) in Objs, S = length(Cells))
  Sizes = sort(Ss0)
  Counts = findall(S-N: S in Sizes,
                   Grp = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), length(Cells) = S),
                   N = length(Grp))

qu_count_by_form(Objs, Counts):
  Fs0 = findall(F: O in Objs, qu_form_(O, F))
  Forms = sort(Fs0)
  Counts = findall(F-N: F in Forms,
                   Grp = findall(O: O in Objs, qu_form_(O, F)),
                   N = length(Grp))

Extremes:

qu_most_frequent_color(Objs, Color):
  qu_count_by_color(Objs, Counts)
  Ns = findall(N: _-N in Counts)
  MaxN = max_list(Ns)
  first Color-MaxN in Counts (cut)

qu_least_frequent_color(Objs, Color):
  qu_count_by_color(Objs, Counts)
  Ns = findall(N: _-N in Counts)
  MinN = min_list(Ns)
  first Color-MinN in Counts (cut)

qu_largest_obj(Objs, Obj):
  Pairs = findall(N-O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), N = length(Cells))
  Ns = findall(N: N-_ in Pairs)
  MaxN = max_list(Ns)
  first MaxN-Obj in Pairs (cut)

qu_smallest_obj(Objs, Obj):
  Pairs = findall(N-O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), N = length(Cells))
  Ns = findall(N: N-_ in Pairs)
  MinN = min_list(Ns)
  first MinN-Obj in Pairs (cut)

Totals and averages:

qu_total_cells(Objs, N):
  Ss = findall(S: obj(_,Cells) in Objs, S = length(Cells))
  N = sum_list(Ss)

qu_avg_size(Objs, N):
  qu_total_cells(Objs, Total)
  Count = length(Objs)
  N = Total // Count

Uniformity tests:

qu_all_same_color(Objs):
  Cs = findall(C: obj(C,_) in Objs)
  sort(Cs) = [_]

qu_all_same_size(Objs):
  Ss = findall(S: obj(_,Cells) in Objs, S = length(Cells))
  sort(Ss) = [_]

qu_all_same_form(Objs):
  Fs = findall(F: O in Objs, qu_form_(O, F))
  sort(Fs) = [_]

Enumeration:

qu_colors(Objs, Colors):
  Cs = findall(C: obj(C,_) in Objs)
  Colors = sort(Cs)

qu_sizes(Objs, Sizes):
  Ss = findall(S: obj(_,Cells) in Objs, S = length(Cells))
  Sizes = sort(Ss)

END OF PART 163


PART 164: SIFT PACK PSEUDOCODE (si_* prefix, Layer 153)

Private helpers:

si_norm_(Cells, Norm):
  Rs = findall(R: r(R,_) in Cells)
  Cs = findall(C: r(_,C) in Cells)
  MinR = min_list(Rs), MinC = min_list(Cs)
  Norm = sort(findall(r(R-MinR, C-MinC): r(R,C) in Cells))

si_on_border_(R, _, _H, _W):- R =:= 0, cut.
si_on_border_(R, _, H, _W) :- R =:= H-1, cut.
si_on_border_(_, C, _H, _W):- C =:= 0, cut.
si_on_border_(_, C, _H, W) :- C =:= W-1.

Color and form filters:

si_by_color(Objs, Color, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(Color, _))

si_not_color(Objs, Color, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(C,_), C \= Color)

si_by_size(Objs, N, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), length(Cells) = N)

si_by_form(Objs, Form, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), si_norm_(Cells) = Form)

Size threshold filters:

si_larger_than(Objs, N, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), length(Cells) > N)

si_smaller_than(Objs, N, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), length(Cells) < N)

Color set filters:

si_color_in(Objs, Colors, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(C,_), memberchk(C, Colors))

si_color_not_in(Objs, Colors, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(C,_), not memberchk(C, Colors))

Size extreme filters (return ALL tied objects, not just first):

si_max_size(Objs, Out):
  Ss = findall(S: obj(_,Cells) in Objs, S = length(Cells))
  MaxS = max_list(Ss)
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), length(Cells) = MaxS)

si_min_size(Objs, Out):
  Ss = findall(S: obj(_,Cells) in Objs, S = length(Cells))
  MinS = min_list(Ss)
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells), length(Cells) = MinS)

Color frequency filters:

si_unique_color(Objs, Out):
  Cs0 = findall(C: obj(C,_) in Objs)
  Colors = sort(Cs0)
  ColorCounts = findall(C-N: C in Colors,
                        Grp = findall(_: obj(C,_) in Objs), N = length(Grp))
  UniqueColors = findall(C: C-1 in ColorCounts)
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(C,_), memberchk(C, UniqueColors))

si_shared_color(Objs, Out):
  [same as si_unique_color but collect C where N > 1]

Border filters:

si_on_border(Objs, H, W, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells),
                exists r(R,C) in Cells with si_on_border_(R,C,H,W))

si_off_border(Objs, H, W, Out):
  Out = findall(O: O in Objs, O = obj(_,Cells),
                not exists r(R,C) in Cells with si_on_border_(R,C,H,W))

END OF PART 164


PART 165: PIGMENT PACK PSEUDOCODE (pg_* prefix, Layer 154)

Private helper:

pg_count_by_color_(Objs, Counts):
  Cs0 = findall(C: obj(C,_) in Objs)
  Colors = sort(Cs0)
  Counts = findall(C-N: C in Colors,
                   Grp = findall(_: obj(C,_) in Objs), N = length(Grp))

Uniform and targeted recoloring:

pg_recolor_all(Objs, Color, Out):
  Out = findall(obj(Color,Cells): obj(_,Cells) in Objs)

pg_recolor_one(Objs, From, To, Out):
  Out = findall(O: obj(C,Cells) in Objs,
                if C =:= From then O = obj(To,Cells) else O = obj(C,Cells))

pg_swap(Objs, C1, C2, Out):
  Out = findall(O: obj(C,Cells) in Objs,
                if C =:= C1 then O = obj(C2,Cells)
                else if C =:= C2 then O = obj(C1,Cells)
                else O = obj(C,Cells))

Color table operations:

pg_apply_table(Objs, Table, Out):
  Out = findall(O: obj(C,Cells) in Objs,
                if memberchk(C-New, Table) then O = obj(New,Cells)
                else O = obj(C,Cells))

pg_apply_table_strict(Objs, Table, Out):
  Out = findall(obj(New,Cells): obj(C,Cells) in Objs, memberchk(C-New, Table))

pg_infer_table(Objs1, Objs2, Table):
  Pairs0 = findall(C1-C2: obj(C1,Cells) in Objs1, obj(C2,Cells) in Objs2)
  Table = sort(Pairs0)

Zip-based recoloring:

pg_zip_recolor([], _, []) :- cut.
pg_zip_recolor(_, [], []) :- cut.
pg_zip_recolor([obj(_,Cells)|Os], [C|Cs], [obj(C,Cells)|Rest]):
  pg_zip_recolor(Os, Cs, Rest)

Frequency-targeted recoloring:

pg_majority_to(Objs, Color, Out):
  pg_count_by_color_(Objs, Counts)
  MaxN = max_list(findall(N: _-N in Counts))
  first MajorC-MaxN in Counts (cut)
  Out = findall(O: obj(C,Cells) in Objs,
                if C =:= MajorC then O=obj(Color,Cells) else O=obj(C,Cells))

pg_minority_to(Objs, Color, Out):
  [analogous to pg_majority_to using min_list and MinN]

pg_unique_to(Objs, Color, Out):
  pg_count_by_color_(Objs, Counts)
  UniqueColors = findall(C: C-1 in Counts)
  Out = findall(O: obj(C,Cells) in Objs,
                if memberchk(C, UniqueColors) then O=obj(Color,Cells)
                else O=obj(C,Cells))

pg_shared_to(Objs, Color, Out):
  pg_count_by_color_(Objs, Counts)
  SharedColors = findall(C: C-N in Counts, N > 1)
  [same if-then-else pattern as pg_unique_to]

Table utilities:

pg_invert_table(Table, Inv):
  Inv = findall(To-From: From-To in Table)

pg_table_from(Table, Froms):
  Fs = findall(F: F-_ in Table)
  Froms = sort(Fs)

pg_consistent(Table):
  not exists F,T1,T2 in Table where F-T1 and F-T2 and T1 \= T2

END OF PART 165


Part 166: Pseudocode for Work Package 176 - Delta Pack

WP-176-PSEUDO-001: dl_added(S1, S2, Added)
  COLLECT O2 FROM S2 WHERE
    O2 = obj(_, Cells)
    AND NOT EXISTS obj(_, Cells) IN S1
  RETURN Added

WP-176-PSEUDO-002: dl_removed(S1, S2, Removed)
  COLLECT O1 FROM S1 WHERE
    O1 = obj(_, Cells)
    AND NOT EXISTS obj(_, Cells) IN S2
  RETURN Removed

WP-176-PSEUDO-003: dl_matched(S1, S2, Pairs)
  COLLECT O1-O2 WHERE
    O1 IN S1, O1 = obj(_, Cells)
    O2 IN S2, O2 = obj(_, Cells)   % same Cells bound from O1
  SORT and deduplicate
  RETURN Pairs

WP-176-PSEUDO-004: dl_recolored(S1, S2, Changes)
  COLLECT C1-C2 WHERE
    obj(C1, Cells) IN S1
    obj(C2, Cells) IN S2
    C1 != C2
  SORT and deduplicate
  RETURN Changes

WP-176-PSEUDO-005: dl_unchanged(S1, S2, Objs)
  COLLECT O WHERE
    O IN S1
    O IN S2   % same color + same cells via term unification
  SORT and deduplicate
  RETURN Objs

WP-176-PSEUDO-006: dl_color_gain(S1, S2, Colors)
  Pal1 = SORTED UNIQUE COLORS IN S1
  Pal2 = SORTED UNIQUE COLORS IN S2
  RETURN C WHERE C IN Pal2 AND C NOT IN Pal1

WP-176-PSEUDO-007: dl_color_loss(S1, S2, Colors)
  Pal1 = SORTED UNIQUE COLORS IN S1
  Pal2 = SORTED UNIQUE COLORS IN S2
  RETURN C WHERE C IN Pal1 AND C NOT IN Pal2

WP-176-PSEUDO-008: dl_count_diff(S1, S2, N)
  N = length(S2) - length(S1)

WP-176-PSEUDO-009: dl_size_diff(S1, S2, N)
  Total1 = SUM OF length(Cells) FOR EACH obj(_, Cells) IN S1
  Total2 = SUM OF length(Cells) FOR EACH obj(_, Cells) IN S2
  N = Total2 - Total1

WP-176-PSEUDO-010: dl_is_added_only(S1, S2)
  REQUIRE dl_removed(S1, S2) = []
  REQUIRE dl_recolored(S1, S2) = []

WP-176-PSEUDO-011: dl_is_removed_only(S1, S2)
  REQUIRE dl_added(S1, S2) = []
  REQUIRE dl_recolored(S1, S2) = []

WP-176-PSEUDO-012: dl_is_recolor_only(S1, S2)
  REQUIRE dl_added(S1, S2) = []
  REQUIRE dl_removed(S1, S2) = []

WP-176-PSEUDO-013: dl_is_stable(S1, S2)
  REQUIRE dl_added(S1, S2) = []
  REQUIRE dl_removed(S1, S2) = []
  REQUIRE dl_recolored(S1, S2) = []

WP-176-PSEUDO-014: dl_scene_diff(S1, S2, delta(Added, Removed, Recolored, Unchanged))
  Added     = dl_added(S1, S2)
  Removed   = dl_removed(S1, S2)
  Recolored = dl_recolored(S1, S2)
  Unchanged = dl_unchanged(S1, S2)
  RETURN delta(Added, Removed, Recolored, Unchanged)


Part 167: Pseudocode for Work Package 177 - Group Pack

WP-177-PSEUDO-001: gp_by_color(Objs, Groups)
  Colors = SORT(DISTINCT(color(O) FOR O IN Objs))
  Groups = [(C, [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE color(O)=C]) FOR C IN Colors]

WP-177-PSEUDO-002: gp_by_size(Objs, Groups)
  Sizes = SORT(DISTINCT(length(cells(O)) FOR O IN Objs))
  Groups = [(N, [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE length(cells(O))=N]) FOR N IN Sizes]

WP-177-PSEUDO-003: gp_by_row(Objs, Groups)
  Rows = SORT(DISTINCT(min_row(O) FOR O IN Objs))
  Groups = [(R, [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE min_row(O)=R]) FOR R IN Rows]
  min_row(O) = min(row(c) FOR c IN cells(O))

WP-177-PSEUDO-004: gp_by_col(Objs, Groups)
  Cols = SORT(DISTINCT(min_col(O) FOR O IN Objs))
  Groups = [(C, [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE min_col(O)=C]) FOR C IN Cols]
  min_col(O) = min(col(c) FOR c IN cells(O))

WP-177-PSEUDO-005: gp_by_form(Objs, Groups)
  Forms = SORT(DISTINCT(gp_norm(cells(O)) FOR O IN Objs))
  Groups = [(F, [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE gp_norm(cells(O))=F]) FOR F IN Forms]
  gp_norm(Cells) = SORT([(R-MinR, C-MinC) FOR (R,C) IN Cells])
    where MinR=min rows, MinC=min cols

WP-177-PSEUDO-006: gp_size_of(Groups, N)
  N = length(Groups)

WP-177-PSEUDO-007: gp_flatten(Groups, Objs)
  Objs = [O FOR (Key, Grp) IN Groups FOR O IN Grp]

WP-177-PSEUDO-008: gp_largest_group(Groups, Key-Grp)
  MaxN = max(length(Grp) FOR (Key, Grp) IN Groups)
  Key  = first Key in Groups WHERE length(Grp) = MaxN
  Grp  = Groups[Key]

WP-177-PSEUDO-009: gp_smallest_group(Groups, Key-Grp)
  MinN = min(length(Grp) FOR (Key, Grp) IN Groups)
  Key  = first Key in Groups WHERE length(Grp) = MinN
  Grp  = Groups[Key]

WP-177-PSEUDO-010: gp_singleton_groups(Groups, Singles)
  Singles = [(Key, Grp) FROM Groups WHERE length(Grp) = 1]

WP-177-PSEUDO-011: gp_shared_groups(Groups, Shared)
  Shared = [(Key, Grp) FROM Groups WHERE length(Grp) > 1]

WP-177-PSEUDO-012: gp_group_sizes(Groups, Sizes)
  Sizes = SORT(DISTINCT(length(Grp) FOR (_, Grp) IN Groups))

WP-177-PSEUDO-013: gp_all_same_size(Groups)
  Base case: Groups = [] SUCCEEDS vacuously.
  General: SORT(DISTINCT(length(Grp) FOR (_, Grp) IN Groups)) = [_]
    i.e. exactly one distinct cardinality.

WP-177-PSEUDO-014: gp_keys(Groups, Keys)
  Keys = SORT(DISTINCT(Key FOR (Key, _) IN Groups))

Part 168: Proximity Pack Pseudocode (WP 178, Layer 157)

Section 168.1: px_centroid/3

PROCEDURE px_centroid(Obj, R, C):
  Cells <- Obj.cells
  Rs <- [r.row FOR r IN Cells]
  SumR <- sum(Rs)
  Cs <- [r.col FOR r IN Cells]
  SumC <- sum(Cs)
  N <- length(Cells)
  R <- SumR // N    // integer division truncates toward zero
  C <- SumC // N

Section 168.2: px_centroid_dist/3

PROCEDURE px_centroid_dist(O1, O2, D):
  (R1, C1) <- centroid(O1)
  (R2, C2) <- centroid(O2)
  D <- |R1-R2| + |C1-C2|

Section 168.3: px_min_cell_dist/3

PROCEDURE px_min_cell_dist(O1, O2, D):
  Dists <- [|R1-R2|+|C1-C2| FOR r(R1,C1) IN O1.cells, r(R2,C2) IN O2.cells]
  D <- min(Dists)

Section 168.4: px_touching/2

PROCEDURE px_touching(O1, O2):
  FOR r(R1,C1) IN O1.cells:
    FOR r(R2,C2) IN O2.cells:
      IF |R1-R2|+|C1-C2| == 1: RETURN true
  RETURN false

Section 168.5: px_nearest/3 and px_farthest/3

PROCEDURE px_nearest(Objs, Ref, Nearest):
  Pairs <- [(centroid_dist(O,Ref), O) FOR O IN Objs]
  MinD <- min([d FOR (d,_) IN Pairs])
  Nearest <- first O such that (MinD, O) IN Pairs

PROCEDURE px_farthest(Objs, Ref, Farthest):
  Pairs <- [(centroid_dist(O,Ref), O) FOR O IN Objs]
  MaxD <- max([d FOR (d,_) IN Pairs])
  Farthest <- first O such that (MaxD, O) IN Pairs

Section 168.6: px_sort_by_dist/3

PROCEDURE px_sort_by_dist(Objs, Ref, Sorted):
  Pairs <- [(centroid_dist(O,Ref), O) FOR O IN Objs]
  SortedPairs <- stable_sort_ascending(Pairs)
  Sorted <- [O FOR (_, O) IN SortedPairs]

Section 168.7: px_within_dist/4 and px_beyond_dist/4

PROCEDURE px_within_dist(Objs, Ref, D, Near):
  Near <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF centroid_dist(O,Ref) <= D]

PROCEDURE px_beyond_dist(Objs, Ref, D, Far):
  Far <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF centroid_dist(O,Ref) > D]

Section 168.8: px_closest_pair/2 and px_farthest_pair/2

PROCEDURE px_closest_pair(Objs, O1-O2):
  N <- length(Objs)
  Triples <- [(centroid_dist(Objs[i],Objs[j]), i, j)
              FOR i IN 1..N, j IN (i+1)..N]
  MinD <- min([d FOR (d,_,_) IN Triples])
  (_, Pi, Pj) <- first triple with d==MinD
  O1 <- Objs[Pi], O2 <- Objs[Pj]

PROCEDURE px_farthest_pair(Objs, O1-O2):
  // Same structure as px_closest_pair but uses max instead of min.

Section 168.9: px_touching_objs/3 and px_non_touching_objs/3

PROCEDURE px_touching_objs(Objs, Ref, Touching):
  Touching <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF touching(O, Ref)]

PROCEDURE px_non_touching_objs(Objs, Ref, NonTouching):
  NonTouching <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF NOT touching(O, Ref)]

Section 168.10: px_dist_rank/3

PROCEDURE px_dist_rank(Objs, Ref, Ranked):
  Pairs <- [(centroid_dist(O,Ref), O) FOR O IN Objs]
  Ranked <- stable_sort_ascending(Pairs)

Part 169: Link Pack Pseudocode (WP 179, Layer 158)

Section 169.1: lk_by_position/3

PROCEDURE lk_by_position([], _, []).
PROCEDURE lk_by_position(_, [], []).
PROCEDURE lk_by_position([O1|T1], [O2|T2], [O1-O2|Links]):
  lk_by_position(T1, T2, Links)

Section 169.2: lk_by_nearest/3

PROCEDURE lk_by_nearest(Objs1, Objs2, Links):
  IF Objs2 == []: Links = [], RETURN
  Links <- [(O1, nearest(O1, Objs2)) FOR O1 IN Objs1]

PROCEDURE nearest(Ref, Objs):
  (R1,C1) <- centroid(Ref)
  Pairs <- [(manhattan_dist(centroid(O),(R1,C1)), O) FOR O IN Objs]
  MinD <- min([d FOR (d,_) IN Pairs])
  RETURN first O such that (MinD, O) IN Pairs

Section 169.3: lk_by_color/3

PROCEDURE lk_by_color(Objs1, Objs2, Links):
  Links <- sort(deduplicate([O1-O2 FOR O1 IN Objs1, O2 IN Objs2
                              IF color(O1) == color(O2)]))

Section 169.4: lk_by_size/3

PROCEDURE lk_by_size(Objs1, Objs2, Links):
  Links <- sort(deduplicate([O1-O2 FOR O1 IN Objs1, O2 IN Objs2
                              IF |cells(O1)| == |cells(O2)|]))

Section 169.5: lk_by_form/3

PROCEDURE lk_by_form(Objs1, Objs2, Links):
  Links <- sort(deduplicate([O1-O2 FOR O1 IN Objs1, O2 IN Objs2
                              IF normalize(cells(O1)) == normalize(cells(O2))]))

PROCEDURE normalize(Cells):
  minR <- min row of Cells; minC <- min col of Cells
  Form <- sort([r(R-minR, C-minC) FOR r(R,C) IN Cells])
  RETURN Form

Section 169.6: lk_source, lk_target, lk_invert, lk_count

PROCEDURE lk_source(Links, Sources): Sources <- [O1 FOR O1-_ IN Links]
PROCEDURE lk_target(Links, Targets): Targets <- [O2 FOR _-O2 IN Links]
PROCEDURE lk_invert(Links, Inverted): Inverted <- [O2-O1 FOR O1-O2 IN Links]
PROCEDURE lk_count(Links, N): N <- length(Links)

Section 169.7: lk_apply_color and lk_apply_cells

PROCEDURE lk_apply_color(Links, Result):
  Result <- [obj(color(O2), cells(O1)) FOR O1-O2 IN Links]

PROCEDURE lk_apply_cells(Links, Result):
  Result <- [obj(color(O1), cells(O2)) FOR O1-O2 IN Links]

Section 169.8: lk_filter_same_color, lk_filter_diff_color

PROCEDURE lk_filter_same_color(Links, Same):
  Same <- [L FOR L=O1-O2 IN Links IF color(O1)==color(O2)]

PROCEDURE lk_filter_diff_color(Links, Diff):
  Diff <- [L FOR L=O1-O2 IN Links IF color(O1)!=color(O2)]

Section 169.9: lk_unlinked/3

PROCEDURE lk_unlinked(Objs, Links, Unlinked):
  Unlinked <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF O NOT IN sources(Links)]

Part 170: Layout Pack Pseudocode (WP 180, Layer 159)

Section 170.1: lt_global_bbox/5

PROCEDURE lt_global_bbox(Objs, R1, C1, R2, C2):
  All_Rs <- [r.row FOR obj IN Objs, r IN obj.cells]
  All_Cs <- [r.col FOR obj IN Objs, r IN obj.cells]
  R1 <- min(All_Rs); R2 <- max(All_Rs)
  C1 <- min(All_Cs); C2 <- max(All_Cs)

Section 170.2: lt_row_range/3 and lt_col_range/3

PROCEDURE lt_row_range(Objs, MinTopR, MaxTopR):
  TopRows <- [min_row(obj) FOR obj IN Objs]
  MinTopR <- min(TopRows); MaxTopR <- max(TopRows)

PROCEDURE lt_col_range(Objs, MinLeftC, MaxLeftC):
  LeftCols <- [min_col(obj) FOR obj IN Objs]
  MinLeftC <- min(LeftCols); MaxLeftC <- max(LeftCols)

Section 170.3: lt_all_same_row/1 and lt_all_same_col/1

PROCEDURE lt_all_same_row(Objs):
  IF Objs == []: RETURN true
  TopRows <- [min_row(obj) FOR obj IN Objs]
  RETURN |sort(TopRows)| == 1

PROCEDURE lt_all_same_col(Objs):
  IF Objs == []: RETURN true
  LeftCols <- [min_col(obj) FOR obj IN Objs]
  RETURN |sort(LeftCols)| == 1

Section 170.4: lt_is_grid/3

PROCEDURE lt_is_grid(Objs, Rows, Cols):
  CentroidPairs <- [(centroid_row(O), centroid_col(O)) FOR O IN Objs]
  CRows <- sort(distinct centroid rows)
  CCols <- sort(distinct centroid cols)
  Rows <- |CRows|; Cols <- |CCols|
  VERIFY: every (R,C) in CRows x CCols appears in CentroidPairs
  VERIFY: |Objs| == Rows * Cols

Section 170.5: lt_is_diagonal_dr/1 and lt_is_diagonal_dl/1

PROCEDURE lt_is_diagonal_dr(Objs):
  Ds <- [centroid_R(O) - centroid_C(O) FOR O IN Objs]
  RETURN |sort(Ds)| == 1

PROCEDURE lt_is_diagonal_dl(Objs):
  Ss <- [centroid_R(O) + centroid_C(O) FOR O IN Objs]
  RETURN |sort(Ss)| == 1

Section 170.6: lt_gap_h/2 and lt_gap_v/2

PROCEDURE lt_gap_h(Objs, Gap):
  Cols <- [centroid_C(O) FOR O sorted ascending by centroid_C]
  Gaps <- [Cols[i+1] - Cols[i] FOR i IN 0..|Cols|-2]
  VERIFY: all gaps equal; Gap <- Gaps[0]; VERIFY Gap > 0

PROCEDURE lt_gap_v(Objs, Gap):
  Rows <- [centroid_R(O) FOR O sorted ascending by centroid_R]
  Gaps <- [Rows[i+1] - Rows[i] FOR i IN 0..|Rows|-2]
  VERIFY: all gaps equal; Gap <- Gaps[0]; VERIFY Gap > 0

Part 171: Weave Pack Pseudocode (wv_*, Layer 160)

Section 171.1: wv_alternate/3

PROCEDURE wv_alternate(L1, L2, Result):
  IF L1 == [] THEN Result <- L2; RETURN
  Result <- [L1[0]] ++ wv_alternate(L2, L1[1:])

Section 171.2: wv_split_even_odd/3

PROCEDURE wv_split_even_odd(List, Evens, Odds):
  IF List == [] THEN Evens <- []; Odds <- []; RETURN
  Evens <- [List[0]] ++ wv_split_even_odd(List[1:], Odds, ...)
  NOTE: roles of Evens and Odds swap at each recursive step.

Section 171.3: wv_stride/3

PROCEDURE wv_stride(List, Step, Result):
  IF List == [] THEN Result <- []; RETURN
  Skip <- Step - 1
  Remaining <- List[Skip+1:]
  Result <- [List[0]] ++ wv_stride(Remaining, Step)

Section 171.4: wv_chunk/3

PROCEDURE wv_chunk(List, N, Chunks):
  IF List == [] THEN Chunks <- []; RETURN
  IF |List| < N THEN Chunks <- []; RETURN
  Chunk <- List[0:N]; Rest <- List[N:]
  Chunks <- [Chunk] ++ wv_chunk(Rest, N)

Section 171.5: wv_pair_wise/2 and wv_triple_wise/2

PROCEDURE wv_pair_wise(List, Pairs):
  IF |List| < 2 THEN Pairs <- []; RETURN
  Pairs <- [[List[0], List[1]]] ++ wv_pair_wise(List[1:])

PROCEDURE wv_triple_wise(List, Triples):
  IF |List| < 3 THEN Triples <- []; RETURN
  Triples <- [[List[0], List[1], List[2]]] ++ wv_triple_wise(List[1:])

Section 171.6: wv_rotate_left/3 and wv_rotate_right/3

PROCEDURE wv_rotate_left(List, K, Result):
  IF List == [] THEN Result <- []; RETURN
  K1 <- K mod |List|
  IF K1 == 0 THEN Result <- List; RETURN
  Front <- List[0:K1]; Back <- List[K1:]
  Result <- Back ++ Front

PROCEDURE wv_rotate_right(List, K, Result):
  K1 <- K mod |List|
  K2 <- |List| - K1
  Result <- wv_rotate_left(List, K2)

Section 171.7: wv_reflect/2, wv_repeat/3, wv_take/3, wv_drop/3

PROCEDURE wv_reflect(List, Result): Result <- reverse(List)

PROCEDURE wv_repeat(List, N, Result):
  IF N == 0 THEN Result <- []; RETURN
  Result <- List ++ wv_repeat(List, N-1)

PROCEDURE wv_take(List, N, Result):
  IF N == 0 OR List == [] THEN Result <- []; RETURN
  Result <- [List[0]] ++ wv_take(List[1:], N-1)

PROCEDURE wv_drop(List, N, Result):
  IF N == 0 THEN Result <- List; RETURN
  IF List == [] THEN Result <- []; RETURN
  Result <- wv_drop(List[1:], N-1)

Section 171.8: wv_cycle/3 and wv_zip/3

PROCEDURE wv_cycle(List, N, Result):
  IF N == 0 THEN Result <- []; RETURN
  Result <- wv_cycle_(List, List, N)

PROCEDURE wv_cycle_(Current, Source, N, Result):
  IF N == 0 THEN Result <- []; RETURN
  IF Current == [] THEN Result <- wv_cycle_(Source, Source, N); RETURN
  Result <- [Current[0]] ++ wv_cycle_(Current[1:], Source, N-1)

PROCEDURE wv_zip(List1, List2, Pairs):
  IF List1 == [] OR List2 == [] THEN Pairs <- []; RETURN
  Pairs <- [List1[0]-List2[0]] ++ wv_zip(List1[1:], List2[1:])

Part 172: Sizeop Pack Pseudocode (sz_*, Layer 161)

Section 172.1: sz_of/2

PROCEDURE sz_of(Obj, N): N <- length(Obj.Cells)

Section 172.2: sz_sort_asc/2 and sz_sort_desc/2

PROCEDURE sz_sort_asc(Objs, Sorted):
  Pairs <- [(sz_of(O), O) FOR O IN Objs]
  Sorted <- [O FOR (_, O) IN keysort(Pairs)]

PROCEDURE sz_sort_desc(Objs, Sorted):
  Pairs <- [(sz_of(O), O) FOR O IN Objs]
  NegPairs <- [(-N, O) FOR (N, O) IN Pairs]
  Sorted <- [O FOR (_, O) IN keysort(NegPairs)]

Section 172.3: sz_smallest/2 and sz_largest/2

PROCEDURE sz_smallest(Objs, Obj):
  MinN <- min([sz_of(O) FOR O IN Objs])
  Obj <- first O in Objs with sz_of(O) = MinN

PROCEDURE sz_largest(Objs, Obj):
  MaxN <- max([sz_of(O) FOR O IN Objs])
  Obj <- first O in Objs with sz_of(O) = MaxN

Section 172.4: sz_nth_smallest/3 and sz_nth_largest/3

PROCEDURE sz_nth_smallest(Objs, N, Obj):
  Sorted <- sz_sort_asc(Objs)
  Obj <- Sorted[N]  (1-indexed)

PROCEDURE sz_nth_largest(Objs, N, Obj):
  Sorted <- sz_sort_desc(Objs)
  Obj <- Sorted[N]  (1-indexed)

Section 172.5: sz_rank_of/3 and sz_assign_colors/3

PROCEDURE sz_rank_of(Objs, Obj, Rank):
  Sorted <- sz_sort_asc(Objs)
  Rank <- position of Obj in Sorted (1-indexed)

PROCEDURE sz_assign_colors(Objs, Colors, Result):
  Sorted <- sz_sort_asc(Objs)
  Result <- [obj(Colors[i], Sorted[i].Cells) FOR i IN 1..min(|Sorted|, |Colors|)]

Section 172.6: sz_by_size/3, sz_above/3, sz_below/3

PROCEDURE sz_by_size(Objs, N, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF sz_of(O) = N]

PROCEDURE sz_above(Objs, N, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF sz_of(O) > N]

PROCEDURE sz_below(Objs, N, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF sz_of(O) < N]

Section 172.7: sz_unique_sizes/2 and sz_total_cells/2

PROCEDURE sz_unique_sizes(Objs, Sizes):
  Sizes <- sort(distinct([sz_of(O) FOR O IN Objs]))

PROCEDURE sz_total_cells(Objs, N):
  N <- sum([sz_of(O) FOR O IN Objs])

Part 173: Posop Pack Pseudocode (po_*, Layer 162)

Section 173.1: Position Extraction

PROCEDURE po_row_of(Obj, Row):
  Rs <- [R FOR r(R,_) IN Obj.Cells]
  Row <- min(Rs)

PROCEDURE po_col_of(Obj, Col):
  Cs <- [C FOR r(_,C) IN Obj.Cells]
  Col <- min(Cs)

Section 173.2: Private Sort Helpers

PROCEDURE po_sort_by_row_(Objs, Sorted):
  Pairs <- [po_row_of(O) - O FOR O IN Objs]
  SortedPairs <- keysort_stable(Pairs)  // ascending by row; equal rows keep input order
  Sorted <- [O FOR (_-O) IN SortedPairs]

PROCEDURE po_sort_by_col_(Objs, Sorted):
  Pairs <- [po_col_of(O) - O FOR O IN Objs]
  SortedPairs <- keysort_stable(Pairs)
  Sorted <- [O FOR (_-O) IN SortedPairs]

PROCEDURE po_sort_reading_(Objs, Sorted):
  Pairs <- [(po_row_of(O)-po_col_of(O)) - O FOR O IN Objs]
  // compound key (Row-Col) sorts row-first then col-second
  SortedPairs <- keysort_stable(Pairs)
  Sorted <- [O FOR (_-O) IN SortedPairs]

Section 173.3: Rank Predicates

PROCEDURE po_row_rank(Objs, Obj, Rank):
  Sorted <- po_sort_by_row_(Objs)
  Rank <- position of Obj in Sorted (1-indexed)

PROCEDURE po_col_rank(Objs, Obj, Rank):
  Sorted <- po_sort_by_col_(Objs)
  Rank <- position of Obj in Sorted (1-indexed)

PROCEDURE po_reading_rank(Objs, Obj, Rank):
  Sorted <- po_sort_reading_(Objs)
  Rank <- position of Obj in Sorted (1-indexed)

Section 173.4: Color Assignment Predicates

PROCEDURE po_assign_by_row(Objs, Colors, Result):
  Sorted <- po_sort_by_row_(Objs)
  Result <- [obj(Colors[i], Sorted[i].Cells) FOR i IN 1..min(|Sorted|, |Colors|)]

PROCEDURE po_assign_by_col(Objs, Colors, Result):
  Sorted <- po_sort_by_col_(Objs)
  Result <- [obj(Colors[i], Sorted[i].Cells) FOR i IN 1..min(|Sorted|, |Colors|)]

PROCEDURE po_assign_reading(Objs, Colors, Result):
  Sorted <- po_sort_reading_(Objs)
  Result <- [obj(Colors[i], Sorted[i].Cells) FOR i IN 1..min(|Sorted|, |Colors|)]

Section 173.5: Threshold Filtering Predicates

PROCEDURE po_above_row(Objs, R, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF po_row_of(O) < R]

PROCEDURE po_from_row(Objs, R, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF po_row_of(O) >= R]

PROCEDURE po_left_of(Objs, C, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF po_col_of(O) < C]

PROCEDURE po_from_col(Objs, C, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF po_col_of(O) >= C]

PROCEDURE po_in_row_band(Objs, R1, R2, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF R1 <= po_row_of(O) <= R2]

PROCEDURE po_in_col_band(Objs, C1, C2, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs IF C1 <= po_col_of(O) <= C2]

Part 174: Objxf Pack Pseudocode (ox_*, Layer 163)

Section 174.1: Bounding Box and Size

PROCEDURE ox_bbox(Obj, R0, C0, R1, C1):
  Rs <- [R FOR r(R,_) IN Obj.Cells]
  Cs <- [C FOR r(_,C) IN Obj.Cells]
  R0 <- min(Rs); R1 <- max(Rs)
  C0 <- min(Cs); C1 <- max(Cs)

PROCEDURE ox_size(Obj, H, W):
  (R0, C0, R1, C1) <- ox_bbox(Obj)
  H <- R1 - R0 + 1
  W <- C1 - C0 + 1

Section 174.2: Translation and Normalization

PROCEDURE ox_translate(Obj, DR, DC, Result):
  Result.Color <- Obj.Color
  Result.Cells <- [r(R+DR, C+DC) FOR r(R,C) IN Obj.Cells]

PROCEDURE ox_to_origin(Obj, Result):
  (R0, C0, _, _) <- ox_bbox(Obj)
  Result <- ox_translate(Obj, -R0, -C0)

PROCEDURE ox_recolor(Obj, NewColor, Result):
  Result <- obj(NewColor, Obj.Cells)

Section 174.3: Rotations

PROCEDURE ox_rot90(Obj, Result):
  (R0, _, R1, _) <- ox_bbox(Obj); H <- R1 - R0 + 1
  C0 <- min column in Obj.Cells
  Result.Cells <- [r(R0+Lc, C0+(H-1)-Lr) FOR r(R,C) IN Obj.Cells,
                   Lr<-R-R0, Lc<-C-C0]
  Result.Color <- Obj.Color

PROCEDURE ox_rot180(Obj, Result):
  (R0, C0, R1, C1) <- ox_bbox(Obj)
  Result.Cells <- [r(R0+R1-R, C0+C1-C) FOR r(R,C) IN Obj.Cells]
  Result.Color <- Obj.Color

PROCEDURE ox_rot270(Obj, Result):
  R0 <- min row; C0 <- min col; C1 <- max col; W <- C1-C0+1
  Result.Cells <- [r(R0+(W-1)-Lc, C0+Lr) FOR r(R,C) IN Obj.Cells,
                   Lr<-R-R0, Lc<-C-C0]
  Result.Color <- Obj.Color

Section 174.4: Reflections

PROCEDURE ox_reflect_h(Obj, Result):
  (R0, _, R1, _) <- ox_bbox(Obj)
  Result.Cells <- [r(R0+R1-R, C) FOR r(R,C) IN Obj.Cells]
  Result.Color <- Obj.Color

PROCEDURE ox_reflect_v(Obj, Result):
  (_, C0, _, C1) <- ox_bbox(Obj)
  Result.Cells <- [r(R, C0+C1-C) FOR r(R,C) IN Obj.Cells]
  Result.Color <- Obj.Color

Section 174.5: Set Algebra

PROCEDURE ox_merge(Obj1, Obj2, Result):
  Result.Color <- Obj1.Color
  Result.Cells <- sort(Obj1.Cells + Obj2.Cells)  // sort deduplicates

PROCEDURE ox_diff(Obj1, Obj2, Result):
  Result.Color <- Obj1.Color
  Result.Cells <- [C FOR C IN Obj1.Cells IF C NOT IN Obj2.Cells]

PROCEDURE ox_intersect(Obj1, Obj2, Result):
  Result.Color <- Obj1.Color
  Result.Cells <- [C FOR C IN Obj1.Cells IF C IN Obj2.Cells]

Section 174.6: Scale Up

PROCEDURE ox_scale_up(Obj, Factor, Result):
  REQUIRE Factor > 0
  Result.Color <- Obj.Color
  Result.Cells <- [r(R*F+DR, C*F+DC) FOR r(R,C) IN Obj.Cells,
                   DR IN [0,F-1], DC IN [0,F-1]]

Part 175: Shrink Pack Pseudocode (sk_*, Layer 164)

Section 175.1: Block Dimensions

PROCEDURE dn_block_dims(Grid, N, BI, BJ):
  H <- length(Grid)
  W <- length(Grid[0])
  BI <- H // N
  BJ <- W // N

Section 175.2: Block Cells

PROCEDURE dn_block_cells(N, I, J, Cells):
  R0 <- I * N; R1 <- R0 + N - 1
  C0 <- J * N; C1 <- C0 + N - 1
  Cells <- [r(R,C) FOR R IN [R0..R1], C IN [C0..C1]]

Section 175.3: Block Color

PROCEDURE dn_block_color(Grid, N, I, J, Color):
  Cells <- dn_block_cells(N, I, J)
  Vals <- [Grid[R][C] FOR r(R,C) IN Cells]
  Unique <- sort(Vals)
  REQUIRE len(Unique) = 1
  Color <- Unique[0]

Section 175.4: Block Majority

PROCEDURE dn_block_majority(Grid, N, I, J, Color):
  Cells <- dn_block_cells(N, I, J)
  Vals <- [Grid[R][C] FOR r(R,C) IN Cells]
  Unique <- sort(Vals)
  Counts <- [(count(V, Vals), V) FOR V IN Unique]
  Color <- V IN argmax(Counts)

Section 175.5: Is Blocky

PROCEDURE dn_is_blocky(Grid, N):
  (BI, BJ) <- dn_block_dims(Grid, N)
  REQUIRE BI > 0, BJ > 0
  FOR I IN [0..BI-1]:
    FOR J IN [0..BJ-1]:
      REQUIRE dn_block_color(Grid, N, I, J) succeeds

Section 175.6: Shrink

PROCEDURE dn_shrink(Grid, N, Small):
  (BI, BJ) <- dn_block_dims(Grid, N)
  Small <- [[dn_block_majority(Grid, N, I, J) FOR J IN [0..BJ-1]] FOR I IN [0..BI-1]]

PROCEDURE dn_shrink_strict(Grid, N, Small):
  REQUIRE dn_is_blocky(Grid, N)
  (BI, BJ) <- dn_block_dims(Grid, N)
  Small <- [[dn_block_color(Grid, N, I, J) FOR J IN [0..BJ-1]] FOR I IN [0..BI-1]]

Section 175.7: Find Scale

PROCEDURE dn_find_scale(Grid, N):
  H <- length(Grid); W <- length(Grid[0])
  REQUIRE H > 1, W > 1
  FOR N IN [2..H]:
    IF H mod N = 0 AND W mod N = 0 AND dn_is_blocky(Grid, N):
      RETURN N

Section 175.8: Object Shrink and Scale Factor

PROCEDURE dn_obj_shrink(obj(Color, Cells), N, Result):
  REQUIRE N > 0
  Raw <- [r(R//N, C//N) FOR r(R,C) IN Cells]
  Result <- obj(Color, sort(Raw))

PROCEDURE dn_scale_factor(Obj1, Obj2, N):
  Norm1 <- normalize_to_origin(Obj1.Cells)
  FOR N IN [2..30]:
    Shrunken <- dn_obj_shrink(Obj2, N)
    Norm2 <- normalize_to_origin(Shrunken.Cells)
    IF Norm1 = Norm2: RETURN N

Part 176: Objmorph Pack Pseudocode (om_*, Layer 165)

Section 176.1: Neighborhood Generation

PROCEDURE om_neighbors4(r(R, C), Neighbors):
  Neighbors <- [r(R-1,C), r(R+1,C), r(R,C-1), r(R,C+1)]

PROCEDURE om_neighbors8(r(R, C), Neighbors):
  Neighbors <- [r(R-1,C-1), r(R-1,C), r(R-1,C+1),
                r(R,  C-1),            r(R,  C+1),
                r(R+1,C-1), r(R+1,C), r(R+1,C+1)]

Section 176.2: Boundary and Interior

PROCEDURE om_boundary4(obj(Color, Cells), obj(Color, Boundary)):
  S <- sort(Cells)
  Boundary <- [r(R,C) IN S WHERE NOT ALL(n IN om_neighbors4(r(R,C)) -> n IN S)]

PROCEDURE om_interior4(obj(Color, Cells), obj(Color, Interior)):
  S <- sort(Cells)
  Interior <- [r(R,C) IN S WHERE ALL(n IN om_neighbors4(r(R,C)) -> n IN S)]

PROCEDURE om_boundary8(obj(Color, Cells), obj(Color, Boundary)):
  S <- sort(Cells)
  Boundary <- [r(R,C) IN S WHERE NOT ALL(n IN om_neighbors8(r(R,C)) -> n IN S)]

PROCEDURE om_interior8(obj(Color, Cells), obj(Color, Interior)):
  S <- sort(Cells)
  Interior <- [r(R,C) IN S WHERE ALL(n IN om_neighbors8(r(R,C)) -> n IN S)]

Section 176.3: Dilation and Erosion

PROCEDURE om_dilate4(obj(Color, Cells), obj(Color, Dilated)):
  S <- sort(Cells)
  NewCells <- FLATTEN([om_neighbors4(c) FOR c IN S])
  Dilated <- sort(S ++ NewCells)

PROCEDURE om_erode4(Obj, Eroded):
  Eroded <- om_interior4(Obj)

PROCEDURE om_dilate8(obj(Color, Cells), obj(Color, Dilated)):
  S <- sort(Cells)
  NewCells <- FLATTEN([om_neighbors8(c) FOR c IN S])
  Dilated <- sort(S ++ NewCells)

PROCEDURE om_erode8(Obj, Eroded):
  Eroded <- om_interior8(Obj)

Section 176.4: Iterated Operations

PROCEDURE om_dilate4_n(Obj, 0, Obj): RETURN Obj
PROCEDURE om_dilate4_n(Obj, N, Result):
  REQUIRE N > 0
  Step <- om_dilate4(Obj)
  Result <- om_dilate4_n(Step, N-1)

PROCEDURE om_erode4_n(Obj, 0, Obj): RETURN Obj
PROCEDURE om_erode4_n(Obj, N, Result):
  REQUIRE N > 0
  Step <- om_erode4(Obj)
  Result <- om_erode4_n(Step, N-1)

Section 176.5: Compound Operations

PROCEDURE om_open4(Obj, Result):
  Eroded <- om_erode4(Obj)
  Result <- om_dilate4(Eroded)

PROCEDURE om_close4(Obj, Result):
  Dilated <- om_dilate4(Obj)
  Result <- om_erode4(Dilated)

Part 177: Voronoi Pack Pseudocode (vn_*, Layer 166)

Section 177.1: Source Cell Collection

PROCEDURE vn_non_bg_cells(Grid, Bg, Cells):
  Cells <- sort([r(R,C) FOR r(R,C) IN grid_positions(Grid) WHERE Grid[R][C] != Bg])

PROCEDURE vn_non_bg_colors(Grid, Bg, Colors):
  Colors <- sort([Grid[R][C] FOR r(R,C) IN grid_positions(Grid) WHERE Grid[R][C] != Bg])

Section 177.2: Nearest Distance and Color

PROCEDURE vn_nearest_dist(Grid, Bg, R, C, Dist):
  NonBg <- vn_non_bg_cells(Grid, Bg)
  Dists <- [|NR-R| + |NC-C| FOR r(NR,NC) IN NonBg]
  Dist <- min(Dists)

PROCEDURE vn_nearest_color(Grid, Bg, R, C, Color):
  Pairs <- [(|NR-R|+|NC-C|)-V FOR r(NR,NC) at value V in Grid WHERE V != Bg]
  Color <- V IN sort(Pairs)[0]

Section 177.3: Painting and Distance Transform

PROCEDURE vn_paint_bg(Grid, Bg, Painted):
  FOR each cell (R,C) in Grid:
    IF Grid[R][C] != Bg: Painted[R][C] <- Grid[R][C]
    ELSE: Painted[R][C] <- vn_nearest_color(Grid, Bg, R, C)

PROCEDURE vn_dist_map(Grid, Bg, DGrid):
  NonBg <- vn_non_bg_cells(Grid, Bg)
  FOR each cell (R,C) in Grid:
    IF Grid[R][C] != Bg: DGrid[R][C] <- 0
    ELSE: DGrid[R][C] <- min([|NR-R|+|NC-C| FOR r(NR,NC) IN NonBg])

Section 177.4: Voronoi Regions

PROCEDURE vn_region_cells(Grid, Bg, Color, Cells):
  Cells <- sort([r(R,C) FOR r(R,C) Bg cell WHERE vn_nearest_color(Grid,Bg,R,C)=Color])

PROCEDURE vn_regions(Grid, Bg, Pairs):
  Colors <- vn_non_bg_colors(Grid, Bg)
  Pairs <- [Color-vn_region_cells(Grid,Bg,Color) FOR Color IN Colors]

Section 177.5: Distance Queries

PROCEDURE vn_max_dist(Grid, Bg, MaxDist):
  Dists <- [vn_nearest_dist(Grid,Bg,R,C) FOR r(R,C) Bg cell]
  MaxDist <- max(Dists)

PROCEDURE vn_at_dist(Grid, Bg, D, Cells):
  Cells <- sort([r(R,C) FOR r(R,C) Bg cell WHERE vn_nearest_dist(Grid,Bg,R,C)=D])

PROCEDURE vn_within_dist(Grid, Bg, D, Cells):
  Cells <- sort([r(R,C) FOR r(R,C) Bg cell WHERE vn_nearest_dist(Grid,Bg,R,C)<=D])

Section 177.6: Medial Axis and Expansion

PROCEDURE vn_medial(Grid, Bg, Cells):
  Cells <- sort([r(R,C) FOR r(R,C) Bg cell
                 WHERE |{V : r(NR,NC) non-Bg at V, dist(R,C,NR,NC)=vn_nearest_dist(...)}| >= 2])

PROCEDURE vn_expand1(Grid, Bg, Color, Cells):
  ColorCells <- {r(R,C) : Grid[R][C]=Color}
  Cells <- sort([r(BR,BC) : r(BR,BC) Bg, r(CR,CC) IN ColorCells,
                 4-adjacent(r(BR,BC), r(CR,CC))])

PROCEDURE vn_expand_n(Grid, Bg, Color, N, Cells):
  ColorCells <- {r(CR,CC) : Grid[CR][CC]=Color}
  Cells <- sort([r(BR,BC) : r(BR,BC) Bg,
                 r(CR,CC) IN ColorCells,
                 |BR-CR|+|BC-CC| <= N])

Part 178: Objcomp Pack Pseudocode (oc_*, Layer 167)

Section 178.1: Touching Test

PROCEDURE oc_touches(obj(_, Cells1), obj(_, Cells2)):
  FOR r(R1,C1) IN Cells1:
    FOR r(R2,C2) IN Cells2:
      IF (R1=R2 AND |C1-C2|=1) OR (C1=C2 AND |R1-R2|=1):
        RETURN true
  RETURN false

Section 178.2: Pair and Adjacency Queries

PROCEDURE oc_touching_pairs(Objs, Pairs):
  Pairs <- [(Objs[I], Objs[J]) FOR I < J WHERE oc_touches(Objs[I], Objs[J])]

PROCEDURE oc_adj_list(Objs, AdjList):
  AdjList <- [Obj-[N FOR N IN Objs WHERE N != Obj AND oc_touches(Obj,N)]
              FOR Obj IN Objs]

PROCEDURE oc_degree(Obj, Objs, N):
  N <- |{O IN Objs : O != Obj AND oc_touches(Obj, O)}|

Section 178.3: Isolation and Connectivity

PROCEDURE oc_isolated(Objs, Isolated):
  Isolated <- [Obj IN Objs WHERE NOT EXISTS Other IN Objs: Other!=Obj AND oc_touches(Obj,Other)]

PROCEDURE oc_connected(Obj, Objs, Component):
  Queue <- [Obj]; Visited <- []
  WHILE Queue != []:
    H <- dequeue(Queue)
    IF H IN Visited: continue
    Visited <- Visited + [H]
    Queue <- Queue + [N IN Objs WHERE N != H AND N NOT IN Visited AND oc_touches(H,N)]
  Component <- sort(Visited)

PROCEDURE oc_components(Objs, Components):
  Todo <- Objs; Components <- []
  WHILE Todo != []:
    H <- head(Todo)
    Comp <- oc_connected(H, Todo)
    Components <- Components + [Comp]
    Todo <- Todo \ Comp

Section 178.4: Component and Degree Aggregates

PROCEDURE oc_num_components(Objs, N): N <- |oc_components(Objs)|
PROCEDURE oc_largest_component(Objs, C): C <- argmax_size(oc_components(Objs))
PROCEDURE oc_smallest_component(Objs, C): C <- argmin_size(oc_components(Objs))
PROCEDURE oc_singleton_components(Objs, S): S <- [C IN oc_components(Objs) WHERE |C|=1]
PROCEDURE oc_shared_components(Objs, G): G <- [C IN oc_components(Objs) WHERE |C|>1]
PROCEDURE oc_max_degree(Objs, D): D <- max([oc_degree(O, Objs) FOR O IN Objs])
PROCEDURE oc_sort_by_degree(Objs, Sorted): Sorted <- keysort([oc_degree(O,Objs)-O FOR O IN Objs])

Part 179: Wavefront BFS Propagation Pack (wf_*, Layer 168)

PROCEDURE wf_passable(Grid, PassColor, Cells):
  Cells <- sort(findall(r(R,C) | Grid[R][C] = PassColor))

PROCEDURE wf_bfs(Grid, Seeds, PassColor, DistPairs):
  Queue <- [0-S | S IN Seeds]
  Enqueued <- sort(Seeds)
  DistPairs <- wf_bfs_(Queue, Grid, PassColor, Enqueued, [])

PROCEDURE wf_bfs_([], Grid, PassColor, Enqueued, Acc):
  RETURN msort(Acc)
PROCEDURE wf_bfs_([D-r(R,C)|Queue], Grid, PassColor, Enqueued, Acc):
  D1 <- D + 1
  Neighbors <- findall(r(NR,NC) | 4adj(R,C,NR,NC) AND Grid[NR][NC]=PassColor AND r(NR,NC) NOT IN Enqueued)
  NewQueue <- Queue ++ [D1-N | N IN Neighbors]
  NewEnqueued <- Neighbors ++ Enqueued
  RETURN wf_bfs_(NewQueue, Grid, PassColor, NewEnqueued, [D-r(R,C)|Acc])

PROCEDURE wf_reachable(Grid, Seeds, PassColor, Cells):
  DP <- wf_bfs(Grid, Seeds, PassColor)
  Cells <- sort(findall(Cell | _-Cell IN DP))

PROCEDURE wf_unreachable(Grid, Seeds, PassColor, Cells):
  All <- wf_passable(Grid, PassColor)
  Reached <- wf_reachable(Grid, Seeds, PassColor)
  Cells <- subtract(All, Reached)

PROCEDURE wf_at_dist(DistPairs, D, Cells):
  Cells <- sort(findall(Cell | D-Cell IN DistPairs))

PROCEDURE wf_within_dist(DistPairs, MaxD, Cells):
  Cells <- sort(findall(Cell | D-Cell IN DistPairs AND D =< MaxD))

PROCEDURE wf_dist_of(DistPairs, Cell, D):
  memberchk(D-Cell, DistPairs)

PROCEDURE wf_max_dist(DistPairs, MaxD):
  MaxD <- max_list(findall(D | D-_ IN DistPairs))

PROCEDURE wf_all_dists(DistPairs, Dists):
  Dists <- sort(findall(D | D-_ IN DistPairs))

PROCEDURE wf_path_exists(Grid, CellA, CellB, PassColor):
  DP <- wf_bfs(Grid, [CellA], PassColor)
  memberchk(_-CellB, DP)

PROCEDURE wf_paint_bg(Grid, Seeds, PassColor, MaxD, NewGrid):
  DP <- wf_bfs(Grid, Seeds, PassColor)
  NewGrid <- rebuild Grid: if Grid[R][C]=PassColor and D-r(R,C) IN DP then min(D,MaxD) else Grid[R][C]

PROCEDURE wf_multi_wave(Grid, ColoredSeeds, PassColor, Painted):
  ColorDPs <- [Color-wf_bfs(Grid, Seeds, PassColor) | Color-Seeds IN ColoredSeeds]
  Painted <- rebuild Grid: if Grid[R][C]=PassColor then WinColor from sort([D-C | C-DP IN ColorDPs, D-r(R,C) IN DP]) else Grid[R][C]

PROCEDURE wf_collision(Grid, ColoredSeeds, PassColor, Cells):
  ColorDPs <- [Color-wf_bfs(Grid, Seeds, PassColor) | Color-Seeds IN ColoredSeeds]
  Cells <- sort(findall(r(R,C) | r(R,C) IN wf_passable AND sort([D-Color | Color-DP IN ColorDPs, D-r(R,C) IN DP]) = [MinD-_|Rest] AND MinD-_ IN Rest))

PROCEDURE wf_enclosed(Grid, PassColor, Cells):
  BorderSeeds <- PassColor cells on grid border (R=0 OR R=NR-1 OR C=0 OR C=NC-1)
  DP <- wf_bfs(Grid, BorderSeeds, PassColor)
  Exterior <- findall(Cell | _-Cell IN DP)
  Cells <- subtract(wf_passable(Grid,PassColor), Exterior)

Part 180: Object Chain Analysis Pack (ch_*, Layer 169)

PROCEDURE ch_touches(O1, O2):
  member(r(R1,C1), cells(O1)), member(r(R2,C2), cells(O2))
  (R1=R2 AND |C1-C2|=1) OR (C1=C2 AND |R1-R2|=1); CUT

PROCEDURE ch_degree(Obj, Objs, N):
  N <- |[O IN Objs WHERE O!=Obj AND ch_touches(Obj,O)]|

PROCEDURE ch_is_chain([]) -> true
PROCEDURE ch_is_chain([_]) -> true
PROCEDURE ch_is_chain([O1,O2]) -> ch_touches(O1,O2)
PROCEDURE ch_is_chain(Objs) WHERE |Objs|>=3:
  Degs <- [ch_degree(O,Objs) FOR O IN Objs]
  REQUIRE: no D IN Degs where D > 2
  REQUIRE: no 0 IN Degs
  REQUIRE: |[D IN Degs WHERE D=1]| = 2

PROCEDURE ch_has_cycle(Objs):
  |Objs| >= 3
  Degs <- [ch_degree(O,Objs) FOR O IN Objs]
  REQUIRE: all D IN Degs: D = 2

PROCEDURE ch_endpoints(Objs, E1, E2):
  [E1,E2] <- [O IN Objs WHERE ch_degree(O,Objs)=1]

PROCEDURE ch_walk_(Current, Objs, Visited):
  Neighbors <- [N IN Objs WHERE N!=Current AND N NOT IN Visited AND ch_touches(Current,N)]
  IF Neighbors=[]: RETURN [Current]
  IF Neighbors=[Next]: RETURN [Current | ch_walk_(Next, Objs, [Current|Visited])]

PROCEDURE ch_linearize(Objs, Ordered):
  E1 <- first element of ch_endpoints(Objs)
  Ordered <- ch_walk_(E1, Objs, [])

PROCEDURE ch_from_endpoint(Objs, Start, Ordered):
  REQUIRE memberchk(Start, Objs)
  Ordered <- ch_walk_(Start, Objs, [])

PROCEDURE ch_nth(Ordered, N, Obj): Obj <- Ordered[N]  (0-based)

PROCEDURE ch_color_seq(Ordered, Colors):
  Colors <- [color(O) FOR O IN Ordered]

PROCEDURE ch_sub(Ordered, I, J, Sub):
  Sub <- Ordered[I..J]  (0-based, inclusive)

PROCEDURE ch_reverse(Ordered, Rev): Rev <- reverse(Ordered)

PROCEDURE ch_length(Objs, N): N <- |Objs|

PROCEDURE ch_is_linear_path([]) -> true
PROCEDURE ch_is_linear_path([_]) -> true
PROCEDURE ch_is_linear_path([O1,O2|Rest]):
  ch_touches(O1,O2) AND ch_is_linear_path([O2|Rest])

PROCEDURE ch_direction(Ordered, h):
  AllRs <- [min_row(O) FOR O IN Ordered]; all equal; CUT
PROCEDURE ch_direction(Ordered, v):
  AllCs <- [min_col(O) FOR O IN Ordered]; all equal; CUT
PROCEDURE ch_direction(_, other)

Part 181: Object Symmetry Analysis Pack Pseudocode (os_*, Layer 170)

PROCEDURE os_bbox(Obj, MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC):
  Rs <- [R FOR r(R,_) IN cells(Obj)]
  Cs <- [C FOR r(_,C) IN cells(Obj)]
  MinR <- min(Rs); MaxR <- max(Rs)
  MinC <- min(Cs); MaxC <- max(Cs)

PROCEDURE os_normalize(obj(Color, Cells), NormObj):
  (MinR, MinC, _, _) <- os_bbox(Obj)
  NormCells <- [r(R-MinR, C-MinC) FOR r(R,C) IN Cells]
  NormObj <- obj(Color, NormCells)

PROCEDURE os_translate(obj(Color, Cells), DR, DC, Moved):
  Moved <- obj(Color, [r(R+DR, C+DC) FOR r(R,C) IN Cells])

PROCEDURE os_reflect_h(Obj, Reflected):
  (_, MinC, _, MaxC) <- os_bbox(Obj)
  Reflected <- obj(color(Obj), [r(R, MinC+MaxC-C) FOR r(R,C) IN cells(Obj)])

PROCEDURE os_reflect_v(Obj, Reflected):
  (MinR, _, MaxR, _) <- os_bbox(Obj)
  Reflected <- obj(color(Obj), [r(MinR+MaxR-R, C) FOR r(R,C) IN cells(Obj)])

PROCEDURE os_rotate180(Obj, Rotated):
  (MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC) <- os_bbox(Obj)
  Rotated <- obj(color(Obj), [r(MinR+MaxR-R, MinC+MaxC-C) FOR r(R,C) IN cells(Obj)])

PROCEDURE os_rotate90(Obj, Rotated):
  (_, MinC, MaxR, _) <- os_bbox(Obj)
  Rotated <- obj(color(Obj), [r(C-MinC, MaxR-R) FOR r(R,C) IN cells(Obj)])
  -- CW rotation normalized to origin: row <- col-MinC, col <- MaxR-row

PROCEDURE os_cells_sorted_(Obj, Sorted): Sorted <- msort(cells(Obj))

PROCEDURE os_is_hsymm(Obj):
  REQUIRE msort(cells(os_reflect_h(Obj))) = msort(cells(Obj))

PROCEDURE os_is_vsymm(Obj):
  REQUIRE msort(cells(os_reflect_v(Obj))) = msort(cells(Obj))

PROCEDURE os_is_rot180(Obj):
  REQUIRE msort(cells(os_rotate180(Obj))) = msort(cells(Obj))

PROCEDURE os_is_rot90(Obj):
  Norm <- os_normalize(Obj)
  RotNorm <- os_normalize(os_rotate90(Norm))
  REQUIRE msort(cells(Norm)) = msort(cells(RotNorm))

PROCEDURE os_has_symmetry(Obj):
  os_is_hsymm(Obj) OR os_is_vsymm(Obj) OR os_is_rot180(Obj) OR os_is_rot90(Obj)

PROCEDURE os_symmetries(Obj, List):
  List <- [Sym IN [h, v, rot180, rot90] WHERE symmetry_holds(Obj, Sym)]

PROCEDURE os_d4_orbit_(Obj):
  N <- os_normalize(Obj)
  R1 <- os_normalize(os_rotate90(N)); R2 <- os_normalize(os_rotate90(R1))
  R3 <- os_normalize(os_rotate90(R2))
  F <- os_normalize(os_reflect_h(N)); F1 <- os_normalize(os_rotate90(F))
  F2 <- os_normalize(os_rotate90(F1)); F3 <- os_normalize(os_rotate90(F2))
  YIELD each of [N, R1, R2, R3, F, F1, F2, F3]

PROCEDURE os_equivalent(Obj1, Obj2):
  S1 <- msort(cells(os_normalize(Obj1)))
  FOR Variant IN os_d4_orbit_(Obj2):
    IF msort(cells(Variant)) = S1: RETURN true; CUT

Part 182: Object Shape Classification Pack Pseudocode (ob_*, Layer 171)

PRIVATE PROCEDURE ob_bbox_(Obj, MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC):
  Rs <- [R FOR r(R,_) IN cells(Obj)]; Cs <- [C FOR r(_,C) IN cells(Obj)]
  MinR <- min(Rs); MaxR <- max(Rs); MinC <- min(Cs); MaxC <- max(Cs)

PROCEDURE ob_bbox_h(Obj, H): H <- MaxR - MinR + 1  [from ob_bbox_]
PROCEDURE ob_bbox_w(Obj, W): W <- MaxC - MinC + 1  [from ob_bbox_]
PROCEDURE ob_bbox_area(Obj, Area): Area <- H * W  [ob_bbox_h * ob_bbox_w]

PROCEDURE ob_is_rect(Obj):
  N <- |cells(Obj)|; Area <- ob_bbox_area(Obj)
  REQUIRE N = Area

PROCEDURE ob_is_hline(Obj): REQUIRE ob_bbox_h(Obj) = 1
PROCEDURE ob_is_vline(Obj): REQUIRE ob_bbox_w(Obj) = 1
PROCEDURE ob_is_single(Obj): REQUIRE ob_bbox_h(Obj) = 1 AND ob_bbox_w(Obj) = 1
PROCEDURE ob_is_square_bbox(Obj): REQUIRE ob_bbox_h(Obj) = ob_bbox_w(Obj)

PROCEDURE ob_holes(Obj, HoleCells):
  (MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC) <- ob_bbox_(Obj)
  HoleCells <- [r(R,C) FOR R IN [MinR..MaxR], C IN [MinC..MaxC]
                WHERE r(R,C) NOT IN cells(Obj)]

PROCEDURE ob_n_holes(Obj, N): N <- |ob_holes(Obj)|
PROCEDURE ob_is_hollow(Obj): REQUIRE ob_n_holes(Obj) > 0

PROCEDURE ob_is_frame(Obj):
  (MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC) <- ob_bbox_(Obj)
  H <- MaxR-MinR+1; W <- MaxC-MinC+1
  REQUIRE H >= 3 AND W >= 3
  REQUIRE FORALL border cell r(R,C): r(R,C) IN cells(Obj)
  REQUIRE NO interior cell r(R,C) IN cells(Obj)

PROCEDURE ob_cell_exposed_(r(R,C), Cells, N):
  N <- |{d IN [d(-1,0),d(1,0),d(0,-1),d(0,1)] WHERE r(R+DR,C+DC) NOT IN Cells}|

PROCEDURE ob_perimeter(Obj, P):
  P <- SUM [ob_cell_exposed_(Cell, cells(Obj)) FOR Cell IN cells(Obj)]

PROCEDURE ob_dense_hull(Obj, HullObj):
  (MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC) <- ob_bbox_(Obj)
  Hull <- [r(R,C) FOR R IN [MinR..MaxR], C IN [MinC..MaxC]]
  HullObj <- obj(color(Obj), Hull)

Part 183: Objrel Pack Pseudocode (or_*, Layer 172)

Section 183.1: Private Helpers

PROCEDURE or_centroid_(Obj, CR, CC):
  Rs <- [R FOR r(R,_) IN cells(Obj)]
  Cs <- [C FOR r(_,C) IN cells(Obj)]
  N  <- len(Rs)
  CR <- sum(Rs) / N
  CC <- sum(Cs) / N

PROCEDURE or_bbox_(Obj, MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC):
  Rs <- [R FOR r(R,_) IN cells(Obj)]
  Cs <- [C FOR r(_,C) IN cells(Obj)]
  (MinR, MaxR) <- (min(Rs), max(Rs))
  (MinC, MaxC) <- (min(Cs), max(Cs))

PROCEDURE or_dir_(DR, DC, Dir):
  IF DR=0 AND DC>0: Dir <- e
  IF DR=0 AND DC<0: Dir <- w
  IF DR>0 AND DC=0: Dir <- s
  IF DR<0 AND DC=0: Dir <- n
  IF DR>0 AND DC>0: Dir <- se
  IF DR>0 AND DC<0: Dir <- sw
  IF DR<0 AND DC>0: Dir <- ne
  IF DR<0 AND DC<0: Dir <- nw
  ELSE: Dir <- same

Section 183.2: Overlap and Set Operations

PROCEDURE or_overlap(Obj1, Obj2):
  FIND Cell IN cells(Obj1) WHERE Cell IN cells(Obj2)
  CUT on first match

PROCEDURE or_shared_cells(Obj1, Obj2, Shared):
  Shared <- [C FOR C IN cells(Obj1) WHERE C IN cells(Obj2)]

PROCEDURE or_n_shared(Obj1, Obj2, N):
  N <- len(or_shared_cells(Obj1, Obj2))

PROCEDURE or_touch4(Obj1, Obj2):
  REQUIRE NOT or_overlap(Obj1, Obj2)
  FIND r(R1,C1) IN cells(Obj1), r(R2,C2) IN cells(Obj2)
    WHERE abs(R1-R2) + abs(C1-C2) = 1
  CUT on first match

PROCEDURE or_touch8(Obj1, Obj2):
  REQUIRE NOT or_overlap(Obj1, Obj2)
  FIND r(R1,C1) IN cells(Obj1), r(R2,C2) IN cells(Obj2)
    WHERE max(abs(R1-R2), abs(C1-C2)) = 1
  CUT on first match

PROCEDURE or_contains(Obj1, Obj2):
  FOR EACH C IN cells(Obj2): REQUIRE C IN cells(Obj1)

PROCEDURE or_union_cells(Obj1, Obj2, Union):
  Union <- sort(cells(Obj1) ++ cells(Obj2))

Section 183.3: Distance and Direction

PROCEDURE or_dist(Obj1, Obj2, D):
  (R1,C1) <- or_centroid_(Obj1)
  (R2,C2) <- or_centroid_(Obj2)
  D <- sqrt((R2-R1)^2 + (C2-C1)^2)

PROCEDURE or_manhattan(Obj1, Obj2, D):
  (R1,C1) <- or_centroid_(Obj1)
  (R2,C2) <- or_centroid_(Obj2)
  D <- abs(R2-R1) + abs(C2-C1)

PROCEDURE or_direction(Obj1, Obj2, Dir):
  (R1,C1) <- or_centroid_(Obj1)
  (R2,C2) <- or_centroid_(Obj2)
  DR <- R2-R1; DC <- C2-C1
  Dir <- or_dir_(DR, DC)

Section 183.4: Alignment and Gaps

PROCEDURE or_aligned_h(Obj1, Obj2):
  R1 <- centroid_row(Obj1); R2 <- centroid_row(Obj2)
  REQUIRE R1 = R2

PROCEDURE or_aligned_v(Obj1, Obj2):
  C1 <- centroid_col(Obj1); C2 <- centroid_col(Obj2)
  REQUIRE C1 = C2

PROCEDURE or_gap_rows(Obj1, Obj2, G):
  (MinR1, MaxR1) <- row_extremes(bbox(Obj1))
  (MinR2, MaxR2) <- row_extremes(bbox(Obj2))
  G <- max(0, max(MinR1,MinR2) - min(MaxR1,MaxR2) - 1)

PROCEDURE or_gap_cols(Obj1, Obj2, G):
  (MinC1, MaxC1) <- col_extremes(bbox(Obj1))
  (MinC2, MaxC2) <- col_extremes(bbox(Obj2))
  G <- max(0, max(MinC1,MinC2) - min(MaxC1,MaxC2) - 1)

Part 184: Objfilter Pack Pseudocode (of_*, Layer 173)

Section 184.1: Private Helpers

PROCEDURE of_size_(Obj, N):
  N <- len(cells(Obj))

PROCEDURE of_bbox_(Obj, MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC):
  Rs <- [R FOR r(R,_) IN cells(Obj)]
  Cs <- [C FOR r(_,C) IN cells(Obj)]
  (MinR, MaxR) <- (min(Rs), max(Rs))
  (MinC, MaxC) <- (min(Cs), max(Cs))

PROCEDURE of_is_rect_(Obj):
  N <- of_size_(Obj)
  (MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC) <- of_bbox_(Obj)
  REQUIRE N = (MaxR-MinR+1) * (MaxC-MinC+1)

PROCEDURE of_is_hline_(Obj):
  (MinR, _, MaxR, _) <- of_bbox_(Obj)
  REQUIRE MinR = MaxR

PROCEDURE of_is_vline_(Obj):
  (_, MinC, _, MaxC) <- of_bbox_(Obj)
  REQUIRE MinC = MaxC

PROCEDURE of_is_single_(Obj):
  REQUIRE of_size_(Obj) = 1

PROCEDURE of_is_hollow_(Obj):
  N <- of_size_(Obj)
  (MinR, MinC, MaxR, MaxC) <- of_bbox_(Obj)
  REQUIRE N < (MaxR-MinR+1) * (MaxC-MinC+1)

PROCEDURE of_largest_acc_([], _, Best, Best): base case
PROCEDURE of_largest_acc_([H|T], BestN, BestObj, Result):
  N <- of_size_(H)
  IF N > BestN: recurse(T, N, H, Result)
  ELSE: recurse(T, BestN, BestObj, Result)

PROCEDURE of_smallest_acc_([], _, Best, Best): base case
PROCEDURE of_smallest_acc_([H|T], BestN, BestObj, Result):
  N <- of_size_(H)
  IF N < BestN: recurse(T, N, H, Result)
  ELSE: recurse(T, BestN, BestObj, Result)

Section 184.2: Color Filters

PROCEDURE of_by_color(Objs, Color, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE color(O) = Color]

PROCEDURE of_not_color(Objs, Color, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE color(O) != Color]

Section 184.3: Size Filters

PROCEDURE of_exact_size(Objs, N, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE of_size_(O) = N]

PROCEDURE of_min_size(Objs, N, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE of_size_(O) >= N]

PROCEDURE of_max_size(Objs, N, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE of_size_(O) <= N]

Section 184.4: Shape Filters

PROCEDURE of_is_rect(Objs, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE of_is_rect_(O)]

PROCEDURE of_is_hline(Objs, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE of_is_hline_(O)]

PROCEDURE of_is_vline(Objs, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE of_is_vline_(O)]

PROCEDURE of_is_single(Objs, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE of_is_single_(O)]

PROCEDURE of_is_hollow(Objs, Filtered):
  Filtered <- [O FOR O IN Objs WHERE of_is_hollow_(O)]

Section 184.5: Aggregate Selection

PROCEDURE of_largest([H|T], Largest):
  N <- of_size_(H)
  Largest <- of_largest_acc_(T, N, H)

PROCEDURE of_smallest([H|T], Smallest):
  N <- of_size_(H)
  Smallest <- of_smallest_acc_(T, N, H)

Section 184.6: Generic Filter and Partition

PROCEDURE of_filter(Objs, Goal, Filtered):
  Filtered <- include(Goal, Objs)  [= SWI include/3]

PROCEDURE of_partition(Objs, Goal, In, Out):
  (In, Out) <- partition(Goal, Objs)  [= SWI partition/4]

Part 185: Canvas Pack Pseudocode (cv_*, Layer 174)

cv_blank(H, W, Bg, Grid):
    H1 = H-1; W1 = W-1
    Grid = findall(Row, (between(0,H1,_), Row=findall(Bg,between(0,W1,_),_)), _)

cv_size(Grid, H, W):
    H = length(Grid)
    W = length(Grid[0])

cv_paint(Grid, obj(Color, Cells), Grid2):
    rebuild each row R: for each col C, if r(R,C) in Cells then Color else original

cv_paint_all(Grid, [], Grid). (base)
cv_paint_all(Grid, [Obj|Rest], Grid2):
    Grid1 = cv_paint(Grid, Obj); Grid2 = cv_paint_all(Grid1, Rest)

cv_paint_at(Grid, obj(Color,Cells), DR, DC, Grid2):
    Cells2 = [r(R+DR,C+DC) | r(R,C) <- Cells]
    cv_paint_cells_(Grid, Cells2, Color, Grid2)

cv_paint_clip(Grid, obj(Color,Cells), Grid2):
    H,W = cv_dims_(Grid); ClipCells = filter in-bounds from Cells
    cv_paint_cells_(Grid, ClipCells, Color, Grid2)

cv_paint_bg(Grid, obj(Color,Cells), Bg, Grid2):
    BgCells = filter cells where Grid[R][C]=Bg
    cv_paint_cells_(Grid, BgCells, Color, Grid2)

cv_erase(Grid, obj(_,Cells), Bg, Grid2):
    rebuild each row R: for each col C, if r(R,C) in Cells then Bg else original

cv_extract(Grid, Color, obj(Color,Cells)):
    Cells = findall(r(R,C), Grid[R][C]=Color, _)

cv_extract_all(Grid, Bg, Objs):
    Triples = findall(R-C-V, Grid[R][C]!=Bg, _)
    Colors = sort(distinct values in Triples)
    Objs = [obj(Color, findall(r(R,C), R-C-Color in Triples)) | Color <- Colors]

cv_render(H, W, Bg, Objs, Grid):
    Blank = cv_blank(H,W,Bg); Grid = cv_paint_all(Blank, Objs)

cv_move(Grid, Obj, DR, DC, Bg, Grid2):
    Grid1 = cv_erase(Grid, Obj, Bg); Grid2 = cv_paint_at(Grid1, Obj, DR, DC)

cv_stamp(obj(Color,Cells), Bg, Patch):
    MinR,MaxR,MinC,MaxC = bbox of Cells
    H=MaxR-MinR+1; W=MaxC-MinC+1
    NormCells = [r(R-MinR, C-MinC) | r(R,C) <- Cells]
    Blank = cv_blank(H,W,Bg); Patch = cv_paint_cells_(Blank, NormCells, Color)

cv_blit(Canvas, Patch, R0, C0, Grid2):
    PH,PW = dims of Patch
    rebuild each canvas cell (R,C):
        PR=R-R0; PC=C-C0
        if 0<=PR<PH and 0<=PC<PW then Patch[PR][PC] else Canvas[R][C]


Part 186: Object Sequence and Progression Analysis (objseq Pack, WP 196)

oq_color_seq(Objs, Colors):
    Colors = [C | rest] where obj(C,_) in Objs, in list order

oq_size_seq(Objs, Sizes):
    Sizes = [N | rest] where N = length(Cells) for each obj(_,Cells) in Objs

oq_centroid_seq(Objs, Centroids):
    for each obj(_,Cells): CR=sum(Rs)//N, CC=sum(Cs)//N

oq_step_seq(Objs, Steps):
    Centroids = centroid_seq(Objs)
    Steps = [dr(R2-R1, C2-C1) for consecutive pairs]

oq_is_growing(Objs):
    Sizes = size_seq(Objs)
    for each consecutive pair: Sizes[i+1] > Sizes[i]

oq_is_shrinking(Objs):
    for each consecutive pair: Sizes[i+1] < Sizes[i]

oq_const_step(Objs, DR, DC):
    require length >= 2
    Steps = step_seq(Objs)
    Steps = [dr(DR,DC) | rest]; all rest = dr(DR,DC)

oq_const_row_step(Objs, DR):
    require length >= 2
    Steps = step_seq(Objs)
    all steps dr(DR, _)

oq_const_col_step(Objs, DC):
    require length >= 2
    all steps dr(_, DC)

oq_color_period(Objs, P, Cycle):
    Colors = color_seq(Objs); N = length
    find smallest P: N mod P = 0, Cycle = Colors[0..P-1], Cycle tiles Colors

oq_size_period(Objs, P, Cycle):
    same as color_period applied to size sequence

oq_collinear(Objs):
    Cs = centroid_seq(Objs)
    for all P3 in Cs[2..]: cross2d(Cs[0], Cs[1], P3) = 0

oq_next_centroid(Objs, r(NR,NC)):
    const_step(Objs, DR, DC)
    last(Cs) = r(LR,LC)
    NR=LR+DR; NC=LC+DC

oq_zip_colors(Objs1, Objs2, Pairs):
    Pairs = [C1-C2 | rest] for each (obj(C1,_), obj(C2,_)) pair in zip


Part 187: Object-Pair Change Analysis and Rule Application (objdelta Pack, WP 197)

dp_color_delta(O1, O2, C1-C2):
    O1=obj(C1,_); O2=obj(C2,_)

dp_pos_delta(O1, O2, dr(DR,DC)):
    r(R1,C1) = centroid(O1); r(R2,C2) = centroid(O2)
    DR=R2-R1; DC=C2-C1

dp_size_delta(O1, O2, D):
    N1=length(cells(O1)); N2=length(cells(O2)); D=N2-N1

dp_same_color(O1, O2):
    O1=obj(C,_); O2=obj(C,_)

dp_same_form(O1, O2):
    norm(cells(O1)) == norm(cells(O2))

dp_same_pos(O1, O2):
    centroid(O1) == centroid(O2)

dp_color_map(Pairs, Map):
    RawMap = [C1-C2 | ...] for each O1-O2 pair
    Map = sort(RawMap)

dp_apply_color(C1-C2, obj(C1,Cells), obj(C2,Cells)):
    head unification; fail if color != C1

dp_apply_color_map(Map, Obj, Obj2):
    for each Rule in Map: dp_apply_color(Rule, Obj, Obj2) -> cut

dp_apply_map_all(Map, Objs, Objs2):
    for each Obj: apply_color_map or keep unchanged

dp_const_dr(Pairs, DR):
    Deltas = [dp_pair_delta_(P) for P in Pairs]
    Deltas = [dr(DR,_) | rest]; all rest have row component DR

dp_const_dc(Pairs, DC):
    all Deltas have col component DC

dp_common_cells(O1, O2, Cells):
    P1=sort(cells(O1)); P2=sort(cells(O2))
    Cells = intersection(P1, P2)

dp_cell_diff(O1, O2, Added, Removed):
    P1=sort(cells(O1)); P2=sort(cells(O2))
    Added = subtract(P2, P1); Removed = subtract(P1, P2)


Part 188: Object Tiling and Multi-Copy Layout (objcopy Pack, WP 198)

tc_place_at(Obj, R0, C0, Obj2):
    MinR,MinC = bbox top-left of Obj
    DR=R0-MinR; DC=C0-MinC; Obj2 = translate(Obj, DR, DC)

tc_recolor_all(Color, Objs, Objs2):
    Objs2 = [obj(Color,Cells) | rest] for each obj(_,Cells) in Objs

tc_tile_row(Obj, N, Step, Objs):
    MinR,MinC = bbox top-left
    Objs = [place_at(Obj, MinR, MinC+I*Step) | I <- 0..N-1]

tc_tile_col(Obj, N, Step, Objs):
    Objs = [place_at(Obj, MinR+I*Step, MinC) | I <- 0..N-1]

tc_tile_grid(Obj, NR, NC, StepR, StepC, Objs):
    Objs = [place_at(Obj, MinR+I*StepR, MinC+J*StepC) | I<-0..NR-1, J<-0..NC-1]

tc_at_positions(Obj, Positions, Objs):
    Objs = [place_at(Obj, R, C) | r(R,C) <- Positions]

tc_align_top(Objs, Objs2):
    GlobalMin = min of minrow(O) for O in Objs
    Objs2 = [shift(O, GlobalMin - minrow(O), 0) | O in Objs]

tc_align_left(Objs, Objs2):
    GlobalMin = min of mincol(O) for O in Objs
    Objs2 = [shift(O, 0, GlobalMin - mincol(O)) | O in Objs]

tc_pack_row(Objs, R, C0, Gap, Objs2):
    shift all to row R; then pack: for each O, place at CurC; advance CurC += bbox_w(O)+Gap

tc_pack_col(Objs, C, R0, Gap, Objs2):
    shift all to col C; pack: place at CurR; advance CurR += bbox_h(O)+Gap

tc_spread_h(Objs, C0, Step, Objs2):
    Obj I -> place_at(Obj, minrow(Obj), C0+I*Step)

tc_spread_v(Objs, R0, Step, Objs2):
    Obj I -> place_at(Obj, R0+I*Step, mincol(Obj))

tc_center(Obj, H, W, Obj2):
    R0=(H-bbox_h(Obj))//2; C0=(W-bbox_w(Obj))//2; Obj2=place_at(Obj,R0,C0)

tc_flip_h(Obj, W, Obj2):
    each cell r(R,C) -> r(R, W-1-C)

Part 189: Object-List Correspondence and Matching (objmatch Pack, WP 199)

Private helpers:

mx_color_(Obj, Color):
    Obj = obj(Color, _)

mx_size_(Obj, N):
    Obj = obj(_, Cells); N = length(Cells)

mx_norm_(Obj, Sorted):
    Obj = obj(_, Cells)
    Rs = [R : r(R,_) in Cells]; Cs = [C : r(_,C) in Cells]
    MinR = min(Rs); MinC = min(Cs)
    Raw = [r(R-MinR, C-MinC) : r(R,C) in Cells]
    Sorted = sort(Raw)

mx_centroid_(Obj, r(CR,CC)):
    Obj = obj(_, Cells)
    Rs = [R : r(R,_) in Cells]; Cs = [C : r(_,C) in Cells]
    N = length(Rs)
    CR = sum(Rs) // N; CC = sum(Cs) // N

mx_sq_dist_(r(R1,C1), r(R2,C2), D2):
    D2 = (R2-R1)^2 + (C2-C1)^2

mx_nearest_in_(Centroids2, Objs2, Centroid1, Obj2):
    Pairs = [(sq_dist(Centroid1,C2), O2) : (C2,O2) in zip(Centroids2,Objs2)]
    (_, Obj2) = first(msort(Pairs))

mx_greedy_match_([], _, [])
mx_greedy_match_([O1|Rest1], Objs2, [O1-O2|Pairs]):
    Objs2 is nonempty
    C1 = centroid(O1)
    Cs2 = [centroid(O) : O in Objs2]
    O2 = nearest_in(Cs2, Objs2, C1)
    Remaining = Objs2 \ {O2}
    Pairs = greedy_match(Rest1, Remaining)
mx_greedy_match_([_|Rest1], [], Pairs):
    Pairs = greedy_match(Rest1, [])

mx_color_delta_(O1-O2, C1-C2): C1=color(O1); C2=color(O2)
mx_pos_delta_(O1-O2, dr(DR,DC)): r(R1,C1)=centroid(O1); r(R2,C2)=centroid(O2); DR=R2-R1; DC=C2-C1
mx_size_delta_(O1-O2, Delta): N1=size(O1); N2=size(O2); Delta=N2-N1

Exported predicates:

mx_by_color(List1, List2, Pairs):
    Pairs = [(O1,O2) : O1 in List1, O2 in List2, color(O1)=color(O2)]

mx_by_size(List1, List2, Pairs):
    Pairs = [(O1,O2) : O1 in List1, O2 in List2, size(O1)=size(O2)]

mx_by_form(List1, List2, Pairs):
    Pairs = [(O1,O2) : O1 in List1, O2 in List2, norm(O1)=norm(O2)]

mx_by_nearest(List1, List2, Pairs):
    Pairs = greedy_match(List1, List2)

mx_unmatched(Pairs, List1, List2, Um1, Um2):
    Matched1 = [O1 : O1-_ in Pairs]
    Matched2 = [O2 : _-O2 in Pairs]
    Um1 = List1 \ Matched1; Um2 = List2 \ Matched2

mx_filter_changed_color(Pairs, Changed):
    Changed = [(O1,O2) : O1-O2 in Pairs, color(O1) != color(O2)]

mx_filter_same_color(Pairs, Same):
    Same = [(O1,O2) : O1-O2 in Pairs, color(O1) = color(O2)]

mx_color_deltas(Pairs, Deltas): Deltas = [color_delta(P) : P in Pairs]
mx_pos_deltas(Pairs, Deltas): Deltas = [pos_delta(P) : P in Pairs]
mx_size_deltas(Pairs, Deltas): Deltas = [size_delta(P) : P in Pairs]

mx_all_same_color_delta([]): trivially true
mx_all_same_color_delta([First|Rest]): Ref=color_delta(First); all P in Rest: color_delta(P)=Ref

mx_all_same_pos_delta([]): trivially true
mx_all_same_pos_delta([First|Rest]): Ref=pos_delta(First); all P in Rest: pos_delta(P)=Ref

mx_all_same_size_delta([]): trivially true
mx_all_same_size_delta([First|Rest]): Ref=size_delta(First); all P in Rest: size_delta(P)=Ref

mx_zip([], [], [])
mx_zip([H1|T1], [H2|T2], [H1-H2|Rest]): Rest = zip(T1, T2)

Part 190: Object Merging, Set Operations, and Component Splitting (objmerge Pack, WP 200)

Private helpers:

mg_cells_(obj(_,Cells), Cells)
mg_color_(obj(Color,_), Color)
mg_maxrow_(Obj, R): findall rows, max_list
mg_maxcol_(Obj, C): findall cols, max_list
mg_minrow_(Obj, R): findall rows, min_list
mg_mincol_(Obj, C): findall cols, min_list
mg_translate_(Cells, DR, DC, Cells2): findall r(R+DR, C+DC)
mg_neighbors4_(r(R,C), [r(R-1,C), r(R+1,C), r(R,C-1), r(R,C+1)])
mg_neighbors8_(r(R,C), 8 surrounding cells)
mg_bfs_(Queue, CellSet, Visited, Component, NeighborPred):
    base: Queue=[] -> Component=Visited
    step: expand Queue[0] neighbors in CellSet not in Visited; append; recurse
mg_components_([], _, _, [])
mg_components_([First|Rest], Color, NeighborPred, [obj(Color,Comp)|Parts]):
    BFS from First; Remaining=Rest\Comp; recurse

Exported predicates:

mg_union_cells(O1, O2, Color, obj(Color,Union)):
    sort(cells(O1),SC1); sort(cells(O2),SC2); Union=union(SC1,SC2)

mg_intersect_cells(O1, O2, Color, obj(Color,Isect)):
    sort(cells(O1),SC1); sort(cells(O2),SC2); Isect=intersection(SC1,SC2)

mg_diff_cells(O1, O2, Color, obj(Color,Diff)):
    sort(cells(O1),SC1); sort(cells(O2),SC2); Diff=subtract(SC1,SC2)

mg_sym_diff_cells(O1, O2, Color, obj(Color,SymDiff)):
    OnlyIn1=subtract(SC1,SC2); OnlyIn2=subtract(SC2,SC1); SymDiff=append(OnlyIn1,OnlyIn2)

mg_concat_h(O1, O2, Gap, obj(color(O1), merged)):
    DC = maxcol(O1)+1+Gap-mincol(O2)
    C2Shifted = translate(cells(O2), 0, DC)
    merged = append(cells(O1), C2Shifted)

mg_concat_v(O1, O2, Gap, obj(color(O1), merged)):
    DR = maxrow(O1)+1+Gap-minrow(O2)
    C2Shifted = translate(cells(O2), DR, 0)
    merged = append(cells(O1), C2Shifted)

mg_merge_list(Objs, Color, obj(Color, Union)):
    AllCells = flatten [cells(O) : O in Objs]
    Union = sort(AllCells)

mg_subtract_list(Base, RemoveList, Color, obj(Color, Result)):
    ToRemove = flatten [cells(O) : O in RemoveList]
    Result = subtract(sort(cells(Base)), sort(ToRemove))

mg_expand_bbox(Obj, obj(Color, Cells)):
    Cells = [r(R,C) : R in MinR..MaxR, C in MinC..MaxC]

mg_hollow_bbox(Obj, obj(Color, Frame)):
    Raw = [r(R,C) : R in MinR..MaxR, C in MinC..MaxC, R=MinR OR R=MaxR OR C=MinC OR C=MaxC]
    Frame = sort(Raw)  % deduplicate corners

mg_pad(Obj, P, Color, obj(Color, Cells)):
    Cells = [r(R,C) : R in (MinR-P)..(MaxR+P), C in (MinC-P)..(MaxC+P)]

mg_split_cc4(Obj, Parts): components(sort(cells(Obj)), color(Obj), neighbors4)
mg_split_cc8(Obj, Parts): components(sort(cells(Obj)), color(Obj), neighbors8)
mg_n_components4(Obj, N): N = length(split_cc4(Obj))

Part 191: Object-List Aggregate Attribute Analysis (objattr Pack, WP 201)

Private helpers:
oa_color_(obj(Color,_), Color)
oa_size_(obj(_,Cells), N): N = length(Cells)
oa_norm_(obj(_,Cells), Sorted): translate to origin, sort cells
oa_topleft_(obj(_,Cells), r(MinR,MinC)): min row and col
oa_count_color_(Objs, Color, Count): findall matching color, length
oa_total_cells_color_(Objs, Color, Total): findall matching sizes, sum_list
oa_mode_(List, Mode): msort + oa_run_max_acc_ for most frequent
oa_run_max_acc_(Rest, Cur, CurCount, Best, BestCount, Mode): recursive run-length max

Exported predicates:

oa_total_cells(Objs, N): findall sizes, sum_list
oa_color_counts(Objs, Pairs): distinct colors; findall C-count_color(C)
oa_cell_counts_by_color(Objs, Pairs): distinct colors; findall C-total_cells_color(C)
oa_n_colors(Objs, N): findall colors, sort, length
oa_n_objs_of_color(Objs, Color, N): count_color_(Objs, Color, N)
oa_dominant_color(Objs, Color): cell_counts; create NegT-C keyed; msort; first color
oa_rarest_color(Objs, Color): cell_counts; create T-C keyed; msort; first color
oa_unique_color(Objs, Color): color_counts; member(Color-1, Pairs)
oa_size_rank(Objs, Ranked): findall NegN-Obj; msort; extract Obj
oa_pos_rank(Objs, Ranked): findall r(R,C)-Obj; msort; extract Obj
oa_majority_size(Objs, N): findall sizes; oa_mode_
oa_all_same_color([]): true; [First|Rest]: color(First)=Color; maplist color_eq(Color)
oa_all_same_size([]): true; [First|Rest]: size(First)=N; maplist size_eq(N)
oa_all_same_form([]): true; [First|Rest]: norm(First)=Norm; maplist norm_eq(Norm)

Part 192: objgroup Pack Pseudocode (WP 202)

PROCEDURE og_group_by_(Objs, KeyPred, Groups)
  Pairs = [(KeyPred(O), O) for O in Objs]
  Keys = sort(distinct keys from Pairs)
  FOR Key in Keys:
    Members = [O | (Key, O) in Pairs]
    YIELD Key-Members
  END

PROCEDURE og_by_color(Objs, Groups)
  CALL og_group_by_(Objs, og_color_, Groups)

PROCEDURE og_by_size(Objs, Groups)
  CALL og_group_by_(Objs, og_size_, Groups)

PROCEDURE og_by_form(Objs, Groups)
  CALL og_group_by_(Objs, og_norm_, Groups)
  // og_norm_: translate to origin, sort cells

PROCEDURE og_by_row(Objs, Groups)
  CALL og_group_by_(Objs, og_row_key_, Groups)
  // og_row_key_: min row of topleft corner

PROCEDURE og_by_col(Objs, Groups)
  CALL og_group_by_(Objs, og_col_key_, Groups)
  // og_col_key_: min col of topleft corner

PROCEDURE og_n_groups(Groups, N)
  N = length(Groups)

PROCEDURE og_n_members(Groups, N, Selected)
  Selected = [G | G in Groups AND length(members(G)) = N]

PROCEDURE og_singletons(Groups, Singletons)
  CALL og_n_members(Groups, 1, Singletons)

PROCEDURE og_largest(Groups, Group)
  ASSERT Groups != []
  Keyed = [(-N, G) | G in Groups, N = length(members(G))]
  (_, Group) = first(sort(Keyed))

PROCEDURE og_smallest(Groups, Group)
  ASSERT Groups != []
  Keyed = [(N, G) | G in Groups, N = length(members(G))]
  (_, Group) = first(sort(Keyed))

PROCEDURE og_all_same_size(Groups)
  IF Groups = [] THEN succeed
  N = length(members(first(Groups)))
  FOR G in rest(Groups): ASSERT length(members(G)) = N

PROCEDURE og_sort_desc(Groups, Sorted)
  Keyed = [(-N, G) | G in Groups, N = length(members(G))]
  Sorted = [G | (_, G) in sort(Keyed)]

PROCEDURE og_flat(Groups, Objs)
  Objs = [O | (_-Members) in Groups, O in Members]

PROCEDURE og_filter_size(Groups, Min, Max, Filtered)
  Filtered = [G | G in Groups, N = length(members(G)), N >= Min, N <= Max]

Part 193: scenecmp Pack Pseudocode (WP 203)

PROCEDURE sm_n_objs(Objs, N)
  N = length(Objs)

PROCEDURE sm_total_cells(Objs, N)
  N = sum(length(cells(O)) for O in Objs)

PROCEDURE sm_colors(Objs, Colors)
  Colors = sort(distinct(color(O) for O in Objs))

PROCEDURE sm_forms(Objs, Forms)
  Forms = sort(distinct(normalize(O) for O in Objs))
  // normalize: translate to origin, sort cells

PROCEDURE sm_same_n_objs(Before, After)
  ASSERT length(Before) = length(After)

PROCEDURE sm_same_total_cells(Before, After)
  ASSERT sm_total_cells(Before) = sm_total_cells(After)

PROCEDURE sm_same_colors(Before, After)
  CB = sm_colors(Before)
  CA = sm_colors(After)
  ASSERT CB = CA

PROCEDURE sm_same_forms(Before, After)
  FB = sm_forms(Before)
  FA = sm_forms(After)
  ASSERT FB = FA

PROCEDURE sm_added_colors(Before, After, Added)
  CB = sm_colors(Before)
  CA = sm_colors(After)
  Added = subtract(CA, CB)

PROCEDURE sm_removed_colors(Before, After, Removed)
  CB = sm_colors(Before)
  CA = sm_colors(After)
  Removed = subtract(CB, CA)

PROCEDURE sm_added_forms(Before, After, Added)
  FB = sm_forms(Before)
  FA = sm_forms(After)
  Added = subtract(FA, FB)

PROCEDURE sm_removed_forms(Before, After, Removed)
  FB = sm_forms(Before)
  FA = sm_forms(After)
  Removed = subtract(FB, FA)

PROCEDURE sm_n_color_change(Before, After, N)
  Added = sm_added_colors(Before, After)
  Removed = sm_removed_colors(Before, After)
  N = length(Added) + length(Removed)

PROCEDURE sm_any_change(Before, After)
  IF NOT sm_same_n_objs(Before, After) THEN succeed
  IF NOT sm_same_colors(Before, After) THEN succeed
  IF NOT sm_same_forms(Before, After) THEN succeed
  ELSE fail

Part 194: objlocate Pack Pseudocode (WP 204)

SHARED: centroid(Obj) = (sum_rows/N, sum_cols/N) for N cells

PROCEDURE lq_above(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefR = row(centroid(Ref))
  Found = [O | O in Objs, row(centroid(O)) < RefR]

PROCEDURE lq_below(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefR = row(centroid(Ref))
  Found = [O | O in Objs, row(centroid(O)) > RefR]

PROCEDURE lq_left_of(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefC = col(centroid(Ref))
  Found = [O | O in Objs, col(centroid(O)) < RefC]

PROCEDURE lq_right_of(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefC = col(centroid(Ref))
  Found = [O | O in Objs, col(centroid(O)) > RefC]

PROCEDURE lq_touching4(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefCells = cells(Ref)
  Found = [O | O in Objs, NOT overlap(cells(O),RefCells), touch4(cells(O),RefCells)]
  touch4: EXISTS cell1 in cells(O), cell2 in RefCells s.t. |R1-R2|+|C1-C2|=1

PROCEDURE lq_touching8(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefCells = cells(Ref)
  Found = [O | O in Objs, NOT overlap(cells(O),RefCells), touch8(cells(O),RefCells)]
  touch8: EXISTS cell1,cell2 s.t. max(|R1-R2|,|C1-C2|)=1

PROCEDURE lq_overlapping(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefCells = cells(Ref)
  Found = [O | O in Objs, EXISTS cell in cells(O) s.t. cell in RefCells]

PROCEDURE lq_same_color(Objs, Ref, Found)
  Color = color(Ref)
  Found = [O | O in Objs, color(O) = Color]

PROCEDURE lq_same_form(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefNorm = normalize(Ref)
  Found = [O | O in Objs, normalize(O) = RefNorm]

PROCEDURE lq_aligned_h(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefR = min_row(Ref)
  Found = [O | O in Objs, min_row(O) = RefR]

PROCEDURE lq_aligned_v(Objs, Ref, Found)
  RefC = min_col(Ref)
  Found = [O | O in Objs, min_col(O) = RefC]

PROCEDURE lq_nearest(Objs, Ref, Nearest)
  ASSERT Objs != []
  RefC = centroid(Ref)
  Keyed = [(sq_dist(RefC, centroid(O)), O) | O in Objs]
  (_, Nearest) = first(sort(Keyed))

PROCEDURE lq_farthest(Objs, Ref, Farthest)
  ASSERT Objs != []
  RefC = centroid(Ref)
  Keyed = [(-sq_dist(RefC, centroid(O)), O) | O in Objs]
  (_, Farthest) = first(sort(Keyed))

PROCEDURE lq_n_touching4(Objs, Ref, N)
  N = length(lq_touching4(Objs, Ref))

Part 195: scenexf Pack — Scene-Level Uniform Transformation of All Objects (sx_*, Layer 184)

PROCEDURE sx_recolor(Scene, OldColor, NewColor, Scene2)
  Scene2 = [recolor_atom(OldColor, NewColor, O) | O in Scene]
  WHERE recolor_atom(Old, New, obj(C, Cells)) =
    IF C == Old THEN obj(New, Cells) ELSE obj(C, Cells)

PROCEDURE sx_recolor_all(Scene, NewColor, Scene2)
  Scene2 = [obj(NewColor, Cells) | obj(_, Cells) in Scene]

PROCEDURE sx_apply_color_map(Scene, Map, Scene2)
  Scene2 = [apply_map(Map, O) | O in Scene]
  WHERE apply_map(Map, obj(C, Cells)) =
    IF (C-NewC) in Map THEN obj(NewC, Cells) ELSE obj(C, Cells)

PROCEDURE sx_shift(Scene, DR, DC, Scene2)
  Scene2 = [shift_obj(DR, DC, O) | O in Scene]
  WHERE shift_obj(DR, DC, obj(Color, Cells)) =
