ARC-AGI-2 Wave 20: section_tile pseudocode (2026-06-29)
section_tile(Grid) ->
  // Step 1: find all-1 rows and all-1 cols
  DivRows <- {R | all cells in Grid[R] == 1}
  DivCols <- {C | all cells in Grid[*][C] == 1}
  // Step 2: extract non-trivial sections
  RowRanges <- ranges(0..NRows, DivRows)   // intervals between dividers
  ColRanges <- ranges(0..NCols, DivCols)
  Sections  <- {slice(Grid, Rows, Cols) | Rows in RowRanges, Cols in ColRanges,
                section is non-trivial}
  // Step 3: classify sections
  Shape1 <- section with (any 0 cell) and (>= 2 distinct non-zero values)
  Solids <- Sections - {Shape1}
  // Step 4: derive tile count from shape2
  Shape2 <- first solid section
  TotalNZ <- count of non-zero cells in Shape2
  N <- TotalNZ // 2
  // Step 5: derive color mapping
  ColorSolids <- Solids - {Shape2}   // remaining solid sections in order
  Colors <- [uniform_value(S) | S in ColorSolids]
  // Step 6: find inner bbox of shape1
  BboxRows, BboxCols <- min/max rows and cols of non-zero cells in Shape1
  InnerPattern <- slice(Shape1, BboxRows, BboxCols)
  // Step 7: build tiled output
  Copies <- []
  for I in 1..N do
    Copy <- apply_color_map(InnerPattern, Colors)
    Copies <- Copies ++ [Copy]
    if I < N: Copies <- Copies ++ [separator_cols_of_2(BboxCols)]   // 2-cell separator
  return stack_vertically(Copies)   // or horizontally depending on layout axis

ARC-AGI-2 Wave 21: chain_link pseudocode (2026-06-29)
chain_link(Grid) ->
  BG <- Grid[0][0]
  LegSeq <- parse_legend(Grid, BG)      // row alternating BG,V,BG,V,...
  Boxes <- detect_boxes(Grid, BG)       // for each non-BG cell: BG-scan 4 dirs
  Changes <- walk_chain(LegSeq, Boxes, Grid, BG)
  return apply_changes(Grid, Changes)

walk_chain([V0|Rest], Boxes, Grid, BG) ->
  StartBox <- first box(V0,...) s.t. full chain completes from it
  return walk(Rest, StartBox, Boxes, Grid, BG, visited={StartBox})

walk([], _, _, _, _, _) -> []
walk([Vb|Rest], CurBox, Boxes, Grid, BG, Visited) ->
  NextBox <- box(Vb,...) not in Visited,
             same col-block or row-block with CurBox,
             gap_clear(Grid, BG, gap_region(CurBox, NextBox))
  Ch <- fill_gap(CurBox, NextBox, Grid, BG)   // color = Va = CurBox.color
  return Ch ++ walk(Rest, NextBox, Boxes, Grid, BG, Visited union {NextBox})

fill_gap(A, B, Grid, BG) ->
  if same_col_block(A, B):
    FRA <- last_nonBG_going_toward_B_vertically(A, Grid, BG)
    FLB <- last_nonBG_going_toward_A_vertically(B, Grid, BG)
    return {(R,C,A.color) : R in FRA+1..FLB-1, C in col_range(A)}
  else same_row_block(A, B):
    FRA <- last_nonBG_going_toward_B_horizontally(A, Grid, BG)
    FLB <- last_nonBG_going_toward_A_horizontally(B, Grid, BG)
    return {(R,C,A.color) : R in row_range(A), C in FRA+1..FLB-1}


ARC-AGI-2 Wave 22: legend_veto pseudocode (2026-06-29)
legend_veto(Grid) ->
  S <- sort({V : V in Grid[0..3][0..3], V != 7, V != 3, V != 0})
  if S = {}: fail
  AllComps <- find_4connected_any_color_comps(Grid, bg=7)
  DataComps <- [C : C in AllComps, not overlaps_legend(C)]
  for each Comp in DataComps:
    Vals <- sort({V : (R,C) in Comp, V=Grid[R][C], V != 7, V != 0})
    if S subset Vals:
      Grid <- erase_comp(Comp, Grid, fill=7)
  return Grid

overlaps_legend(Comp) -> exists (R,C) in Comp s.t. R <= 3 AND C <= 3

find_4connected_any_color_comps(Grid, bg) ->
  Seeds <- all (R,C) s.t. Grid[R][C] != bg   // reading order
  Visited <- {}
  Comps <- []
  for each (R,C) in Seeds not in Visited:
    Comp <- BFS from (R,C) through non-bg cells of any color
    Visited <- Visited union Comp
    Comps <- Comps ++ [Comp]
  return Comps

erase_comp(Comp, Grid, fill) ->
  for each (R,C) in Comp: Grid[R][C] <- fill
  return Grid

ARC-AGI-2 Wave 23: period_extend pseudocode (2026-06-29)
period_extend(Grid) ->
  NR = num_rows(Grid), NC = num_cols(Grid)
  RowCount = count_active_rows(Grid)   // rows with 2+ same-color non-BG cells
  ColCount = count_active_cols(Grid)   // cols with 2+ same-color non-BG cells
  Out = blank_grid(NR, NC)
  if RowCount >= ColCount:
    for R in 0..NR-1: Out = apply_line(Grid, R, ROW, NC-1, Out)
  else:
    for C in 0..NC-1: Out = apply_line(Grid, C, COL, NR-1, Out)
  return Out

apply_line(Grid, LineIdx, Dir, MaxPos, Out) ->
  Pairs = [(P, V) | non_BG cell at line position P with value V]
  if no anchor pair in Pairs: copy Pairs as singletons into Out; return Out
  (AnchorColor, AnchorPositions, Step) = find_anchor(Pairs)
  PatPos = {P | P mod Step = AnchorPositions[0] mod Step, 0 <= P <= MaxPos}
  Stops = [(P, V) | (P, V) in Pairs, V != AnchorColor, P in PatPos]
  Singletons = [(P, V) | (P, V) in Pairs, V != AnchorColor, P not in PatPos]
  if Stops non-empty:
    (StopP, StopC) = Stops[0]
    if StopP < min(AnchorPositions): MinFill = StopP; MaxFill = max(AnchorPositions)
    else: MinFill = min(AnchorPositions); MaxFill = StopP
    FillCells = [(P, StopC) | P in PatPos, MinFill <= P <= MaxFill]
  else:
    FillCells = [(P, AnchorColor) | P in PatPos]
  write FillCells + Singletons into Out at LineIdx
  return Out

find_anchor(Pairs) ->
  StepVals = sorted [(|P2-P1|, V) | (P1,V) and (P2,V) in Pairs, P2>P1]
  (Step, AnchorColor) = StepVals[0]   // smallest step wins
  AnchorPositions = [P | (P, AnchorColor) in Pairs]
  return (AnchorColor, AnchorPositions, Step)

WP-282 shape_sort (Layer 257) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 24 Pseudocode
Task: 2ba387bc.

shape_sort(Grid) ->
  Colors = sort(distinct non-zero values in Grid)
  Shapes = [one_shape(Grid, C) for C in Colors] sorted by R0-C0 reading order
  Hollows = [S for S in Shapes if has_zero(S.sub)]
  Solids  = [S for S in Shapes if not has_zero(S.sub)]
  Pairs = zip_pad(Hollows, Solids, zero_block)
  Output = concat([left4 ++ right4 for row in each pair block])

one_shape(Grid, Color) ->
  Rs = [R | Grid[R][C] = Color for some C]
  Cs = [C | Grid[R][C] = Color for some R]
  R0 = min(Rs), C0 = min(Cs)
  Sub = Grid[R0..R0+3][C0..C0+3]
  return (R0, C0, Sub)

zip_pad([], [], []) -> []
zip_pad([H|Hs], [], rest) -> [[H, zero_block] | zip_pad(Hs, [], rest)]
zip_pad([], [S|Ss], rest) -> [[zero_block, S] | zip_pad([], Ss, rest)]
zip_pad([H|Hs], [S|Ss], rest) -> [[H, S] | zip_pad(Hs, Ss, rest)]

WP-283 bar_extend (Layer 258) pseudocode:
  arc2_transform(bar_extend, Grid, Out):
    D = find_divider(Grid)   % column where all non-BG values are identical
    for each Row in Grid:
      Bar = Row[0..D-1]
      Div = Row[D]
      PC = rightmost_nonbg(Bar)    % primary color
      if PC == 0: OutRow = Row; continue
      CP = count(PC, Bar)
      SC = first_other_nonbg(Bar, PC)  % secondary color (0 if none)
      CS = count(SC, Bar) if SC != 0 else 1
      Period = CP * CS
      PeriodCells = [cell(i) for i in 0..Period-1]
        where cell(i) = PC if i mod CP == 0
                       = SC if SC!=0 and i mod CS == 0
                       = 0  otherwise
      RFill = [PeriodCells[i mod Period] for i in 0..RightWidth-1]
      OutRow = Bar ++ [Div] ++ RFill
    Out = all OutRows

WP-284 straighten_diag (Layer 259) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 26
Task: 7b80bb43.
Pseudocode:
  BG = most_common_value(Grid)
  LV = first_nonbg_value(Grid)
  Diag = {(r,c) : Grid[r][c]!=BG
                   and no 4-conn neighbor is non-BG
                   and some diagonal neighbor is non-BG}
  if Diag is empty: fail
  DiagNbr = {(nr,nc) : (r,c) in Diag,
                        (nr,nc) is 8-neighbor of (r,c),
                        (nr,nc) not in Diag,
                        Grid[nr][nc] != BG}
  Comps = 8-connected components of Diag
  Fills = []
  for each Comp in Comps:
    Anchors = {(ar,ac) : (r,c) in Comp,
                          (ar,ac) is 8-neighbor of (r,c),
                          (ar,ac) not in Diag,
                          Grid[ar][ac] != BG}
    for each Anchor (ar,ac) in Anchors:
      Tip = argmax_{(r,c) in Comp} |r-ar| + |c-ac|
      DDR = sign(Tip.r - ar),  DDC = sign(Tip.c - ac)
      IsH = Anchor has 4-conn non-diag non-BG in same row
      IsV = Anchor has 4-conn non-diag non-BG in same col
      if IsH and DDC != 0:
        Fill1 = scan(ar, ac, 0, DDC)
        Fills += Fill1 (if scan succeeds)
      if IsV and DDR != 0:
        Fill2 = scan(ar, ac, DDR, 0)
        Fills += Fill2 (if scan succeeds)
  scan(ar, ac, fdr, fdc) -> Gap or fail:
    r,c = ar+fdr, ac+fdc; Gap = []
    loop:
      if (r,c) out of bounds: fail
      if Grid[r][c] == BG: Gap += (r,c); r+=fdr; c+=fdc
      elif (r,c) in Diag: r+=fdr; c+=fdc  % skip diagonal
      else: return Gap  % found closing cell
  G = copy of Grid with Diag cells set to BG, Fills cells set to LV
  repeat until no change:
    for each (r,c) in DiagNbr where G[r][c] != BG:
      n4 = 4-conn non-BG neighbors of (r,c) in G
      if len(n4) == 1:
        (ar,ac) = n4[0]
        a_others = 4-conn non-BG neighbors of (ar,ac) in G, excluding (r,c)
        if a_others is non-empty:
          if (ar-r)==0: prune if anchor has no same-row neighbor in a_others
          else:         prune if anchor has no same-col neighbor in a_others
          if prune: G[r][c] = BG; changed = True
  Out = G

WP-285 stream_extend (Layer 260) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 27
Input: Grid (list of lists), BG = 0, AVal = 1 (A-marker color).
Output: Out (same dimensions, seed chains extended to grid boundary).

Procedure stream_extend(Grid) -> Out:
  NRows = len(Grid), NCols = len(Grid[0])
  BG = most common color in Grid
  AVal = 1
  ACells = {(r,c) : Grid[r][c] == AVal}
  Comps = connected_components_4(ACells)
  Out = Grid
  for each Comp in Comps:
    for each Dir in {up, down, left, right}:
      for each (r,c) in Comp where (r+dr, c+dc) not in Comp:
        Chain = collect_chain(Grid, r+dr, c+dc, Dir)
        if Chain != [] and chain ends at BG (not grid boundary):
          for each position P in extension region (beyond Chain to grid edge):
            D = distance from chain anchor to P
            Out[P] = Chain[D mod len(Chain)].value

collect_chain(Grid, r, c, Dir) -> Chain or []:
  Chain = []
  while (r,c) in bounds:
    V = Grid[r][c]
    if V == BG: return reverse(Chain)   % chain ends at BG gap
    if V == AVal: fail                  % hit another marker, abort
    Chain.prepend((r, c, V))
    (r, c) += step(Dir)
  fail                                  % reached boundary without BG gap

extension_region(Chain, Dir, NRows, NCols):
  Anchor = Chain[0]
  P = len(Chain)
  if Dir == up:    positions r from 0 to Anchor.r - P, same col
  if Dir == down:  positions r from Anchor.r + P to NRows-1, same col
  if Dir == left:  positions c from 0 to Anchor.c - P, same row
  if Dir == right: positions c from Anchor.c + P to NCols-1, same row

WP-286 slide_open (Layer 261) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 28
Input: Grid (list of lists).
Output: Out (same dimensions, 0-cell components slid to divider; open rows
        filled with 2 right of the divider).

Procedure slide_open(Grid) -> Out:
  NRows = len(Grid), NCols = len(Grid[0])
  DC = column where all values == 5 (found by between(0, NCols-1, DC) with forall check)
  ZeroCells = [(r,c) : Grid[r][c] == 0 and c < DC]
  Comps = connected_components_4(ZeroCells)
  G = Grid
  for each Comp in Comps:
    MaxCol = max(c for _,c in Comp)
    Shift = (DC - 1) - MaxCol
    for (r,c) in Comp: G[r][c] = 6     % erase pass (placeholder, never in output)
    for (r,c) in Comp: G[r][c+Shift] = 0  % place pass
  Out = fill_open(G, NRows, NCols, DC)

fill_open(Grid, NRows, NCols, DC) -> Out:
  DC1 = DC - 1, DC2 = DC - 2
  Out = Grid
  for R in 0..NRows-1:
    VRight = Grid[R][DC1]
    VGap   = Grid[R][DC2]
    if VRight == 0 and VGap != 0:
      LeftZeros = [c : 0 <= c <= DC2-1 and Grid[R][c] == 0]
      if LeftZeros != []:
        for C in DC+1..NCols-1: Out[R][C] = 2

WP-287 diag_beam (Layer 262) - ARC-AGI-2 Wave 29
Input: Grid (list of lists containing only BG, 1, and 6 values).
Output: Out (same dimensions, beams between diagonal 1-pairs filled with 1;
        perpendicular rays from 6-obstacles filled with 6).

Procedure diag_beam(Grid) -> Out:
  BG = Grid[0][0]
  assert: all non-BG cells have value 1 or 6
  Ones  = [(r,c) : Grid[r][c] == 1]
  Sixes = [(r,c) : Grid[r][c] == 6]
  NRows = len(Grid), NCols = len(Grid[0])
  Pairs = [(P1,P2) : P1 in Ones, P2 in Ones, P1 < P2,
            abs(P1.r - P2.r) == abs(P1.c - P2.c), abs(P1.r - P2.r) > 0]
  assert: Pairs is non-empty
  G = Grid
  for each (R1,C1)-(R2,C2) in Pairs:
    DR = sign(R2 - R1),  DC = sign(C2 - C1)
    G = march(R1+DR, C1+DC, DR, DC, R2, C2, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G)
  Out = G

march(R, C, DR, DC, R2, C2, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G) -> G:
  if R == R2 and C == C2: return G           % reached destination
  if (R,C) in Sixes:
    G = bounce(R, C, DR, DC, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G)
  else:
    G[R][C] = 1
  return march(R+DR, C+DC, DR, DC, R2, C2, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G)

bounce(R, C, DR, DC, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G) -> G:
  G = ray(R, C,  DR, -DC, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G)
  G = ray(R, C, -DR,  DC, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G)
  return G

ray(R, C, DR, DC, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G) -> G:
  NR = R + DR, NC = C + DC
  if NR < 0 or NR >= NRows or NC < 0 or NC >= NCols: return G  % out of bounds
  if (NR,NC) in Sixes: return G              % stop at existing obstacle
  G[NR][NC] = 6
  return ray(NR, NC, DR, DC, Sixes, NRows, NCols, G)

% Wave 30 - frame_absorb (WP-288, Layer 263)

frame_absorb(Grid) -> Out:
  Positions = [R-C | nth0(R,Grid,Row), nth0(C,Row,V), V != 0, V != 5]
  if Positions empty: fail
  Comps = fa_comps(Positions)
  if len(Comps) < 2: fail
  Blocks = [fa_block(Grid, Cells) | Cells in Comps]
  Actions = fa_solve(Blocks)
  if Actions empty: fail
  Out = foldl(fa_exec, Actions, Grid)

fa_comps(Positions) -> [Comp, ...]:
  if Positions empty: return []
  [H|T] = Positions
  Comp, Remaining = fa_bfs([H], [H], T)
  return [Comp] + fa_comps(Remaining)

fa_bfs(Queue, Visited, Unvisited) -> (Component, Remaining):
  if Queue empty: return (Visited, Unvisited)
  [H|Q] = Queue
  Ns = [N | fa_adj(H,N), N in Unvisited, N not in Visited], sort Ns
  return fa_bfs(Q+Ns, Visited+Ns, Unvisited - Ns)

fa_adj(R-C) -> neighbours:
  yield (R-1)-C if R-1 >= 0
  yield (R+1)-C
  yield R-(C-1) if C-1 >= 0
  yield R-(C+1)

fa_block(Grid, Cells) -> block(CR, CC, CV, AV, Cells):
  Vals = [Grid[R][C] | R-C in Cells]
  Colors = distinct(Vals)
  if len(Colors) == 2:
    C1, C2 = Colors
    if count(C1, Vals) == 1: CV=C1, AV=C2
    else: CV=C2, AV=C1
    CR-CC = cell in Cells where Grid[CR][CC] == CV
  else:  % monochrome
    AV = CV = Colors[0]
    CR-CC = cell in Cells with max 4-degree within Cells

fa_max_deg(Cells) -> Best:
  DegCells = [(count(fa_adj(Cell) intersect Cells), Cell) | Cell in Cells]
  Best = Cell paired with max degree

fa_solve(Blocks) -> Actions:
  return fa_solve_worker(Blocks, [])

fa_solve_worker([], Acc) -> Acc
fa_solve_worker(Available, Acc) -> Actions:
  % Priority 1: monochrome block
  if exists Y in Available with Y.CV == Y.AV:
    if exists X in Available, X != Y, X.CV == Y.AV:
      return fa_solve_worker(Available-{X,Y}, [absorb(X,Y)] + Acc)
    else:
      return fa_solve_worker(Available-{Y}, [erase(Y)] + Acc)
  % Priority 2: chain start
  if exists X in Available with no Z in Available s.t. Z.CV == X.AV:
    if exists Y in Available, Y != X, X.CV == Y.AV:
      return fa_solve_worker(Available-{X,Y}, [absorb(X,Y)] + Acc)
    else:
      return fa_solve_worker(Available-{X}, [erase(X)] + Acc)
  % Cycle fallback: erase all
  return [erase(B) | B in Available] + Acc

fa_exec(absorb(X,Y), Grid) -> Grid':
  Grid' = erase_cells(Y.Cells, Grid)
  Grid'[X.CR][X.CC] = Y.CV

fa_exec(erase(B), Grid) -> Grid':
  Grid' = erase_cells(B.Cells, Grid)

erase_cells(Cells, Grid) -> Grid':
  Grid' = set each R-C in Cells to 0 in Grid

WP-289 shape_beam (Layer 264):
shape_beam(Grid) -> Out:
  BG = most_common(Grid)
  (RR, RC, BeamDir) = find_rod(Grid)   % 4-cell; beam=opposite of 2-trail
  RodCells = {4-cell} union {2-trail cells}
  ShapeCells = {(R,C) : Grid[R][C] in {1,3}}
  Components = bfs_partition(ShapeCells)
  Shapes = [classify(C, Grid, BG) for C in Components]
    classify: separate 1-cells and 3-cells;
              find exit-dir: 3s share a row -> check row±1 for BG (up/down);
                             3s share a col -> check col±1 for BG (left/right);
              Cross = cols of 3s (vertical exit) or rows of 3s (horizontal);
              ExitAP = shared row or shared col of the 3s.
  BeamCells = run_beam(BeamDir, [RC], RR, Shapes)
  run_beam(Dir, Cross, AS, Shapes):
    hit = first shape with a cell at Cross-pos and row/col ahead of AS
    if hit at pos HR/HC:
      fill gap cells (AS to HR+1 or AS to HC-1)
      add all shape cells
      NAS = ExitAP ± 1
      return gap + shape + run_beam(ExitDir, ExitCross, NAS, Shapes minus hit)
    else:
      fill from AS to grid-edge at Cross-pos
  All2 = RodCells union BeamCells
  Out = blank(BG) with 2 at every cell in All2

WP-290 shape_classify (Layer 265) - Wave 32
  Guard: sort(flatten(Grid)) has exactly 2 elements.
  BG = most-frequent value in flatten(Grid).
  NonBG = all (R,C) where Grid[R][C] != BG.
  Outside = BFS from boundary BG cells through BG (4-connected).
  Holes = {(R,C) : Grid[R][C] = BG, (R,C) not in Outside}.
  Border = {(R,C) : (R,C) in Outside,
            exists 8-connected neighbour (RN,CN) with Grid[RN][CN] != BG}.
  Comps = 4-connected components of NonBG positions.
  HoleComps = {comp in Comps : exists (R,C) in comp,
               exists 4-connected (RN,CN) of (R,C) in Holes}.
  HoleCells = union of all cells in HoleComps.
  G1 = Grid with Holes painted 6.
  G2 = G1 with Border painted 2.
  Out = G2 with HoleCells painted 8.

WP-291 tile_stamp (Layer 266) - Wave 33
  BG = most-frequent value in flatten(Grid).
  Cells = all (R,C) where Grid[R][C] != BG.
  Comps = 4-connected components of Cells.
  KernComp = unique component whose cells use >1 distinct Grid value.
  KR1,KC1,KR2,KC2 = bounding box of KernComp.
  KR = KR2-KR1+1. KC = KC2-KC1+1.
  Kern = Grid[KR1..KR2, KC1..KC2] (sub-grid, verbatim including interior BG).
  PatCells = union of all Cells not in KernComp.
  PR1,PC1,PR2,PC2 = bounding box of PatCells.
  PNR = PR2-PR1+1. PNC = PC2-PC1+1.
  Out has PNR*KR rows and PNC*KC cols.
  For ROut in 0..PNR*KR-1:
    TR = ROut // KR. DR = ROut mod KR.
    KernRow = Kern[DR].
    For TC in 0..PNC-1:
      R = PR1+TR. C = PC1+TC.
      if (R,C) in PatCells: Seg = KernRow
      else: Seg = [BG]*KC
    Out[ROut] = concat(Seg for TC in 0..PNC-1).

Wave 34 - rail_fill (WP-292, Layer 267). Task 271d71e2.

PROCEDURE rail_fill(Grid) -> Out:
  NR, NC = dimensions(Grid).
  BG = Grid[0][0].
  ZeroCells = {(R,C) | Grid[R][C] = 0}.
  Boxes = {(R1,C1,R2,C2) | (R1,C1) in ZeroCells, (R2,C2) in ZeroCells,
             R2 > R1+1, C2 > C1+1,
             zero_border(Grid,R1,C1,R2,C2),
             valid_interior(Grid,R1,C1,R2,C2)}.
  Plans = [box_transform(Grid,NR,NC,Box) for Box in Boxes].
  Out = build_grid(NR,NC,BG,Plans).

PROCEDURE box_transform(Grid,NR,NC,R1,C1,R2,C2) -> Plan:
  Dir,Inner,Outer = find_arm(Grid,NR,NC,R1,C1,R2,C2).
  Gap = arm_gap(Dir,Inner,Outer).
  H = R2-R1-1. W = C2-C1-1.
  N7in = count_7s_in_interior(Grid,R1,C1,R2,C2).
  N7gained = min(Gap, H*W - N7in).
  N7new = N7in + N7gained.
  Order = fill_order(Dir, H, W).
  Interior = make_interior(H, W, N7new, Order).
  NewBox = shift_box(Dir, R1,C1,R2,C2, N7gained).
  NewGap = Gap - N7gained.
  NewInner = if NewGap=0 then none else outer + NewGap*(sign toward inner).
  RailRange = (R1..R2 if Dir in {arm_left,arm_right} else C1..C2).
  return Plan(NewBox, Interior, Dir, Outer, RailRange, NewInner).

FILL ORDER by Dir:
  arm_left:   for C in 0..W-1: for R in H-1..0: yield (R,C).
  arm_right:  for C in W-1..0: for R in 0..H-1: yield (R,C).
  arm_top:    for R in 0..H-1: for C in 0..W-1: yield (R,C).
  arm_bottom: for R in H-1..0: for C in W-1..0: yield (R,C).

MAKE INTERIOR(H,W,N7,Order):
  SevenCells = first N7 elements of Order.
  For (Ri,Ci) in [0..H-1]x[0..W-1]: Interior[Ri][Ci] = 7 if (Ri,Ci) in SevenCells else 5.

BUILD GRID(NR,NC,BG,Plans):
  For each (R,C): find first Plan P where cell_in_plan(R,C,P) gives V; else V=BG.

WAVE 35: bbox_fill PSEUDOCODE

DETECT_LEGEND(Grid, BG):
  NR = len(Grid), NC = len(Grid[0]), HalfNR = NR//2
  For LC in 0..NC-2:
    Cands = {R : R in HalfNR..NR-1, Grid[R][LC] != BG}
    If Cands is empty: continue
    LastR = max(Cands)
    Block = scan_up from LastR while Grid[R][LC] != BG
    If Block non-empty: LegRows = sorted(Block); break
  LC1 = LC+1
  LegMap = [(Grid[R][LC], Grid[R][LC1]) for R in LegRows]
  Return (LC, LegRows, LegMap)

IS_ERASE(V, BG): return V == 0 and BG != 0

COMPUTE_INFOS(Grid, BG, LegCells, LegMap):
  For (K,V) in LegMap where not IS_ERASE(V, BG):
    KCells = [(R,C) : Grid[R][C]==K and (R,C) not in LegCells]
    If KCells empty: skip
    (R1,C1,R2,C2) = BBOX(KCells)
    Area = (R2-R1+1)*(C2-C1+1)
    Dense = (len(KCells) == Area)
    Yield (Area, K, V, R1, C1, R2, C2, Dense)
  Sort ascending by Area

CELL_VALUE(R, C, OrigV, BG, LegCells, LegMap, InfosAsc):
  If (R,C) in LegCells: return OrigV
  If OrigV == BG: return FILL_FOR(R, C, InfosAsc) or BG
  (K,V) = LegMap entry for OrigV (if any)
  If K found and IS_ERASE(V, BG): return FILL_FOR(R, C, InfosAsc) or BG
  If K found:
    Find inf(K,V,R1,C1,R2,C2,Dense) where R in R1..R2 and C in C1..C2
    If Dense: return V  else: return OrigV
  Return OrigV  # unmapped color

FILL_FOR(R, C, InfosAsc):
  # InfosAsc sorted ascending; first match = smallest containing bbox
  For inf(K,V,R1,C1,R2,C2,Dense) in InfosAsc:
    If R in R1..R2 and C in C1..C2: return V
  Fail (no enclosing bbox)

BBOX_FILL(Grid):
  BG = Grid[0][0]
  (LC, LegRows, LegMap) = DETECT_LEGEND(Grid, BG)
  LegCells = {(R,C) : R in LegRows, C in {LC, LC+1}}
  InfosAsc = sorted COMPUTE_INFOS(Grid, BG, LegCells, LegMap)
  Out = [[CELL_VALUE(R,C,...) for C in 0..NC-1] for R in 0..NR-1]
  Return Out

WAVE 36: slide_void PSEUDOCODE

FIND_VOID(Grid): return top-left (VR,VC), H, W from bounding box of all 0-cells.
FIND_MARKER(Grid): return top-left (MR,MC), H, W from bounding box of all 2-cells.

PASSABLE(v): return v == 0 or v == 1

ROW_PASSABLE(Grid, FR, C, W):
  For IC in C..C+W-1: if not PASSABLE(Grid[FR][IC]): return False
  Return True

COL_PASSABLE(Grid, R, FC, H):
  For IR in R..R+H-1: if not PASSABLE(Grid[IR][FC]): return False
  Return True

BLOCK_NBRS(Grid, NR, NC, R, C, H, W):
  # Each slide: check only the new cells entering the block
  Nbrs = []
  If R-1 >= 0 and ROW_PASSABLE(Grid, R-1, C, W): Nbrs.append((R-1, C))
  If R+H <= NR-1 and ROW_PASSABLE(Grid, R+H, C, W): Nbrs.append((R+1, C))
  If C-1 >= 0 and COL_PASSABLE(Grid, R, C-1, H): Nbrs.append((R, C-1))
  If C+W <= NC-1 and COL_PASSABLE(Grid, R, C+W, H): Nbrs.append((R, C+1))
  Return Nbrs

BLOCK_BFS(Grid, NR, NC, VR, VC, H, W):
  # BFS over block top-left positions; returns {(R,C): dist}
  Dist = {(VR,VC): 0}
  Queue = [(VR,VC,0)]
  While Queue non-empty:
    (R,C,D) = dequeue
    For (NR2,NC2) in BLOCK_NBRS(Grid, NR, NC, R, C, H, W):
      If (NR2,NC2) not in Dist:
        Dist[(NR2,NC2)] = D+1
        Enqueue (NR2,NC2,D+1)
  Return Dist

IS_DEADEND(Grid, NR, NC, R, C, H, W):
  Return len(BLOCK_NBRS(Grid, NR, NC, R, C, H, W)) == 1

ADJ_MARKER(Grid, NR, NC, R, C, H, W):
  Check all face cells of block (R,C,H,W); return True if any == 2

SLIDE_VOID(Grid):
  VR,VC,H,W = FIND_VOID(Grid)
  MR,MC,_,_ = FIND_MARKER(Grid)
  NR,NC = len(Grid), len(Grid[0])
  Reached = BLOCK_BFS(Grid, NR, NC, VR, VC, H, W)
  DeadEnds = [(Dist[(R,C)],R,C) for (R,C) in Reached
              if (R,C) != (VR,VC) and IS_DEADEND(Grid, NR, NC, R, C, H, W)]
  If DeadEnds:
    (_, TE_R, TE_C) = max(DeadEnds)  # farthest dead-end
    If ADJ_MARKER(Grid, NR, NC, TE_R, TE_C, H, W):
      (TR, TC) = (MR, MC)
    Else:
      (TR, TC) = (TE_R, TE_C)
  Else:
    (TR, TC) = (MR, MC)  # fallback
  OldCells = {(R,C) : R in VR..VR+H-1, C in VC..VC+W-1}
  NewCells = {(R,C) : R in TR..TR+H-1, C in TC..TC+W-1}
  Out[R][C] = 1 if (R,C) in OldCells
            = 0 if (R,C) in NewCells
            = Grid[R][C] otherwise
  Return Out

WAVE 37: concentric_rings (WP-295, Layer 270)
Task 13e47133.

FLATTEN(Grid): return sorted list of all cell values.

MOST_FREQ(Cells): return value V with highest occurrence count.

BG(Grid): MOST_FREQ(FLATTEN(Grid)).

DIV(Grid, BG): let NonBG = [v : v in FLATTEN(Grid), v != BG];
               MOST_FREQ(NonBG).

NBRS4(NR, NC, R, C): {(R+DR, C+DC) : DR-DC in [(-1,0),(1,0),(0,-1),(0,1)],
                       0 <= R+DR <= NR, 0 <= C+DC <= NC}.

NBRS8(NR, NC, R, C): NBRS4(...) union {(R+DR,C+DC) : DR in {-1,0,1},
                      DC in {-1,0,1}, (DR,DC) != (0,0),
                      0 <= R+DR <= NR, 0 <= C+DC <= NC}.

IS_BND(Grid, NR, NC, Div, R, C):
  If R=0 or R=NR or C=0 or C=NC: True
  If any (NR2,NC2) in NBRS8(NR,NC,R,C) and Grid[NR2][NC2]=Div: True
  Else: False.

FLOOD(Grid, NR, NC, Div, Queue, Visited):
  BFS from Queue over NBRS4 neighbours with value != Div;
  return all reached cells.

COMPS(Grid, NR, NC, Div):
  NDCs = all (R,C) where Grid[R][C] != Div;
  partition NDCs into 4-connected components via FLOOD.

BFS_RINGS(Grid, NR, NC, Div, Sources):
  Multi-source BFS from Sources over NBRS4 (cannot cross Div).
  Return {(R,C): distance} ring map.

BUILD_CYCLE(RCPairs, BG):
  Sort RCPairs by ring R ascending.
  MaxRing = max(R : R-Color in RCPairs).
  For i in 0..MaxRing:
    Cycle[i] = Color if i-Color in RCPairs, else BG.
  Return Cycle.

CONCENTRIC_RINGS(Grid):
  NR, NC = dims(Grid).
  BG = BG(Grid); Div = DIV(Grid, BG).
  Comps = COMPS(Grid, NR, NC, Div).
  For each Comp in Comps:
    Bdry0 = [(R,C) : (R,C) in Comp, IS_BND(Grid,NR,NC,Div,R,C)].
    RM = BFS_RINGS(Grid, NR, NC, Div, Bdry0).
    Markers = [(R,Color) : (R,C) in Comp, Grid[R][C] != BG,
               Grid[R][C] != Div, RM[(R,C)] = Ring].
    Cycle = BUILD_CYCLE(Markers, BG).
    CLen = len(Cycle).
  Out[R][C] = Div if Grid[R][C]=Div
            = Cycle[RM[(R,C)] mod CLen] for (R,C) in any Comp.
  Return Out.

WAVE 38: fill_enclosed (WP-296, Layer 271)
FUNCTION fill_enclosed(Grid):
  Flat = FLATTEN(Grid); Srt = MSORT(Flat)
  BG = MOST_COMMON(Srt)
  Ms = [V : COUNT(V in Srt) = 1, V != BG]
  VAdjs = [VADJ(M, Grid, BG) for M in Ms]
  AllComps = ALL_BG_COMPONENTS(Grid, BG)      // list-based BFS
  (FDom, FOthers, FrameSet, VDecContam) = FRAME_INFO(Grid, BG, Ms, VAdjs, AllComps)
  VDec = VDecContam ++ [V in Flat : V not in BG+Ms+VAdjs+FrameSet]
  Pockets = [C in AllComps : IS_POCKET(C, Grid, FrameSet)]
  Assigns = CLASSIFY_ALL(Pockets, Grid, Ms, VAdjs, FDom, FOthers, VDec)
  RETURN APPLY_FILLS(Grid, Assigns)

FUNCTION VADJ(M, Grid, BG):
  Nbrs = [V : (R,C) with Grid[R][C]=M, (AR,AC) 4-adj to (R,C), V=Grid[AR][AC], V!=BG, V!=M]
  IF Nbrs = [] THEN RETURN none ELSE RETURN MOST_COMMON(Nbrs)

FUNCTION ALL_BG_COMPONENTS(Grid, BG):
  AllBG = [(R,C) : Grid[R][C]=BG]; Visited=[]; Comps=[]
  FOR each Cell in AllBG:
    IF Cell not in Visited:
      (Comp, Visited) = BFS_COMP(Grid, BG, [Cell], [Cell]+Visited, [Cell])
      Comps += [Comp]
  RETURN Comps

FUNCTION FRAME_INFO(Grid, BG, Ms, VAdjs, AllComps):
  FSAdj = UNIQUE([V : VA in VAdjs, (R,C) with Grid[R][C]=VA,
                      (NR,NC) 4-adj, V=Grid[NR][NC], V!=BG, V not in Ms+VAdjs])
  IF FSAdj = []:
    FDom = MOST_COMMON([V in Grid : V!=BG, V not in Ms+VAdjs])
    FOthers = other distinct such values; VDecContam = []
  ELSE:
    FDom = MOST_COMMON(FSAdj)
    FOthers = [V in FSAdj, V!=FDom : EXISTS comp C in AllComps
                 where ALL in-grid non-C neighbors of ALL cells in C have value V]
    VDecContam = FSAdj - {FDom} - FOthers
  FrameSet = [FDom] ++ FOthers
  RETURN (FDom, FOthers, FrameSet, VDecContam)

FUNCTION IS_POCKET(Cluster, Grid, FrameSet):
  FrameSet != []
  FOR each (R,C) in Cluster:
    FOR each (NR,NC) 4-adj to (R,C), (NR,NC) in-grid, (NR,NC) not in Cluster:
      Grid[NR][NC] must be in FrameSet
  RETURN true

FUNCTION CLASSIFY_ALL(Pockets, Grid, Ms, VAdjs, FDom, FOthers, VDec):
  IF FOthers != []:
    RETURN [(Cl, Ms[0]) : Cl in Pockets, NOT FDOM_ONLY(Cl, Grid, FDom)]
  Assigns = [(Cl, M) : Cl in Pockets, M = CLEAN_INDICATOR(Cl, Grid, Ms, VAdjs, VDec)]
  IF Assigns = [] AND Pockets != []:
    RETURN [(Cl, Ms[0]) : Cl in Pockets]   // exception: no indicators
  RETURN Assigns

FUNCTION CLEAN_INDICATOR(Cluster, Grid, Ms, VAdjs, VDec):
  FrameNbrs = unique in-grid non-cluster 4-neighbors of Cluster cells
  FOR (FR,FC) in FrameNbrs:
    FOR (AR,AC) 4-adj to (FR,FC):
      IF Grid[AR][AC] in VAdjs:
        VA_Chain = BFS on VA-valued cells starting at (AR,AC)
        IF no cell in VA_Chain is 4-adj to any VDec cell: RETURN Ms[VAdjs.indexOf(VA)]
  RETURN none

FUNCTION FDOM_ONLY(Cluster, Grid, FDom):
  Cluster is rectangular AND all FrameNbrs of Cluster have value FDom

WAVE 39: room_outline (WP-297, Layer 272)
Task: 8f3a5a89.

FUNCTION room_outline(Grid):
  NR = rows(Grid); NC = cols(Grid)
  SR, SC = first (R,C) where Grid[R][C] = 6   // seed
  Vis = FLOOD_FILL_BG8(Grid, SR, SC)           // 4-connected BFS through 8-cells
  WallCells = [(R,C) : Grid[R][C] != 8, Grid[R][C] != 6]
  WallComps = WALL_COMPONENTS(WallCells)        // 4-connected partition
  WallKeep = flatten([C : C in WallComps, EXISTS cell in C 4-adj to Vis])
  BdryWalls = flatten([C : C in WALL_COMPONENTS(WallKeep),
                           EXISTS cell in C on grid boundary])
  RETURN BUILD_OUTPUT(Grid, SR, SC, Vis, WallKeep, BdryWalls)

FUNCTION FLOOD_FILL_BG8(Grid, SR, SC):
  BFS from (SR,SC); expand 4-neighbours with value 8 not yet visited.
  Return msort of all reached (R,C).

FUNCTION WALL_COMPONENTS(Cells):
  While Cells non-empty:
    Seed = first unassigned cell in Cells.
    BFS through Cells 4-neighbours; collect reachable cells as one component.
    Remove component cells from Cells.
  Return list of components.

FUNCTION BUILD_OUTPUT(Grid, SR, SC, Vis, WallKeep, BdryWalls):
  For each (R,C):
    IF R=SR, C=SC           : emit 6           // seed
    ELIF Grid[R][C]=8, (R,C) in Vis:
      IF on grid boundary OR 8-adj to BdryWalls: emit 7   // perimeter
      ELSE                  : emit 8           // interior
    ELIF Grid[R][C]=8       : emit 8           // inaccessible BG
    ELIF (R,C) in WallKeep  : emit Grid[R][C]  // preserved wall
    ELSE                    : emit 8           // erased wall

WAVE 40: grid_tile (WP-298, Layer 273) — 2026-07-01

FUNCTION ARC2_TRANSFORM_GRID_TILE(Grid):
  (Rmin, Cmin) = BBOX_NON7(Grid)          // top-left of 3x3 non-7 region
  (Block, HEdge, VEdge, Corner) = DECODE_TILE(Grid, Rmin, Cmin)
  Return BUILD_OUTPUT(Block, HEdge, VEdge, Corner)

FUNCTION BBOX_NON7(Grid):
  Cells = {(R,C) : Grid[R][C] != 7}
  Return (min R in Cells, min C in Cells)

FUNCTION DECODE_TILE(Grid, R0, C0):
  S = Grid[R0..R0+2][C0..C0+2]    // 3x3 sub-grid
  block  = 7 IF S[0][0]=7 AND S[0][2]=7 AND S[2][0]=7 AND S[2][2]=7 ELSE 0
  v_edge = 7 IF S[0][1]=7 AND S[2][1]=7 ELSE 0
  h_edge = 7 IF S[1][0]=7 AND S[1][2]=7 ELSE 0
  corner = 7 IF S[1][1]=7 ELSE 0
  Return (block, h_edge, v_edge, corner)

FUNCTION BUILD_OUTPUT(Block, HEdge, VEdge, Corner):
  For R in 0..15, C in 0..15:
    RM = R mod 3, CM = C mod 3
    IF RM=0, CM=0: base = Corner
    ELIF RM=0:     base = HEdge
    ELIF CM=0:     base = VEdge
    ELSE:          base = Block
    IF R in 5..10 AND C in 5..10 AND base=0: emit 9
    ELSE: emit base
  Return 16x16 grid

WAVE 41: box_absorb (WP-299, Layer 274)
FUNCTION transform_box_absorb(Grid):
  CR, CC = find_2(Grid)              // locate box centre
  BoxCells = [(CR-1..CR+1, CC-1..CC+1)] in reading order  // 9 cells
  Absorbed = BFS_absorb(Grid, BoxCells, cap=9)
  N = |Absorbed|
  Slots = BoxCells[0..N-1]           // first N box cells
  RETURN build_output(Grid, Absorbed, Slots)

FUNCTION BFS_absorb(Grid, InitQueue, Cap):
  Queue = InitQueue (FIFO)
  Visited = InitQueue
  Absorbed = []
  WHILE Queue not empty AND Cap > 0:
    H = dequeue(Queue)
    New = unvisited non-6 4-neighbours of H in Grid
    Nine = {c in New : Grid[c] = 9}
    Take = Nine[0..min(|Nine|,Cap)-1]
    Absorbed += Take; Cap -= |Take|
    Visited += New; enqueue(Queue, New)  // BFS: new at back
  RETURN Absorbed

FUNCTION build_output(Grid, Absorbed, Slots):
  FOR each cell RC:
    IF RC in Slots:    emit 9
    ELIF RC in Absorbed: emit 7 (BG)
    ELSE: emit Grid[RC]

WAVE 42: section_sort (WP-300, Layer 275)

FUNCTION section_sort(Grid):
  (HDivs, VDivs) = find_dividers(Grid)       // rows/cols where all cells = 6
  RSegs = make_segments(nrows(Grid), HDivs)   // (Start,End) pairs between dividers
  CSegs = make_segments(ncols(Grid), VDivs)
  Kind = classify(HDivs, VDivs)               // h | v | td
  Secs = extract_sections(Grid, RSegs, CSegs) // list of sec(SubGrid, Idx, Count)
  Ordered = sort_sections(Kind, Secs)         // ascending by Count; ties by -Idx
  OutDir = output_direction(Kind, Secs)       // v or h
  RETURN assemble(Ordered, OutDir)

FUNCTION find_dividers(Grid):
  HDivs = [R : Row R of Grid has all cells = 6]
  VDivs = [C : Column C of Grid has all cells = 6]

FUNCTION make_segments(N, Divs):
  Bounds = [-1] ++ Divs ++ [N]
  RETURN [(A+1, B-1) : (A,B) adjacent pairs in Bounds]

FUNCTION classify(HDivs, VDivs):
  IF HDivs=[] RETURN h
  IF VDivs=[] RETURN v
  RETURN td

FUNCTION extract_sections(Grid, RSegs, CSegs):
  FOR RI in 0..len(RSegs)-1, CI in 0..len(CSegs)-1:
    Idx = RI * len(CSegs) + CI
    Sub = subgrid(Grid, RSegs[RI], CSegs[CI])
    N = count non-BG non-6 cells in Sub
    YIELD sec(Sub, Idx, N)

FUNCTION sort_sections(Kind, Secs):
  IF Kind = v: RETURN reverse(Secs)
  IF Kind = h: RETURN Secs
  IF Kind = td:
    Keys = [(N, -Idx, Sec) : sec(Sub, Idx, N) in Secs]
    RETURN [Sec : sorted Keys ascending by (N, -Idx)]

FUNCTION output_direction(Kind, Secs):
  IF Kind = v: RETURN h
  IF Kind = h: RETURN v
  IF Kind = td:
    TotalH = sum of bbox heights of all sections
    TotalW = sum of bbox widths of all sections
    IF TotalH > TotalW: RETURN v ELSE RETURN h

FUNCTION assemble(Ordered, v):
  DivRow = row of all-6 with same width as sections
  RETURN vstack(Ordered, DivRow)   // sections interleaved with DivRow

FUNCTION assemble(Ordered, h):
  FOR each row index R:
    RETURN hstack([Sec[R] : Sec in Ordered])  // rows interleaved with 6-columns

WAVE 43 PSEUDOCODE: frame_stamp

FUNCTION frame_stamp(Grid):
  BG = mode(all cells of Grid)
  NR, NC = dimensions of Grid
  LastCol = NC - 1
  Row0 = Grid[0]
  BdrBG = mode(Row0[4..LastCol], excluding BG)
  ColAnoms = {C: K for K in 4..LastCol if Row0[K] not in {BdrBG, BG}} as Color->[Cols]
  RowAnoms = {C: R for R in 0..NR-1 if Grid[R][LastCol] not in {BdrBG, BG}} as Color->[Rows]
  LShapes  = {C: [(R,C)...] for R in 0..NR-1, C in 0..3 if Grid[R][C] != BG} as Color->Cells
  Stamps = []
  FOR each (Color, Cells) in LShapes:
    IF Color in ColAnoms AND Color in RowAnoms:
      N = |Cells|
      SumR = sum(R for (R,C) in Cells)
      SumC = sum(C for (R,C) in Cells)
      Pls = [(R, K) for R in RowAnoms[Color], K in ColAnoms[Color]]
      APPEND (N, stamp(Color, Cells, SumR, SumC, N, Pls)) to Stamps
  SORT Stamps by N descending (largest first)
  Out = copy of Grid
  FOR each Color in placed colors: ERASE left-side Cells to BG in Out
  FOR each stamp in Stamps (descending N order):
    FOR each (NewR, NewK) in Pls:
      DR = round((NewR * N - SumR) / N)
      DC = round((NewK * N - SumC) / N)
      FOR each (R, C) in Cells:
        IF 0 <= R+DR < NR AND 0 <= C+DC < NC:
          Out[R+DR][C+DC] = Color
  RETURN Out

WAVE 44: jigsaw_fill (WP-302, Layer 277) — 2026-07-01
PROCEDURE arc2_transform(jigsaw_fill, Grid, Out):
  (Tmpl, Hole, ObjGrid, ObjBg) = jf_find_split(Grid)
  Holes = jf_holes(Tmpl, Hole)       // list of R-C pairs
  Pieces = jf_pieces(ObjGrid, ObjBg) // list of [R-C-V ...] components
  TR = len(Tmpl); TC = len(Tmpl[0])
  PiecesWP = augment(Pieces, Holes, TR, TC)
  Sorted = msort by first element (placement count)
  ColorMap = cover(Sorted, Holes)
  Out = apply(Tmpl, ColorMap)

PROCEDURE jf_find_split(Grid):
  FOR each row split point r:
    Tmpl = Grid[0..r]; Obj = Grid[r+1..]
    IF check_tmpl_obj(Tmpl, Obj): RETURN (Tmpl, Hole, Obj, ObjBg)
    Tmpl = Grid[r..]; Obj = Grid[0..r-1]
    IF check_tmpl_obj(Tmpl, Obj): RETURN (Tmpl, Hole, Obj, ObjBg)
  FOR each col split point c:
    Tmpl = Grid[*][0..c]; Obj = Grid[*][c+1..]
    IF check_tmpl_obj(Tmpl, Obj): RETURN (Tmpl, Hole, Obj, ObjBg)
    Tmpl = Grid[*][c..]; Obj = Grid[*][0..c-1]
    IF check_tmpl_obj(Tmpl, Obj): RETURN (Tmpl, Hole, Obj, ObjBg)

PROCEDURE check_tmpl_obj(Tmpl, Obj):
  TFlat = flatten(Tmpl)
  IF distinct(TFlat) != 2: RETURN False
  Solid = TFlat[0][0]  // corner cell = solid color
  Hole = the other distinct color
  HC = count(TFlat, Hole)
  IF HC == 0: RETURN False
  OFlat = flatten(Obj)
  IF distinct(OFlat) <= 2: RETURN False
  ObjBg = mode(OFlat)
  PC = count(OFlat, x: x != ObjBg)
  RETURN PC == HC

PROCEDURE jf_pieces(Grid, Bg):
  Visited = {}; Components = []
  FOR R, C in row-major order:
    IF (R,C) not in Visited AND Grid[R][C] != Bg:
      Comp = BFS({(R,C)}, Grid, Bg, Visited)
      Components.append(Comp)
  RETURN Components

PROCEDURE augment(Pieces, Holes, TR, TC):
  FOR piece in Pieces:
    Norm = normalize(piece)  // shift to (0,0) bounding box
    Placements = valid_placements(Norm, Holes, TR, TC)
    YIELD (len(Placements), Norm, Placements)

PROCEDURE cover(PiecesWP, Holes):
  IF PiecesWP empty: IF Holes empty: RETURN {}; ELSE FAIL
  (N, Norm, Placements) = PiecesWP[0]; Rest = PiecesWP[1..]
  FOR (R0, C0) in Placements:
    Cells = place(Norm, R0, C0)
    IF all (R,C) in Cells are in Holes:
      NewHoles = Holes - {(R,C) for (R,C,V) in Cells}
      Map = cover(Rest, NewHoles)
      RETURN Map + {(R,C): V for (R,C,V) in Cells}
  FAIL

Score: 41/120 = 34.17% -> 42/120 = 35.00%.

WAVE 45: stair_fill (WP-303, Layer 278) — 2026-07-01
Task 28a6681f. Fill staircase step pockets with 1-cells.

PROCEDURE stair_fill(Grid):
  N = count_ones(Grid)
  IF N == 0: RETURN Grid
  NR = rows(Grid); NC = cols(Grid)
  Pockets = {}
  // Phase 1: doubly-bounded pockets (left AND right are staircase walls)
  FOR R = NR-1 DOWN TO 0:
    IF N == 0: BREAK
    Ranges = open_runs(Grid[R])     // maximal runs of non-wall cells
    DB = [r FOR r IN Ranges WHERE left_wall(Grid[R],r) AND right_wall(Grid[R],r) AND below_ok(Grid,R,r,Pockets)]
    SORT DB BY gap_size ASCENDING
    FOR (C_L, C_R) IN DB:
      FOR C = C_L TO C_R:
        IF N == 0: BREAK
        ADD (R,C) TO Pockets; N -= 1
  // Phase 2: single-bounded pockets (left=wall, right=grid boundary)
  IF N > 0:
    FOR R = NR-1 DOWN TO 0:
      IF N == 0: BREAK
      Ranges = open_runs(Grid[R])
      SB = [r FOR r IN Ranges WHERE left_wall(Grid[R],r) AND C_R==NC-1 AND below_ok(Grid,R,r,Pockets)]
      SORT SB BY gap_size ASCENDING
      FOR (C_L, C_R) IN SB:
        FOR C = C_L TO C_R:
          IF N == 0: BREAK
          ADD (R,C) TO Pockets; N -= 1
  // Build output
  FOR R,C IN Grid:
    IF (R,C) IN Pockets: Out[R][C] = 1
    ELIF is_wall(Grid[R][C]): Out[R][C] = Grid[R][C]
    ELSE: Out[R][C] = 0
  RETURN Out

PROCEDURE below_ok(Grid, R, C_L, C_R, Pockets):
  IF R == NR-1: RETURN TRUE          // grid bottom = floor
  FOR C = C_L TO C_R:
    IF NOT (is_wall(Grid[R+1][C]) OR (R+1,C) IN Pockets):
      RETURN FALSE
  RETURN TRUE

Score: 42/120 = 35.00% -> 43/120 = 35.83%.

WAVE 46: two_join (WP-304, Layer 279) — 2026-07-01

PROCEDURE two_join(Grid):
  NR = rows(Grid); NC = cols(Grid)
  AllPos = {(R,C) : Grid[R][C] != 1}
  Sevens = {(R,C) : Grid[R][C] == 7}
  G1, G2 = 7_cluster_split(Sevens)   // two 4-connected groups of 7-cells

  FOR ordering IN [(G1, G2), (G2, G1)]:
    base_7, shift_7 = ordering
    ObjA = BFS(base_7, AllPos)         // BFS through all non-1 cells from base_7
    ObjB = AllPos - ObjA               // everything else (includes isolated pieces)
    dr = min_row(base_7) - min_row(shift_7) - 1
    dc = min_col(base_7) - min_col(shift_7)
    ObjB_shifted = {(R+dr, C+dc) : (R,C) IN ObjB}
    IF all positions in ObjB_shifted have R>=0, C>=0:
      size[ordering] = bounding_box_area(ObjA UNION ObjB_shifted)
    ELSE:
      size[ordering] = infinity

  Pick ordering with minimum size (smaller merged bbox = correct connection)
  Out = grid of 1s with dimensions max_row+1 x max_col+1
  FOR (R,C) IN FinalA UNION FinalBs: Out[R][C] = 4
  RETURN Out

PROCEDURE 7_cluster_split(Sevens):
  seed = first element of Sevens
  G1 = BFS_within_7s(seed, Sevens)    // BFS staying within 7-cell set
  G2 = Sevens - G1
  RETURN G1, G2

WP-305: shape_count (Layer 280, Task 58490d8a)

PROCEDURE shape_count(Grid):
  (TR0,TR1,TC0,TC1) = bbox of all 0-cells in Grid  // template region
  Colors = [(TR,V) : TR odd in [1..TR1-TR0], V = first nonzero in Grid[TR0+TR][TC0..TC1]]
  NTR = TR1-TR0+1; NTC = TC1-TC0+1
  Out = NTR x NTC grid of 0s
  FOR (TR, Color) IN Colors:
    Cells = sorted {(R,C) : Grid[R][C]=Color, (R,C) not in template region}
    Count = 0
    WHILE Cells not empty:
      Seed = first element of Cells (top-left order)
      Inst = EXPAND({Seed}, Cells)
      Count += 1
      Cells = Cells - Inst
    FOR i IN 0..Count-1: Out[TR][1+2*i] = Color
  RETURN Out

PROCEDURE EXPAND(Cur, All):
  LOOP:
    (R0,R1,C0,C1) = tight_bbox(Cur)
    Expanded = {p in All : R0-1 <= p.r <= R1+1, C0-1 <= p.c <= C1+1}
    IF sorted(Expanded) == sorted(Cur): RETURN Cur
    Cur = Expanded

WP-306: stamp_grid (Layer 281, Task dfadab01)
FUNCTION stamp_grid(Grid) -> Out:
  BG = most_common_color(Grid)
  SHAPE_FOUND, SC, SR0, SC0 = find_shape(Grid, BG)
  IF SHAPE_FOUND:
    MVal = identify_stamp_pattern(Grid, SC, SR0, SC0)
    DefR = SR0 + 4, DefC = SC0 + 4
    Markers = {(R,C,V) : Grid[R][C]=V, V!=BG,
               NOT(V==SC AND SR0<=R<=SR0+3 AND SC0<=C<=SC0+3),
               NOT(R==DefR AND C==DefC)}
  ELSE:
    Markers = {(R,C,V) : Grid[R][C]=V, V!=BG}
  Out = all_BG_grid(NRows, NCols)
  FOR EACH (MR, MC, MV) in Markers:
    StampColor, Offsets = STAMP_DEF[MV]
    FOR EACH (DR, DC) in Offsets:
      Out[MR+DR][MC+DC] = StampColor
  RETURN Out

FUNCTION find_shape(Grid, BG) -> (SC, SR0, SC0):
  FOR EACH color SC != BG:
    Cells = {(R,C) : Grid[R][C] == SC}
    IF len(Cells) > 1:
      SR0=minR, SR1=maxR, SC0=minC, SC1=maxC
      IF SR1-SR0==3 AND SC1-SC0==3: RETURN (SC, SR0, SC0)
  RETURN NOT_FOUND

STAMP_DEF = {
  2: (color=4, [(0,0),(0,1),(0,2),(0,3),(1,0),(1,3),(2,0),(2,3),(3,0),(3,1),(3,2),(3,3)]),
  3: (color=1, [(0,1),(0,2),(1,0),(1,3),(2,0),(2,3),(3,1),(3,2)]),
  5: (color=6, [(0,0),(0,1),(1,0),(1,1),(2,2),(2,3),(3,2),(3,3)]),
  8: (color=7, [(0,0),(0,3),(1,1),(1,2),(2,1),(2,2),(3,0),(3,3)])}

WP-307: layout_stack (Layer 282, Task 291dc1e1)
Pseudocode:

FUNCTION layout_stack(Grid) -> Output:
  (CR, CC) = find_corner(Grid)   // cell with value 0 at a grid corner
  AdjVal = Grid[CR][adjacent_to_CC_inward]
  Mode = (AdjVal == 1) ? row_major : col_major
  PrimReverse = (CR == last_row)
  SecReverse = (CC == last_col)
  Interior = Grid minus row CR, minus col CC

  IF Mode == col_major:
    Bands = find_col_bands(Interior)    // consecutive active col groups
    IF SecReverse: reverse Bands
    AllBlocks = []
    FOR Band in Bands:
      Stretches = find_row_stretches(Interior, Band)  // max consecutive active rows
      IF PrimReverse: reverse Stretches
      FOR Stretch in Stretches:
        AllBlocks.append(rotate_90_ccw(extract_subgrid(Interior, Stretch, Band)))
  ELSE:
    RowBands = find_row_bands(Interior)
    IF PrimReverse: reverse RowBands
    AllBlocks = []
    FOR RBand in RowBands:
      ColStretches = find_col_stretches(Interior, RBand)
      IF SecReverse: reverse ColStretches
      FOR Stretch in ColStretches:
        AllBlocks.append(extract_subgrid(Interior, RBand, Stretch))

  MaxW = max(width(B) for B in AllBlocks)
  Output = []
  FOR Block in AllBlocks:
    FOR Row in Block:
      Pad = (MaxW - len(Row)) // 2
      Output.append([8]*Pad + Row + [8]*(MaxW-len(Row)-Pad))

FUNCTION rotate_90_ccw(Grid[R][C]) -> Grid[C][R]:
  Output[i][j] = Grid[j][C-1-i]   // column C-1-i of input = output row i

FUNCTION frame_assemble(Grid) -> Output:
  Flat = flatten(Grid)
  BG = mode(Flat)
  NonBg = [v for v in Flat if v != BG]
  ColorCounts = {v: count(v, NonBg) for v in distinct(NonBg)}
  MaxCount = max(ColorCounts.values())
  FrameColors = {v for v, n in ColorCounts if n * 2 >= MaxCount}
  FrameCells = [(r,c) for r,c in Grid if Grid[r][c] in FrameColors]
  R1,R2,C1,C2 = bbox(FrameCells)
  TR = R2-R1+1; TC = C2-C1+1
  Holes = [(r,c) for r in R1..R2, c in C1..C2 if Grid[r][c] == BG]
  AllComps = find_4connected_components(Grid, BG)
  PieceComps = [comp for comp in AllComps
                if no cell in comp has color in FrameColors]
  PiecesWP = []
  FOR each piece in PieceComps:
    Norm = normalize(piece)
    MaxDR = max(dr for dr,dc,v in Norm)
    MaxDC = max(dc for dr,dc,v in Norm)
    Placements = [(R1+dr0, C1+dc0) for dr0 in 0..TR-MaxDR-1,
                                        dc0 in 0..TC-MaxDC-1
                  if all (R1+dr0+dr, C1+dc0+dc) in Holes for dr,dc,v in Norm]
    PiecesWP.append((len(Placements), Norm, Placements))
  sort PiecesWP by len(Placements) ascending
  ColorMap = {}
  backtrack_cover(PiecesWP, Holes, ColorMap)
  Output = subgrid(Grid, R1..R2, C1..C2) with (r,c) -> ColorMap.get((r,c), Grid[r][c])

Wave 52 - plus_mark (WP-310, Layer 285, task 1818057f):

  FUNCTION plus_mark(Grid):
    H = num_rows(Grid)
    W = num_cols(Grid)
    plus_cells = {}
    FOR R IN 1..H-2:          // interior rows only
      FOR C IN 1..W-2:        // interior cols only
        IF Grid[R][C] = 4 AND Grid[R-1][C] = 4 AND Grid[R+1][C] = 4
               AND Grid[R][C-1] = 4 AND Grid[R][C+1] = 4:
          plus_cells.add({(R,C),(R-1,C),(R+1,C),(R,C-1),(R,C+1)})
    Out = copy(Grid)
    FOR (R,C) IN plus_cells:
      Out[R][C] = 8
    RETURN Out

Wave 53 - template_expand (WP-311, Layer 286, task c4d067a0):
  FUNCTION template_expand(Grid):
    BG = mode(flatten(Grid))
    template_cells = {(R,C) : Grid[R][C] != BG and all 4 neighbours are BG}
    seed_cells = {(R,C) : Grid[R][C] != BG and not in template_cells}
    TRows = sorted distinct row indices in template_cells
    TCols = sorted distinct col indices in template_cells
    SeedRowMin = min row in seed_cells
    SeedRowMax = max row in seed_cells
    BH = SeedRowMax - SeedRowMin + 1
    col_runs = contiguous_column_runs(seed_cells at row SeedRowMin)
    BW = col_runs[0].end - col_runs[0].start + 1
    Stride = col_runs[1].start - col_runs[0].start
    SeedColors[i] = Grid[SeedRowMin][col_runs[i].start]
    Find (L, C0) such that: for all i in 0..len(SeedColors)-1:
      Grid[TRows[L]][TCols[C0+i]] == SeedColors[i]
    AnchorRow = SeedRowMin - L * Stride
    AnchorCol = col_runs[0].start - C0 * Stride
    FOR each cell (R, C):
      LI = (R - AnchorRow) // Stride
      CGI = (C - AnchorCol) // Stride
      IF LI and CGI in bounds AND in-block offsets < BH and BW:
        TV = Grid[TRows[LI]][TCols[CGI]]
        IF TV != BG: Out[R][C] = TV ELSE Out[R][C] = Grid[R][C]
      ELSE: Out[R][C] = Grid[R][C]
    RETURN Out
Score: 50/120 = 41.67% -> 51/120 = 42.50%.

noise_erase (Layer 287, task 71e489b6):
  FUNCTION transform_noise_erase(Grid):
    H = rows(Grid), W = cols(Grid)
    stray0 = {}
    FOR each cell (R,C) with Grid[R][C] == 0:
      ones = count of in-bounds 4-neighbors with value 1
      avail = count of in-bounds 4-neighbors
      IF ones >= min(3, avail): add (R,C) to stray0_seeds
    BFS from stray0_seeds:
      FOR each (R,C) in queue:
        FOR each 4-neighbor (NR,NC) with Grid[NR][NC] == 0 and (NR,NC) not in stray0:
          IF count of 1-valued 4-neighbors of (NR,NC) >= 2:
            add (NR,NC) to stray0, enqueue (NR,NC)
    frame = {}
    FOR each (R,C) in stray0:
      FOR each 8-neighbor (NR,NC) in bounds and not in stray0:
        add (NR,NC) to frame
    stray1 = {}
    FOR each cell (R,C) with Grid[R][C] == 1:
      ones = count of in-bounds 4-neighbors with value 1
      IF ones <= 1: add (R,C) to stray1
    FOR each cell (R,C):
      IF (R,C) in stray0: Out[R][C] = 0
      ELSE IF (R,C) in frame: Out[R][C] = 7
      ELSE IF (R,C) in stray1: Out[R][C] = 0
      ELSE: Out[R][C] = Grid[R][C]
    RETURN Out

pocket_shot (Layer 288, WP-313):
  FUNCTION pocket_shot(Grid):
    BG = most_common_value(Grid)
    Twos = [R-C | Grid[R][C] = 2 for all (R,C)]
    Blocks = connected_component_bboxes(Grid, Twos, value=2)
    ZeroSet = {}, TwoSet = {}, EraseSet = {}
    FOR each Block (R1-R2-C1-C2) in Blocks:
      found_dir = None
      FOR D in [up, down, left, right]:
        XPegs = []
        valid = True
        leading = R1 if D=up else R2 if D=down else C1 if D=left else C2
        FOR each slice in block (col for vertical D, row for horizontal D):
          XPos = scan_skip_bg2(Grid, BG, leading, slice, D)
          IF XPos fails OR not valid_peg(Grid, BG, XPos, D):
            valid = False; break
          XPegs.append(dim(XPos, D))  -- row for vertical, col for horizontal
        IF valid AND all XPegs equal:
          Land = compute_landing(Block, D, XPegs[0])
          found_dir = D; break
      IF found_dir != None:
        ZeroSet += original_and_trail(Block, found_dir, Land)
        TwoSet  += landing_cells(Land)
      ELSE:
        EraseSet += all_cells(Block)
    FOR each cell (R,C) in Grid:
      IF (R,C) in TwoSet:  Out[R][C] = 2
      ELIF (R,C) in ZeroSet: Out[R][C] = 0
      ELIF (R,C) in EraseSet: Out[R][C] = BG
      ELSE: Out[R][C] = Grid[R][C]
    RETURN Out

  FUNCTION valid_peg(Grid, BG, XR-XC, D):
    OppPos = neighbor(XR-XC, opposite(D))
    IF in_bounds(OppPos) AND Grid[OppPos] != BG: RETURN False  -- Cond1
    ParPos = neighbor(XR-XC, D)
    IF NOT in_bounds(ParPos) OR Grid[ParPos] = BG OR Grid[ParPos] = 2: RETURN False  -- Cond2
    PerpArms = count of neighbors of ParPos in perpendicular(D) that are arm-cells
    RETURN PerpArms >= 2  -- Cond3

shape_walk (Layer 289, WP-314):
  FUNCTION shape_walk(Grid):
    DC = first column index where all rows have value 4
    5R, 5C = position of cell with value 5
    OutC5 = 5C - DC - 1
    NbRows = [R | some col in 0..DC-1 is non-zero at row R]
    SectStarts = first row of each group of 3 consecutive rows in NbRows
    MidCol = DC - 3
    LeftBlks = [blk(color, dir, len) | SR in SectStarts, block at (SR, 0)]
    MidBlks  = [blk(color, dir, len) | SR in SectStarts, block at (SR, MidCol)]
    AllBlks = LeftBlks ++ MidBlks
    ChainCells = walk_chain(AllBlks, row=1, col=OutC5)
    Out = H x DC grid of 0s, with Out[0][OutC5]=5 and each (R,C,Color) in ChainCells
    RETURN Out

  FUNCTION classify_block(Grid, R, C):
    Raw = 3x3 cells at top-left (R, C)
    Shape = normalize(Raw)  -- 0->0, non-zero->1
    MATCH Shape:
      [[1,0,1],[1,0,1],[1,1,1]] -> (left,  2)
      [[1,1,0],[1,0,1],[0,1,0]] -> (right, 3)
      [[1,0,1],[0,1,0],[0,1,0]] -> (down,  2)
      [[1,1,1],[0,1,0],[1,0,1]] -> (left,  4)

  FUNCTION walk_chain(Blocks, R, C):
    IF Blocks is empty: RETURN []
    blk(Color, Dir, Len) = head(Blocks)
    Seg = cells_for_segment(R, C, Dir, Len)
    Tip = last cell of Seg
    Rest = walk_chain(tail(Blocks), Tip.row+1, Tip.col)
    RETURN [(Ri, Ci, Color) | (Ri,Ci) in Seg] ++ Rest

  FUNCTION cells_for_segment(R, C, Dir, Len):
    IF Dir = left:  RETURN [(R, C-i) | i in 0..Len-1]
    IF Dir = right: RETURN [(R, C+i) | i in 0..Len-1]
    IF Dir = down:  RETURN [(R+i, C) | i in 0..Len-1]

FUNCTION arc2_transform_frame_reflect(Grid) -> Out:
  FR, FC = first non-8 cell row-major
  HoleR = FR+3; HoleC = FC+3
  FOR each sub-region (RSub,CSub) != (1,1):
    Sub = extract_3x3(Grid, FR+RSub*3, FC+CSub*3)
    Rot = rotate_180(Sub)
    place Rot at (FR+(2*RSub-1)*3, FC+(2*CSub-1)*3)
  HoleMods = fill_hole(Grid, FR, FC, HoleR, HoleC)
  RETURN apply_mods(Grid, StampMods + HoleMods)

FUNCTION fill_hole(...):
  Filler = Grid[FR][FC+4]; AI = Grid[HoleR-1][HoleC+1]
  FOR i,j in {0,1,2}:
    cell = mix(L[i], T[j], AI, Filler, corner(i,j))
  WHERE L=[L0,AI,L2], T=[T0,AI,T2]

FUNCTION arc2_transform_cross_reflect(Grid) -> Out:
  BG = Grid[0][0]
  R, C = find cross row and col (full line of same non-BG value)
  Anchor = first non-BG value found scanning TR quadrant (rows<R, cols>C)
  (TL_MinR, TL_MaxR, TL_MinC, _) = bbox of Anchor in TL quadrant
  N_tl = TL_MaxR - TL_MinR + 1
  Sats = distinct non-BG non-Anchor values in TL
  FOR each SV in Sats:
    (MinR, MaxR, MinC, MaxC) = bbox(SV, TL)
    SH = MaxR - MinR + 1; SW = MaxC - MinC + 1
    DR = MinR - TL_MinR; DC = MinC - TL_MinC
    SatInfos += (SV, DR, DC, SH, SW)
  (TR_MinR, TR_MaxR, TR_MinC, _) = bbox(Anchor, TR); N_tr = TR_MaxR - TR_MinR + 1
  (BR_MinR, BR_MaxR, BR_MinC, _) = bbox(Anchor, BR); N_br = BR_MaxR - BR_MinR + 1
  (BL_MinR, BL_MaxR, BL_MinC, _) = bbox(Anchor, BL); N_bl = BL_MaxR - BL_MinR + 1
  AllMods = []
  FOR each (SV, DR, DC, SH, SW) in SatInfos:
    TR: NewDC = N_tl-DC-SW
        DR_q=DR*N_tr//N_tl; DC_q=NewDC*N_tr//N_tl
        H_q=SH*N_tr//N_tl; W_q=SW*N_tr//N_tl
        place block SV at (TR_MinR+DR_q, TR_MinC+DC_q), size H_q x W_q
    BR: NewDR=N_tl-DR-SH; NewDC=N_tl-DC-SW
        DR_q=NewDR*N_br//N_tl; DC_q=NewDC*N_br//N_tl
        H_q=SH*N_br//N_tl; W_q=SW*N_br//N_tl
        place block SV at (BR_MinR+DR_q, BR_MinC+DC_q), size H_q x W_q
    BL: NewDR=N_tl-DR-SH
        DR_q=NewDR*N_bl//N_tl; DC_q=DC*N_bl//N_tl
        H_q=SH*N_bl//N_tl; W_q=SW*N_bl//N_tl
        place block SV at (BL_MinR+DR_q, BL_MinC+DC_q), size H_q x W_q
  RETURN apply_mods(Grid, AllMods)

Layer 292 - WP-317 - scaled_frame pseudocode

FUNCTION scaled_frame(Grid):
  FC, R0, C0, R1, C1 = find_frame(Grid)
  Holes = [R-C | interior(R0,C0,R1,C1), Grid[R][C]=0]
  HComps = connected_components_4(Holes)
  Objects = background_objects(Grid, FC, R0,C0,R1,C1)   // size >= 4
  Scale = round(sqrt(GCD(cell_counts(Objects))))
  Matches = match_holes_to_objects(HComps, Objects, Scale)
  OutH = (R1-R0+1)*Scale; OutW = (C1-C0+1)*Scale
  RETURN [[cell_color(R,C,Grid,FC,R0,C0,Scale,Matches)
           FOR C IN 0..OutW-1] FOR R IN 0..OutH-1]

FUNCTION find_frame(Grid):
  FOR EACH distinct non-0 color FC IN Grid:
    FCells = cells of color FC
    R0,C0,R1,C1 = bounding_box(FCells)
    IF R1 > R0+1 AND C1 > C0+1
       AND all_border_cells(Grid, FC, R0,C0,R1,C1)
       AND exists hole inside interior:
      RETURN FC, R0, C0, R1, C1

FUNCTION background_objects(Grid, FC, R0,C0,R1,C1):
  Cells = [V-R-C | Grid[R][C]=V, V!=0, V!=FC,
           (R<R0 OR R>R1 OR C<C0 OR C>C1)]
  Comps = connected_components_4(R-C positions)
  RETURN [Color-Cells | component with size >= 4]

FUNCTION match_holes_to_objects(HComps, Objects, Scale):
  Scale2 = Scale * Scale
  HAnnot = [(len(HC), centroid_col(HC), HC) FOR HC IN HComps]
  OAnnot = [(len(Cells)//Scale2, centroid_col(Cells), Color)
            FOR Color-Cells IN Objects]
  HSort = sort(HAnnot); OSort = sort(OAnnot)
  RETURN [HC-Color | (_, _, HC) IN HSort, (_, _, Color) IN OSort]

FUNCTION cell_color(R,C,Grid,FC,R0,C0,Scale,Matches):
  FRow = R0 + R // Scale; FCol = C0 + C // Scale
  IF Grid[FRow][FCol] = 0:
    RETURN fill_color(Matches, FRow, FCol)
  ELSE: RETURN FC

Layer 293 - WP-318 - layout_tile pseudocode
FUNCTION layout_tile(Grid):
  DivRows = rows where all values in {0,5} AND count(5s)*2 >= row_width
  DivCols = cols where all values in {0,5} AND count(5s) >= 1
  [RG0, RG1, RG2] = split content rows (non-DivRows) into 3 contiguous groups
  ColGroups = non-DivCols split into contiguous groups, filtered to non-empty
  S = len(ColGroups[0])
  Templates = [subgrid(Grid, RG0, CG) for CG in ColGroups]
  Markers = [first non-zero non-5 cell in subgrid(Grid, RG2, CG) for CG]
  Layouts = [subgrid(Grid, RG1, CG) for CG in ColGroups]
  Assigns = [(r,c,TI): for each Layout, each non-zero non-5 cell (r,c)=V,
             find template TI containing V]
  Build S*S x S*S output: cell(OR,OC):
    BR=OR//S, BC=OC//S, IR=OR mod S, IC=OC mod S
    IF (BR,BC,TI) in Assigns:
      TV = Templates[TI][IR][IC]
      OV = 0 if TV==0 else Markers[TI]
    ELSE OV = 0

Wave 61 - frame_pour (WP-319, Layer 294)
1. Detect BG (most frequent), F (frame color), FC (fill-seed).
2. FC centroid determines opening direction (opposite side).
3. Compute Bnd, wall extents LW/RW, float slope S=2.0/DC.
4. Interior shadow-cone: scan far->Bnd; fill range from F-cells (degenerate fallback to wall extents); track blocked set from B-cells.
5. Exterior cone: depth loop; E=truncate((D-1)/S); range [LW-E,RW+E]; blocked set inherited.
6. Apply: BG cells in fill set -> FC.
SPARC: Specification v287, Pseudocode v279, Architecture v280, Refinement v339, Completion v345.

Wave 62 - shape_slide (WP-320, Layer 295) [Mentova]
1. Detect background BG (most frequent cell value).
2. Collect all non-BG cells as R-C-V triples.
3. BFS flood-fill to find all 4-connected components.
4. Classify: size-1 components = seeds; size>1 = shapes.
5. Split seeds: on any grid edge = anchor; otherwise = floating.
6. For each anchor seed: left/right edge -> vert slide (target row = anchor row);
   top/bottom edge -> horiz slide (target col = anchor col).
7. For each shape: find unique-color cell (appears exactly once in component);
   if its color matches an anchor seed, compute displacement to align with target;
   shift all cells; discard out-of-bounds cells.
8. For each floating seed with matching anchor color: slide to target row/col.
9. Apply all moves: vacate old positions (replace with BG), fill new positions.
SPARC: Specification v288, Pseudocode v280, Architecture v281, Refinement v340, Completion v346.

Wave 64 - snake_frame (WP-322, Layer 297, Acc_362)
Rule: snake_frame
Task: cb2d8a2c
Pattern: a single pointer cell (value 3) on a grid edge traces a rectangular wrap-path
  around each snake object (connected 1/2 body). Pointer navigates nearest-to-farthest
  from its edge; at each snake, it turns perpendicular based on 1-distribution (towards
  the half with more 1s), reaches the far boundary (snake_edge +/- (num_1s+1)), then
  returns to primary direction. All 1s in snake cells become 2s in the output.
FR-ARC2-322-1: Exactly four distinct values {1,2,3,8} in first training input required;
  exactly one cell holds value 3.
FR-ARC2-322-2: Near boundary for vertical snakes from right/left edge:
  NearC = RC + N1 + 1 (right edge) or NearC = LC - N1 - 1 (left edge).
FR-ARC2-322-3: Far boundary direction: TopH >= BotH -> go to BR + N1 + 1 (clamped);
  else go to TR - N1 - 1 (clamped).
FR-ARC2-322-4: For top/bottom edge (horizontal snakes): near row = TR - N1 - 1 or
  BR + N1 + 1; far col uses LH >= RH -> go right, else go left; grid boundary overrides.
Predicates: cbsf_ptr, cbsf_cells, cbsf_row, cbsf_partition, cbsf_bfs, cbsf_adj4,
  cbsf_analyse, cbsf_is1, cbsf_edge, cbsf_order, cbsf_trace, cbsf_hline, cbsf_vline,
  cbsf_out, cbsf_outrow,
  arc2_transform(snake_frame), arc2_induce_rule(snake_frame).
File: Mentova/src/mentova/games/arc_benchmark_2.pl
Task solved: cb2d8a2c. Score: 60/120 = 50.00% -> 61/120 = 50.83%.
SPARC: Specification v290, Pseudocode v282, Architecture v283, Refinement v342, Completion v348.


Wave 64 - snake_frame (WP-322, Layer 297)
1. Locate pointer (value 3): scan rows for cell with value 3; record PR, PC.
2. Collect snake cells: scan all cells for values 1 or 2; store as R-C pairs.
3. Partition into components: BFS from each unclaimed cell; 4-adjacency.
4. Analyse each component: bounding rows TR/BR, cols LC/RC, count N1 (value-1 cells);
   split N1 into TopH (rows <= VMid) and BotH (rows > VMid) for vertical snakes;
   split into LH (cols <= HMid) and RH (cols > HMid) for horizontal snakes.
5. Detect pointer edge: PR=0 -> top; PR=H-1 -> bottom; PC=0 -> left; PC=W-1 -> right.
6. Order snakes: right -> sort by -RC; left -> sort by LC; top -> sort by TR; bottom -> sort by -BR.
7. Trace path: recursive; each snake produces two segments:
   a. Primary-direction segment to near boundary.
   b. Perpendicular segment to far boundary (direction from half-counts, clamped).
   Base case: continue in primary direction to grid edge.
8. Build output: path cells -> 3; snake cells with value 1 -> 2; others unchanged.


Wave 65 - hole_color (WP-323, Layer 298)
1. Find all non-background 4-connected components (arc2_all_comps_ with BG 0).
2. Grey components: color = 5. Legend templates: color != 5, bbox height >= 2,
   width >= 2, fill rate >= 75% (cell count * 4 >= bbox area * 3).
3. For each template comp(V, Cells): count enclosed holes with wall color V:
   a. Exterior BFS: seeds = all grid-border cells with value != V; expand
      4-adjacent through cells with value != V.
   b. Hole seeds: value-0 cells 4-adjacent to Cells, in bounds, not exterior.
   c. Hole count N = number of 4-connected components among hole seeds
      (BFS through value-0 non-exterior cells).
   Legend map entry: N -> V.
4. For each grey comp(5, Cells) on the ORIGINAL grid: count holes with wall
   color 5 (same procedure); look up target color in legend map; if the count
   is absent, target = 0 (erase).
5. Apply all recolorings: foldl arc2_set_cell_ over each component's cells.
6. Induction pre-filter: first training input contains a 5; first training
   output contains no 5; then forall training pairs verify the transform.
7. Transform guard: the transform itself first checks that the grid contains
   at least one grey (5) cell, so dispatcher enumeration fails fast on grids
   without grey cells.


Wave 66 - mosaic_heal (WP-324, Layer 299)
1. Guard: the grid contains at least one zero cell.
2. Row healing pass: for each row containing a zero, search the grid for a
   donor row such that:
   a. donor differs from the row itself;
   b. at every index where both are non-zero, the values are equal
      (any shared non-zero disagreement fails the candidate outright);
   c. at least 5 indices have equal non-zero values (confidence threshold);
   d. merging (zeros take donor values) actually changes the row.
   Replace the row by the merge; rows without a suitable donor are kept.
3. Column healing pass: transpose the grid, run the row healing pass, and
   transpose back.
4. Fixpoint: repeat row-plus-column passes until a full pass changes nothing.
5. If zeros remain: diagonal repair - merge the grid row-wise with its own
   transpose so each zero at (r, c) takes the value at (c, r); then run the
   fixpoint again.
6. Accept only if the final grid contains no zero cells.
7. Induction pre-filter: first training input contains a zero; first training
   output contains no zero; row counts of input and output match; then forall
   training pairs verify the transform.


Wave 67 - mirror_patch (WP-325, Layer 300)
1. Locate the cover: collect all color 8 cells; compute their bounding box;
   require the block to be solid (cell count equals bounding-box area).
2. Detect the horizontal mirror axis: for each candidate column sum SC from
   1 to 2*NC-3, reject SC if any visible cell disagrees with its in-grid
   mirror G[r][SC-c]; accept SC only with more than 50 supporting visible
   pairs. Detect the vertical axis SR the same way over row sums.
3. Mirror fixpoint: while some covered cell has a visible donor, fill it
   from the first visible source among:
   a. horizontal mirror (r, SC-c);
   b. vertical mirror (SR-r, c);
   c. point mirror (SR-r, SC-c).
   Healed cells become donors for later iterations of the same pass.
4. Transpose fallback: if covered cells remain (their mirrors fall outside
   the grid or inside the cover), fill each from its transpose donor
   (r, c) <- (c, r) when that cell is visible; if any cell was filled,
   run the mirror fixpoint again and repeat.
5. Extract the patch: read the healed cells inside the cover bounding box
   as the output grid; require the patch to contain no 8s.
6. Induction pre-filter: first training input has a solid 8-block whose
   bounding-box height and width equal the first output's dimensions; the
   first output contains no 8; then forall training pairs verify the
   transform.
SPARC: Specification v293, Pseudocode v285, Architecture v286, Refinement v345, Completion v351.


Wave 68 - diag_corridor (WP-326, Layer 301)
1. Background: flatten the grid; the most frequent cell value is the
   background color; every other cell is a bank cell.
2. Chains: sort bank coordinates by row then column; repeatedly take the
   topmost remaining cell and grow a chain by following the anti-diagonal
   step (r+1, c-1) while the neighbor is present in the pool.
3. Chain info: for each chain record the shared line sum s = r + c and the
   interval [dmin, dmax] of the cross coordinate d = r - c over its cells.
4. Bracketing: for every background cell and every pair of chain infos with
   s1 < s2, mark the cell when s1 < r + c < s2 and
   max(dmin1, dmin2) =< r - c =< min(dmax1, dmax2).
5. Paint: sort the marked cells to remove duplicates; rebuild the grid,
   replacing each marked cell with color 2 and keeping all other cells.
6. Induction pre-filter: equal input and output row counts; exactly two
   distinct input colors; output palette equals input palette plus color 2;
   then forall training pairs verify the transform.
SPARC: Specification v294, Pseudocode v286, Architecture v287, Refinement v346, Completion v352.


Wave 69 - frame_compass (WP-327, Layer 302)
1. Border colors: for each of the four border lines (first row, last row,
   first column, last column) keep the non-zero values and take the most
   frequent as that side's color; require at least one border line to be
   one solid non-zero color.
2. Interior component: collect all non-zero cells; partition them into
   4-connected components by flood fill over a shrinking pool; discard
   every component containing a cell on row 0, the last row, column 0, or
   the last column; keep the largest remaining component.
3. Split: crop cells are component cells whose color is not any border
   side color; frame cells are component cells whose color matches one.
4. Compass: compute the crop bounding box; require exactly two frame
   colors; for each frame color require all its cells to sit on the line
   one cell above, below, left of, or right of the bounding box (input
   edge) and require exactly one border side to own the color (output
   edge).
5. Transform: find the unique dihedral-four element mapping both input
   edges to their output edges in the 32-fact edge-permutation table;
   slice the bounding box out of the grid; apply the element by delegating
   to rotate_90_cw, rotate_90_ccw, rotate_180, reverse_rows,
   vertical_flip, transpose, or transpose plus rotate_180.
6. Induction pre-filter: first output strictly smaller than first input in
   both dimensions; a solid non-zero border line; then forall training
   pairs verify the transform.
SPARC: Specification v295, Pseudocode v287, Architecture v288, Refinement v347, Completion v353.


Wave 70 - shape_catalog (WP-328, Layer 303)
1. Background and components: take the most frequent cell value as the
   background; partition all non-background cells into 4-connected
   same-color components with the shared arc2_all_comps_ sweep.
2. Frame selection: pick the component with the most cells as the frame
   lattice and compute its bounding box.
3. Block validation and crop: require every bounding-box cell to hold the
   frame color or the background color, then slice the bounding box out of
   the grid as the block.
4. Catalogue canonicalization: for every non-frame component, shift its
   cells so the minimum corner is the origin, generate the eight
   dihedral-four variants (identity, two flips, half turn, transpose, two
   quarter turns, anti-transpose), sort each variant, and keep the
   lexicographically smallest as the canonical shape paired with the
   component color.
5. Motif extraction: run arc2_all_comps_ over the cropped block with the
   frame color playing the background role, so the background pockets
   inside the block emerge as 4-connected motif components.
6. Dominant vote: canonicalize each motif the same way, collect every
   catalogue color with an identical canonical shape, require at least one
   vote, and choose the most frequent color, smallest value on ties.
7. Paint: rebuild the block cell by cell, keeping frame-color cells and
   replacing each motif cell with its assigned color.
8. Induction pre-filter: first output fits inside the first input and is
   strictly smaller in at least one dimension; the first input carries at
   least five distinct colors; then forall training pairs verify the
   transform.
SPARC: Specification v296, Pseudocode v288, Architecture v289, Refinement v348, Completion v354.


Wave 71 - wallpaper_motif (WP-329, Layer 304)
1. Separator detection: read the color of row 0 and require the row to be
   uniform; collect all rows uniform in that color as separator rows;
   transpose the grid with arc2_transform(transpose) and repeat the same
   scan for separator columns, requiring the same color and at least two
   separators in each direction.
2. Tile bands: compute the index spans between consecutive separators,
   adding the span before the first separator and the span after the last
   separator when non-empty.
3. Tile extraction: for every row-band and column-band pair, slice the
   tile out of the grid and record it with its tile-grid coordinates.
4. Majority and minority: sort the tile patterns and require exactly two
   distinct designs with different occurrence counts; the more frequent
   design is the standard tile, the less frequent is the motif tile.
5. Motif color: choose a color present in the motif tile and absent from
   the standard tile.
6. Placement mask: collect the positions of the motif color inside the
   motif tile; the mask must be non-empty.
7. Anchor search: for each row offset and column offset that keeps the
   mask inside the tile grid, shift the mask and accept the first offset
   at which every observed motif tile position is covered.
8. Repaint: rebuild the grid cell by cell - separator rows and columns
   unchanged, motif tile at anchored mask positions, standard tile at all
   other tile positions, indexing each cell into its tile pattern by its
   offset within the band.
9. Induction pre-filter: equal first input and output dimensions, uniform
   first row, first column entirely in the separator color; then forall
   training pairs verify the transform.
SPARC: Specification v297, Pseudocode v289, Architecture v290, Refinement v349, Completion v355.


Wave 72 - band_stamp (WP-330, Layer 305)
1. Background: compute the most common cell value with arc2_bg_color_.
2. Band rows: scan the rows with their indices; a band row starts and
   ends with the same edge color E, holds a non-empty uniform interior
   color C between the edges, and satisfies E different from C; record
   each band row as its index paired with E and C.
3. Band grouping: group runs of consecutive band-row indices sharing the
   same E and C into band(E, C, Top, Bot) spans.
4. Legend cells: collect every non-background cell whose row index is
   not a band row as an R-C-V triple.
5. Components: partition the legend cells into same-color 4-connected
   components by breadth-first flooding - seed with the first unassigned
   cell, repeatedly absorb pool cells of the same color orthogonally
   adjacent to the frontier, and emit comp(Color, Cells).
6. Stamps: for each band(E, C, Top, Bot) and each component comp(C,
   Cells), find the component's maximum row MaxR, compute the downward
   shift D = Bot - MaxR, and emit a stamp cell (R + D)-Col-E for every
   component cell R-Col.
7. Render: rebuild the grid cell by cell - stamped cells take the stamp
   color, band-row cells keep their input value, and every other cell is
   erased to the background color.
8. Induction pre-filter: equal first input and output dimensions and at
   least one band row in the first input; then forall training pairs
   verify the transform.
SPARC: Specification v298, Pseudocode v290, Architecture v291, Refinement v350, Completion v356.


Wave 73 - lattice_stamp (WP-331, Layer 306)
1. Background: compute the most common cell value with arc2_bg_color_.
2. Cells: collect every non-background cell as an R-C-V triple and
   require exactly two distinct non-background colors A and B.
3. Components: partition the cells into same-color 4-connected
   components with bst_components_ breadth-first flooding.
4. Roles: try color A, then color B, as the template color T - the
   template color must form exactly two components, one with two or
   more cells (the template) and one single cell (the map center); the
   other color M supplies the marker cells, of which at least one must
   exist.
5. Template frame: compute the template bounding box - top row, bottom
   row, left column, right column - and from it the template height TH
   and width TW.
6. Stamps: for each marker at (MR, MC), compute the offset DR = MR
   minus the center row and DC = MC minus the center column; require
   both offsets even; halve them into unit counts UR and UC; emit a
   stamp cell (R + UR * TH)-(C + UC * TW)-T for every template cell
   R-C; require the total stamp count to equal markers times template
   cells, and every stamp cell to lie inside the grid.
7. Center repaint: emit a stamp cell R-C-M for every template cell R-C,
   repainting the original template in the marker color.
8. Render: rebuild the grid cell by cell on a fresh background -
   stamped cells take the stamp color and every other cell is the
   background color.
9. Induction pre-filter: equal first input and output dimensions and
   exactly two distinct non-background colors in the first input; then
   forall training pairs verify the transform.
SPARC: Specification v299, Pseudocode v291, Architecture v292, Refinement v351, Completion v357.


Wave 74 - hole_census (WP-332, Layer 307)
1. Background: compute the most common cell value with arc2_bg_color_.
2. Cells: collect every non-background cell as an R-C-V triple and
   partition the cells into same-color 4-connected components with
   bst_components_ breadth-first flooding.
3. Census annotation: for each component, compute its bounding box with
   hc_bbox4_ and its hole census - collect the background cells inside
   the bounding box, flood them into 4-connected components, and count
   the components.
4. Split: the maximum bounding-box area over all components identifies
   the tiles; every component at that area is a tile and every other
   component is a shape; require equal tile and shape counts, one shared
   tile size, one shared strictly smaller shape size.
5. Pairing: for each tile with census K, collect the shapes with census
   K and require exactly one; require the resulting pairing to use every
   shape exactly once (sorted used-shape list has full length).
6. Layout: the output origin is the smallest tile top row and left
   column; the output height and width span to the lowest and rightmost
   tile edges; the shape offset inside a tile is half the size gap in
   each dimension.
7. Render: for each output cell, find the pairing entry whose tile
   covers the cell; inside the centered shape window sample the shape's
   source cell from the input - shape color stays, anything else takes
   the tile color; outside the window the cell takes the solid tile
   color; outside every tile the cell is background.
8. Induction pre-filter: the first output must have strictly fewer rows
   and strictly fewer columns than the first input; then forall training
   pairs verify the transform.
SPARC: Specification v300, Pseudocode v292, Architecture v293, Refinement v352, Completion v358.


Wave 75 - glyph_swap (WP-333, Layer 308)
1. Background: compute the most common cell value with arc2_bg_color_
   and require it to differ from the frame color 5.
2. Frame: collect every color-5 cell, take the bounding box with
   hc_bbox4_, and verify all four edges of the box are solid color 5.
3. Legends: for every anchor whose 3x4 window lies fully outside the
   frame box, match the interlock AABB / AAAB / AABB with two colors A
   and B both different from the background and from 5; collect the
   pairs A-B, sort them, require unique source colors, and record all
   covered legend cells.
4. Blocks: collect the colored cells of the frame interior, partition
   them into same-color 4-connected components with bst_components_,
   fix B as the first component's bounding-box height, and require
   every component to be a solid B-by-B square.
5. Glyphs: for each distinct block color, collect its cells outside the
   frame box that are not legend cells, require the bounding box to be
   exactly B-by-B, and convert the cells to in-box offsets as the mask.
6. Replacements: for every block cell, output the legend-mapped color
   if its offset is in the glyph mask and the background otherwise.
7. Render: emit the rows and columns of the frame bounding box;
   replaced cells take their new value and all other cells copy the
   input.
8. Induction pre-filter: the first output must have strictly fewer rows
   and strictly fewer columns than the first input and carry frame
   color 5 in its top-left and bottom-left cells; then forall training
   pairs verify the transform.
SPARC: Specification v301, Pseudocode v293, Architecture v294, Refinement v353, Completion v359.


Wave 76 - puzzle_fit (WP-334, Layer 309)
1. Background: compute the most common cell value with arc2_bg_color_.
2. Pieces: collect every non-background cell as row-column-color and
   flood the cells into 8-connected components over mixed colors, so
   diagonal contacts and the color-5 anchor stud stay in one piece.
3. Normalize: shift each piece to its bounding-box origin and sort its
   cells into scanline order; sum the cell counts and require the
   total to be a perfect square N * N, fixing the output side N.
4. Variants: for each piece emit identity and the three quarter-turn
   rotations of its cell set, then deduplicate by sorting; do not
   emit reflections.
5. Search: keep the empty board cells as a sorted scanline list; at
   each step select an unplaced piece and a rotation variant, anchor
   the variant's scanline-first cell on the scanline-first empty cell,
   require every shifted cell to lie inside the board and on empty
   positions, subtract the covered positions, and recurse until the
   board is full and all pieces are used.
6. Anchor: accept the first solution whose placed cells contain the
   color-5 stud at row 0, column 0 - under rotations only this
   solution is unique.
7. Render: paint the placed cells row by row into the N-by-N output
   square, each cell keeping its input color.
8. Induction pre-filter: the first output must have strictly fewer
   rows and strictly fewer columns than the first input, be exactly
   square, carry color 5 in its top-left cell, and not carry color 5
   in its bottom-left cell; then forall training pairs verify the
   transform.
SPARC: Specification v302, Pseudocode v294, Architecture v295, Refinement v354, Completion v360.


Wave 77 - palette_jigsaw (WP-335, Layer 310)
1. Background: compute the most common cell value with arc2_bg_color_.
2. Pieces: collect every non-background cell as row-column-color and
   flood the cells into 8-connected components over mixed colors;
   require exactly four components.
3. Key: partition the components by distinct-color count; exactly one
   component - the key - carries more than one color; its body color
   is its most frequent cell color, and the four cells differing from
   the body form a 2-by-2 palette block read as top-left, top-right,
   bottom-left, bottom-right.
4. Masks: shift each piece to its bounding-box origin and replace its
   cell colors with a piece index tag, the key being index 1 with its
   palette cells counted as shape cells; sum the mask cell counts and
   require the total to be a perfect square N * N, fixing the output
   side N.
5. Search: run the exact-cover engine over the N-by-N board with the
   four quarter-turn rotation variants of each mask - the
